namespace ZenLib
{
    public class ZenTicket
    {
        private const string LogSource = "ZenTicket";

        ZendeskClient _client;
        string _server;

        
        public int DefaultsAdded { get; private set; }
        public int DefaultsUpdated { get; private set; }
        public int SettlementsAdded { get; private set; }
        public int SettlementsUpdated { get; private set; }

        public ZenTicket(ZendeskClient client, string server)
        {
            _client = client;
            _server = server;
            ResetCounters();
        }

        public void ResetCounters()
        {
            DefaultsAdded = 0;
            DefaultsUpdated = 0;
            SettlementsAdded = 0;
            SettlementsUpdated = 0;
        }

        public async Task<TicketResponse> SyncTicket(long ticket_id)
        {
            ZenLogger.Info(LogSource, "Checking Default on Ticket: {0}", ticket_id);
            var ticket = await _client.Tickets.GetAsync(ticket_id);
            bool has_default = HasDefaultDate(ticket_id, ticket.Ticket);
            if (has_default)
            {
                ZenLogger.Info(LogSource, "Syncing Ticket: {0}", ticket_id);
                CreateOrUpdateDefaultEvent(ticket.Ticket);
            }

            return ticket;
        }


        public bool TicketExists(long ticket_id)
        {
            string sql = "select id from ZenTickets where id = @ticket_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@ticket_id", ticket_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count > 0;
        }


        public void ClearAllTicketData(long zenticket_id)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.ClearAllZenDesk @zenticket_id=@zenticket_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@zenticket_id", zenticket_id);
            q.Execute();
        }
        public void ClearTicket(long ticket_id)
        {
            ClearTags(ticket_id);
            string sql = "delete from ZenTickets where id = @ticket_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@ticket_id", ticket_id);
            q.Execute();
        }
        public void ClearTicketDefaults(long ticket_id)
        {
            string sql = "delete from Defaults where zenticket_id = @ticket_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@ticket_id", ticket_id);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public bool DefaultExistsForTicket(long zenticket_id)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM Defaults WHERE zenticket_id = @zenticket_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@zenticket_id", zenticket_id);
            var result = q.ExecuteSingle<int>();
            return result > 0;
        }

        public void UpdateDefaultCureDate(Ticket t)
        {
            
            string cure_date_str = "";
            foreach (var f in t.CustomFields)
            {
                if (f.Id == ZendeskFieldIds.CustomFields.CureDate)
                {
                    cure_date_str = f.Value;
                    break;
                }
            }

            
            DateTime? newCureDate = null;
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(cure_date_str))
            {
                if (DateTime.TryParse(cure_date_str, out DateTime parsed))
                {
                    newCureDate = parsed;
                }
            }

            
            DateTime? existingCureDate = GetExistingCureDate(t.Id);

            
            if (!newCureDate.HasValue && !existingCureDate.HasValue)
            {
                ZenLogger.Debug(LogSource, "Zenticket {0}: Cure date is empty in both Zendesk and database. No update needed.", t.Id);
                return;
            }

            
            if (newCureDate.HasValue && existingCureDate.HasValue && newCureDate.Value.Date == existingCureDate.Value.Date)
            {
                ZenLogger.Debug(LogSource, "Zenticket {0}: Cure date unchanged ({1}). No update needed.", t.Id, newCureDate.Value.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd"));
                return;
            }

            
            string sql = "UPDATE Defaults SET cure_date = @cure_date, update_time = @update_time WHERE zenticket_id = @zenticket_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);

            if (newCureDate.HasValue)
            {
                q.AddParameter("@cure_date", newCureDate.Value);
            }
            else
            {
                q.AddParameter("@cure_date", DBNull.Value);
            }

            q.AddParameter("@update_time", t.UpdatedAt);
            q.AddParameter("@zenticket_id", t.Id);
            q.Execute();

            DefaultsUpdated++;
            ZenLogger.Info(LogSource, "Default cure_date updated for Zenticket Id {0}. (old: {1}, new: {2}, updated_at: {3})", 
                t.Id, 
                existingCureDate.HasValue ? existingCureDate.Value.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd") : "null",
                newCureDate.HasValue ? newCureDate.Value.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd") : "null",
                t.UpdatedAt);
        }
        private DateTime? GetExistingCureDate(long zenticket_id)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT cure_date FROM Defaults WHERE zenticket_id = @zenticket_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@zenticket_id", zenticket_id);
            DataTable dt = q.ExecuteTable();

            if (dt == null || dt.Rows.Count == 0)
                return null;

            object val = dt.Rows[0]["cure_date"];
            if (val == null || val == DBNull.Value)
                return null;

            return Convert.ToDateTime(val);
        }

        public void CreateOrUpdateDefaultEvent(Ticket t)
        {
            if (DefaultExistsForTicket(t.Id))
            {
                UpdateDefaultCureDate(t);
            }
            else
            {
                CreateDefaultEvent(t);
            }
        }

        public void InsertTicket(Ticket t)
        {
            string sql = "INSERT INTO ZenTickets (id, assignee_id, created_at, description, due, external_id, form_id, forumtopic_id, group_id, has_incidents, is_public, priority, problem_id, subject_raw, recipient, requester_id, satisfaction_rating, status, subject, submitter_id, type, updated_at, via, asset_id) VALUES (@id, @assignee_id, @created_at, @description, @due, @external_id, @form_id, @forumtopic_id, @group_id, @has_incidents, @is_public, @priority, @problem_id, @subject_raw, @recipient, @requester_id, @satisfaction_rating, @status, @subject, @submitter_id, @type, @updated_at, @via, @asset_id)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@id", t.Id);
            q.AddParameter("@assignee_id", t.AssigneeId);
            q.AddParameter("@created_at", t.CreatedAt);
            q.AddParameter("@description", t.Description);
            q.AddParameter("@due", t.Due);
            q.AddParameter("@external_id", t.ExternalId);
            q.AddParameter("@form_id", t.FormId);
            q.AddParameter("@forumtopic_id", t.ForumTopicId);
            q.AddParameter("@group_id", t.GroupId);
            q.AddParameter("@has_incidents", t.HasIncidents);
            q.AddParameter("@is_public", t.IsPublic);
            q.AddParameter("@priority", t.Priority);
            q.AddParameter("@problem_id", t.ProblemId);
            q.AddParameter("@subject_raw", t.RawSubject);
            q.AddParameter("@recipient", t.Recipient);
            q.AddParameter("@requester_id", t.RequesterId);
            q.AddParameter("@satisfaction_rating", t.SatisfactionRating != null ? t.SatisfactionRating.ToString() : (object)DBNull.Value);
            q.AddParameter("@status", t.Status);
            q.AddParameter("@subject", t.Subject);
            q.AddParameter("@submitter_id", t.SubmitterId);
            q.AddParameter("@type", t.Type);
            q.AddParameter("@updated_at", t.UpdatedAt);
            q.AddParameter("@via", t.Via.Channel);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", null);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public String GetFormValue(IReadOnlyCustomFields customFields, long compareFieldVal)
        {
            foreach (var f in customFields)
            {
                if (f.Id == compareFieldVal)
                {
                    return f.Value;
                }
            }
            return null;
        }

        
        private static readonly Dictionary<string, int> DelinquencySubtypeMap = new Dictionary<string, int>
        {
            { "senior_mortgage_fcl", 5 },
            { "junior_mortgage_fcl", 6 },
            { "hoa_fcl", 7 },
            { "property_tax_fcl", 8 },
            { "federal_tax_fcl", 9 },
            { "state_tax_fcl", 10 },
            { "mortgage_dlq", 32 },
            { "property_tax_dlq", 33 },
            { "hoa_dlq", 34 },
            { "other_fcl", 35 }
        };

        private static readonly Dictionary<string, int> MisrepresentationSubtypeMap = new Dictionary<string, int>
        {
            { "loan_stacking", 2 },
            { "thfl_breach", 3 },
            { "fraud", 4 }
        };

        private static readonly Dictionary<string, int> UnauthorizedTransferSubtypeMap = new Dictionary<string, int>
        {
            { "3rd_party_transfer", 12 },
            { "transfer_to_llc", 13 }
        };

        private static readonly Dictionary<string, int> UnapprovedLiensSubtypeMap = new Dictionary<string, int>
        {
            { "undisclosed_senior_lien", 14 },
            { "state_tax_lien", 15 },
            { "federal_tax_lien", 16 },
            { "hoa_lien", 17 },
            { "priority_lien", 18 }
        };

        private static readonly Dictionary<string, int> FinancialDifficultySubtypeMap = new Dictionary<string, int>
        {
            { "ch_7_bankruptcy", 19 },
            { "ch_11_bankruptcy", 20 },
            { "ch_12_bankruptcy", 21 },
            { "ch_13_bankruptcy", 22 }
        };

        private static readonly Dictionary<string, int> InsuranceLapseSubtypeMap = new Dictionary<string, int>
        {
            { "hoi_policy_lapse", 23 },
            { "flood_policy_lapse", 24 }
        };

        private static readonly Dictionary<string, int> SimpleServicingTypeMap = new Dictionary<string, int>
        {
            { "failure_to_perform", 1 },
            { "occupancy", 11 },
            { "", 25 },
            { "condition_of_property", 26 },
            { "rental_terms", 27 },
            { "cooperation", 28 },
            { "other_adverse_acts", 29 }
        };

        public int GetDefaultTypeId(Ticket t)
        {
            if (t.FormId != ZendeskFieldIds.FormIds.SpecialServicing)
            {
                return -1;
            }

            string servicingType = GetFormValue(t.CustomFields, ZendeskFieldIds.CustomFields.SpecialServicingType) ?? "";

            
            if (SimpleServicingTypeMap.TryGetValue(servicingType, out int simpleTypeId))
            {
                return simpleTypeId;
            }

            
            switch (servicingType)
            {
                case "misrepresetation":
                    string misrepSubtype = GetFormValue(t.CustomFields, ZendeskFieldIds.CustomFields.MisrepresentationSubtype);
                    if (misrepSubtype != null && MisrepresentationSubtypeMap.TryGetValue(misrepSubtype, out int misrepTypeId))
                    {
                        return misrepTypeId;
                    }
                    break;

                case "delinquency":
                    string delinqSubtype = GetFormValue(t.CustomFields, ZendeskFieldIds.CustomFields.DelinquencySubtype);
                    if (delinqSubtype != null && DelinquencySubtypeMap.TryGetValue(delinqSubtype, out int delinqTypeId))
                    {
                        return delinqTypeId;
                    }
                    break;

                case "unauthorized_transfer":
                    string transferSubtype = GetFormValue(t.CustomFields, ZendeskFieldIds.CustomFields.UnauthorizedTransferSubtype);
                    if (transferSubtype != null && UnauthorizedTransferSubtypeMap.TryGetValue(transferSubtype, out int transferTypeId))
                    {
                        return transferTypeId;
                    }
                    break;

                case "unapproved_liens":
                    string liensSubtype = GetFormValue(t.CustomFields, ZendeskFieldIds.CustomFields.UnapprovedLiensSubtype);
                    if (liensSubtype != null && UnapprovedLiensSubtypeMap.TryGetValue(liensSubtype, out int liensTypeId))
                    {
                        return liensTypeId;
                    }
                    break;

                case "financial_difficulty":
                    string financialSubtype = GetFormValue(t.CustomFields, ZendeskFieldIds.CustomFields.FinancialDifficultySubtype);
                    if (financialSubtype != null && FinancialDifficultySubtypeMap.TryGetValue(financialSubtype, out int financialTypeId))
                    {
                        return financialTypeId;
                    }
                    break;

                case "insurance_lapse":
                    string insuranceSubtype = GetFormValue(t.CustomFields, ZendeskFieldIds.CustomFields.InsuranceLapseSubtype);
                    if (insuranceSubtype != null && InsuranceLapseSubtypeMap.TryGetValue(insuranceSubtype, out int insuranceTypeId))
                    {
                        return insuranceTypeId;
                    }
                    break;
            }

            return -1;
        }

        public void CreateDefaultEvent(Ticket t)
        {
            string sql = "INSERT INTO Defaults (defaulttype_id, asset_id, default_date, cure_date, update_time, update_by, zenticket_id, headline, description)  VALUES (@defaulttype_id, @asset_id, @default_date, @cure_date, @update_time, @update_by, @zenticket_id, @headline, @description)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);

            string asset_id = "";
            string default_date_str = "";
            string cure_date_str = "";
            foreach (var f in t.CustomFields)
            {
                if (f.Id == ZendeskFieldIds.CustomFields.AssetId)
                {
                    asset_id = f.Value;
                }
                else if (f.Id == ZendeskFieldIds.CustomFields.DefaultDate)
                {
                    default_date_str = f.Value;
                }
                else if (f.Id == ZendeskFieldIds.CustomFields.CureDate)
                {
                    cure_date_str = f.Value;
                }
            }

            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);

            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(default_date_str))
            {
                q.AddParameter("@default_date", DateTime.Parse(default_date_str));
            }
            else
            {
                q.AddParameter("@default_date", DBNull.Value);
            }

            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(cure_date_str))
            {
                q.AddParameter("@cure_date", DateTime.Parse(cure_date_str));
            }
            else
            {
                q.AddParameter("@cure_date", DBNull.Value);
            }

            q.AddParameter("@update_time", t.UpdatedAt);
            q.AddParameter("@update_by", "zensync");
            q.AddParameter("@zenticket_id", t.Id);
            q.AddParameter("@headline", t.Subject);
            q.AddParameter("@description", t.Description);

            int default_type_id = GetDefaultTypeId(t);
            q.AddParameter("@defaulttype_id", default_type_id);

            q.ExecuteTable();

            if (default_type_id == -1)
            {
                ZenLogger.Warning(LogSource, "Zenticket {0} needs to push an update to defaults table but is unable to map Zenticket ID. (default_date: {1}, cure_date: {2}, updated_at: {3})", t.Id, default_date_str, cure_date_str, t.UpdatedAt);
            }
            else
            {
                DefaultsAdded++;
                ZenLogger.Info(LogSource, "Default of Default type {0} was created for Zenticket Id {1}. (default_date: {2}, cure_date: {3}, updated_at: {4})", default_type_id, t.Id, default_date_str, cure_date_str, t.UpdatedAt);
            }
        }

        public void InsertTags(long zenticket_id, IEnumerable<string> tags)
        {
            ClearTags(zenticket_id);
            foreach (string s in tags)
                InsertTag(zenticket_id, s);
        }
        public bool HasDefaultDate(long zenticket_id, Ticket t)
        {
            foreach (var f in t.CustomFields)
                if (f.Id == ZendeskFieldIds.CustomFields.DefaultDate && f.Value != null && f.Value.Replace(" ", "") != "")
                {
                    return true;
                }
            return false;
        }
        public async Task<bool> testHasDefaultDate(long ztid)
        {
            var ticket = await _client.Tickets.GetAsync(ztid);
            return HasDefaultDate(ztid, ticket.Ticket);
        }
        public void InsertCustomFields(long zenticket_id, Ticket t)
        {
            ClearCustomFields(zenticket_id);
            foreach (var f in t.CustomFields)
                InsertCustomField(zenticket_id, f.Id, f.Value);
        }

            q.Execute();
        }

        private static readonly HashSet<long> SettlementFormIds = new HashSet<long>
        {
            ZendeskFieldIds.FormIds.OwnerBuyout,
            ZendeskFieldIds.FormIds.HomeSale
        };

        private static readonly HashSet<string> ValidSettlementTypes = new HashSet<string>
        {
            "home_sale",
            "owner_buyout",
            "unlock_refi"
        };

        public string GetSettlementType(Ticket t)
        {
            if (!t.FormId.HasValue || !SettlementFormIds.Contains(t.FormId.Value))
                return null;

            string ticketType = GetFormValue(t.CustomFields, ZendeskFieldIds.CustomFields.SpecialServicingType);
            if (ticketType != null && ValidSettlementTypes.Contains(ticketType))
                return ticketType;

            return null;
        }

        public bool SettlementRequestExistsForTicket(long zenticket_id)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ZenSettlementRequests WHERE zenticket_id = @zenticket_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@zenticket_id", zenticket_id);
            var result = q.ExecuteSingle<int>();
            return result > 0;
        }

        public void CreateSettlementRequest(Ticket t)
        {
            string settlementType = GetSettlementType(t);
            if (settlementType == null)
                return;

            string asset_id = "";
            string avm_value = "";
            foreach (var f in t.CustomFields)
            {
                if (f.Id == ZendeskFieldIds.CustomFields.AssetId)
                    asset_id = f.Value;
                else if (f.Id == ZendeskFieldIds.CustomFields.AVMValue)
                    avm_value = f.Value;
            }

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(asset_id))
            {
                ZenLogger.Warning(LogSource, "Skipping settlement request for Zenticket {0} - asset_id is required but missing.", t.Id);
                return;
            }
            else if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(avm_value))
            {
                ZenLogger.Warning(LogSource, "Skipping settlement request for Zenticket {0} with empty AVM value - please verify if this is correct. (asset_id: {1})", t.Id, asset_id);
                return;
            }

            string sql = "INSERT INTO ZenSettlementRequests (asset_id, ticket_type, avm_value, created_at, update_time, zenticket_id, subject) VALUES (@asset_id, @ticket_type, @avm_value, @created_at, @update_time, @zenticket_id, @subject)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@ticket_type", settlementType);
            q.AddParameter("@avm_value", avm_value);
            q.AddParameter("@created_at", t.CreatedAt);
            q.AddParameter("@update_time", t.UpdatedAt);
            q.AddParameter("@zenticket_id", t.Id);
            q.AddParameter("@subject", t.Subject);
            q.Execute();

            SettlementsAdded++;
            ZenLogger.Info(LogSource, "Settlement request ({0}) created for Zenticket {1}. (asset_id: {2}, avm: {3})", settlementType, t.Id, asset_id, avm_value);
        }

        public void UpdateSettlementRequest(Ticket t)
        {
            string settlementType = GetSettlementType(t);

            string asset_id = "";
            string avm_value = "";
            foreach (var f in t.CustomFields)
            {
                if (f.Id == ZendeskFieldIds.CustomFields.AssetId)
                    asset_id = f.Value;
                else if (f.Id == ZendeskFieldIds.CustomFields.AVMValue)
                    avm_value = f.Value;
            }

            string sql = "UPDATE ZenSettlementRequests SET asset_id = @asset_id, ticket_type = @ticket_type, avm_value = @avm_value, update_time = @update_time, subject = @subject WHERE zenticket_id = @zenticket_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@ticket_type", settlementType);
            q.AddParameter("@avm_value", string.IsNullOrEmpty(avm_value) ? (object)DBNull.Value : avm_value);
            q.AddParameter("@update_time", t.UpdatedAt);
            q.AddParameter("@subject", t.Subject);
            q.AddParameter("@zenticket_id", t.Id);
            q.Execute();

            SettlementsUpdated++;
            ZenLogger.Info(LogSource, "Settlement request updated for Zenticket {0}. (asset_id: {1}, type: {2}, avm: {3}, updated_at: {4})", t.Id, asset_id, settlementType, avm_value, t.UpdatedAt);
        }

        public void CreateOrUpdateSettlementRequest(Ticket t)
        {
            if (SettlementRequestExistsForTicket(t.Id))
                UpdateSettlementRequest(t);
            else
                CreateSettlementRequest(t);
        }

        public async Task<TicketResponse> SyncSettlementTicket(long ticket_id)
        {
            var ticket = await _client.Tickets.GetAsync(ticket_id);
            string settlementType = GetSettlementType(ticket.Ticket);
            if (settlementType != null)
            {
                ZenLogger.Info(LogSource, "Processing settlement request ({0}) for Ticket: {1}", settlementType, ticket_id);
                CreateOrUpdateSettlementRequest(ticket.Ticket);
            }
            return ticket;
        }
    }
}

namespace ZenLib
{
    public class ZenUser
    {

        ZendeskClient _client;
        string _server;
        public ZenUser(ZendeskClient client, string server)
        {
            _client = client;
            _server = server;
        }

        public bool UserExists(long user_id)
        {
            string sql = "select id from ZenUsers where id = @user_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@user_id", user_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count > 0;
        }

        public void ClearUser(long user_id)
        {
            string sql = "delete from ZenUsers where id = @user_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@user_id", user_id);
            q.Execute();
        }
        public void InsertUser(UserResponse u)
        {

            string asset_id = u.UserFields.Where(n => n.Key.Contains("asset_id")).First().Value?.ToString();
            string sql = "INSERT INTO ZenUsers (id,active, created_at, email, external_id, last_login, locale_id, moderator, [name], notes, only_private_comments, phone, restricted_agent, [role], shared, shared_agent, [signature], suspended, ticket_restriction, timezone, updated_at,asset_id) VALUES (@id,@active, @created_at, @email, @external_id, @last_login, @locale_id, @moderator, @name, @notes, @only_private_comments, @phone, @restricted_agent, @role, @shared, @shared_agent, @signature, @suspended, @ticket_restriction, @timezone, @updated_at,@asset_id)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@id", u.Id);
            q.AddParameter("@active", u.Active);
            q.AddParameter("@created_at", u.CreatedAt);
            q.AddParameter("@email", u.Email);
            q.AddParameter("@external_id", u.ExternalId);
            q.AddParameter("@last_login", u.LastLoginAt);
            q.AddParameter("@locale_id", u.LocaleId);
            q.AddParameter("@moderator", u.Moderator);
            q.AddParameter("@name", u.Name);
            q.AddParameter("@notes", u.Notes);
            q.AddParameter("@only_private_comments", u.OnlyPrivateComments);
            q.AddParameter("@phone", u.Phone);
            q.AddParameter("@restricted_agent", u.RestrictedAgent);
            q.AddParameter("@role", u.Role);
            q.AddParameter("@shared", u.Shared);
            q.AddParameter("@shared_agent", u.SharedAgent);
            q.AddParameter("@signature", u.Signature);
            q.AddParameter("@suspended", u.Suspended); ;
            q.AddParameter("@ticket_restriction", u.TicketRestriction);
            q.AddParameter("@timezone", u.TimeZone);
            q.AddParameter("@updated_at", u.UpdatedAt);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.Execute();
        }

       
    }
}


--- FILE: ZenLib\ZenClient.cs ---
namespace ZenLib
{
    public class ZenClient
    {
        private const string LogSource = "ZenClient";
        private const string DefaultNotificationRecipients = "brandan.carlson@unlock.com;ryan.thrift@unlock.com;jagat.shah@unlock.com;nick.carnot@unlock.com";
        private readonly string _notificationRecipients;

        private readonly string _token;
        private readonly string _url;
        private readonly string _email;

        public ZendeskClient _client;
        public ZenTicket _zt;
        public ZenUser _zu;
        public string _server;
        private Dictionary<long, DateTime> _defaultsCache;
        private Dictionary<long, DateTime> _settlementsCache;

        public ZenClient(string server, string email, string token, string url, string notificationRecipients = null)
        {
            _server = server;
            _email = email;
            _token = token;
            _url = url;
            _notificationRecipients = notificationRecipients ?? DefaultNotificationRecipients;

            var zendeskOptions = new ZendeskOptions
            {
                EndpointUri = _url,
                Username = _email,
                Token = _token
            };

            var loggerFactory = new LoggerFactory();
            var zendeskOptionsWrapper = new OptionsWrapper<ZendeskOptions>(zendeskOptions);
            _client = new ZendeskClient(new ZendeskApiClient(zendeskOptionsWrapper), loggerFactory.CreateLogger<ZendeskClient>());

            _zt = new ZenTicket(_client, _server);
            _zu = new ZenUser(_client, _server);

            LoadDefaultsCache();
            LoadSettlementsCache();
        }

        private void LoadDefaultsCache()
        {
            _defaultsCache = new Dictionary<long, DateTime>();
            string sql = "select zenticket_id, update_time from Defaults WHERE zenticket_id IS NOT NULL";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            var table = q.ExecuteTable();
            foreach (System.Data.DataRow row in table.Rows)
            {
                long zenticket_id = Convert.ToInt64(row["zenticket_id"]);
                DateTime update_time = Convert.ToDateTime(row["update_time"]);
                _defaultsCache[zenticket_id] = update_time;
            }
            ZenLogger.Info(LogSource, "Loaded {0} entries into defaults cache", _defaultsCache.Count);
        }

        private void LoadSettlementsCache()
        {
            _settlementsCache = new Dictionary<long, DateTime>();
            try
            {
                string sql = "SELECT zenticket_id, update_time FROM ZenSettlementRequests WHERE zenticket_id IS NOT NULL";
                Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
                var table = q.ExecuteTable();
                if (table != null)
                {
                    foreach (System.Data.DataRow row in table.Rows)
                    {
                        long zenticket_id = Convert.ToInt64(row["zenticket_id"]);
                        DateTime update_time = Convert.ToDateTime(row["update_time"]);
                        _settlementsCache[zenticket_id] = update_time;
                    }
                }
                ZenLogger.Info(LogSource, "Loaded {0} entries into settlements cache", _settlementsCache.Count);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                ZenLogger.Warning(LogSource, "Could not load settlements cache: {0}", ex.Message);
            }
        }

        public bool SettlementTicketNeedsUpdate(long ticket_id, DateTime updated_at)
        {
            DateTime cachedUpdateTime;
            if (_settlementsCache != null && _settlementsCache.TryGetValue(ticket_id, out cachedUpdateTime))
            {
                return Math.Abs((cachedUpdateTime - updated_at).TotalMinutes) > 30 && updated_at > cachedUpdateTime;
            }
            return true;
        }

        public async Task SyncTicket(long ticketId)
        {
            await _zt.SyncTicket(ticketId);
        }

        public async Task SyncAllTickets(string updatedAfter, bool clearUserIfExists)
        {
            ZenLogger.Info(LogSource, "Starting ticket sync - REFRESHING TICKET SYNC");

            
            DateTime updatedAfterDate;
            if (!DateTime.TryParse(updatedAfter, out updatedAfterDate))
            {
                updatedAfterDate = DateTime.UtcNow.AddDays(-30); 
                ZenLogger.Warning(LogSource, "Invalid date supplied; defaulting to 30 days prior.");
            }

            
            _zt.ResetCounters();

            CursorPager cp = new CursorPager();
            cp.Size = 100;

            var response = await _client.Tickets.GetAllAsync(cp);
            var meta = response.Meta;
            long prev_ticket_id = -1;

            int pageGuard = 0;
            const int maxPages = 1000;
            int ticketsProcessed = 0;
            bool syncAborted = false;

            while (pageGuard++ < maxPages)
            {
                foreach (Ticket ticket in response)
                {
                    if (ticket.UpdatedAt > updatedAfterDate)
                    {
                        await ProcessTicketWithRetryAsync(ticket, prev_ticket_id);
                        prev_ticket_id = ticket.Id;
                        ticketsProcessed++;
                    }
                }

                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(meta.AfterCursor))
                {
                    break;
                }

                cp.AfterCursor = meta.AfterCursor;
                ZenLogger.Debug(LogSource, "Fetching next page with cursor: {0}", meta.AfterCursor);

                
                response = await ExecuteWithRetryAsync<ICursorPagination<Ticket>>(
                    async () => await _client.Tickets.GetAllAsync(cp),
                    3,
                    "Failed to get new page of tickets"
                );

                if (response == null)
                {
                    ZenLogger.Error(LogSource, "Aborting ticket sync due to repeated page failures.");
                    syncAborted = true;
                    break;
                }

                meta = response.Meta;
            }

            
            int recordsAdded = _zt.DefaultsAdded;
            int recordsUpdated = _zt.DefaultsUpdated;

            ZenLogger.Info(LogSource, "Sync complete. Processed {0} tickets. Defaults Added: {1}, Defaults Updated: {2}", ticketsProcessed, recordsAdded, recordsUpdated);

            
            SendSyncCompletionEmail(ticketsProcessed, recordsAdded, recordsUpdated, syncAborted);
        }

        private void SendSyncCompletionEmail(int ticketsProcessed, int recordsAdded, int recordsUpdated, bool syncAborted)
        {
            try
            {
                string subject = syncAborted 
                    ? "[ZenSync] Ticket Sync ABORTED - " + DateTime.Now.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm")
                    : "[ZenSync] Ticket Sync Complete - " + DateTime.Now.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm");

                string body = string.Format(
@"ZenSync Ticket Synchronization Report

=====================================

Sync Status: {0}
Completed At: {1}

Summary:
--------
Tickets Processed: {2}
Default Records Added: {3}
Default Records Updated: {4}

---
This is an automated notification from ZenSync.",
                    syncAborted ? "ABORTED" : "SUCCESS",
                    DateTime.Now.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"),
                    ticketsProcessed,
                    recordsAdded,
                    recordsUpdated);

                Mail mail = new Mail("uam_sendgrid");
                mail.SendSMTPMail(
                    _notificationRecipients,
                    null,
                    null,
                    subject,
                    body,
                    null,
                    false,
                    true,
                    "zensync@unlock.com");

                ZenLogger.Info(LogSource, "Sync completion email sent to {0}", _notificationRecipients);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                ZenLogger.Error(LogSource, "Failed to send sync completion email: {0}", ex.Message);
            }
        }

        public async Task SyncSettlementRequests(string updatedAfter, HashSet<long> skippedTicketIds = null)
        {
            ZenLogger.Info(LogSource, "Starting settlement request sync");

            DateTime updatedAfterDate;
            if (!DateTime.TryParse(updatedAfter, out updatedAfterDate))
            {
                updatedAfterDate = DateTime.UtcNow.AddDays(-30);
                ZenLogger.Warning(LogSource, "Invalid date supplied; defaulting to 30 days prior.");
            }

            _zt.ResetCounters();

            CursorPager cp = new CursorPager();
            cp.Size = 100;

            var response = await _client.Tickets.GetAllAsync(cp);
            var meta = response.Meta;

            int pageGuard = 0;
            const int maxPages = 1000;
            int ticketsProcessed = 0;
            int settlementTicketsFound = 0;
            bool syncAborted = false;

            while (pageGuard++ < maxPages)
            {
                foreach (Ticket ticket in response)
                {
                    if (skippedTicketIds != null && skippedTicketIds.Contains(ticket.Id))
                    {
                        ZenLogger.Debug(LogSource, "Skipping ticket {0} (in skip list)", ticket.Id);
                        continue;
                    }

                    if (ticket.UpdatedAt > updatedAfterDate)
                    {
                        ticketsProcessed++;

                        
                        if (ticket.FormId == ZendeskFieldIds.FormIds.OwnerBuyout ||
                            ticket.FormId == ZendeskFieldIds.FormIds.HomeSale)
                        {
                            bool needsUpdate = SettlementTicketNeedsUpdate(ticket.Id, ticket.UpdatedAt);
                            if (needsUpdate)
                            {
                                await ExecuteWithRetryAsync<object>(
                                    async () =>
                                    {
                                        await _zt.SyncSettlementTicket(ticket.Id);
                                        _settlementsCache[ticket.Id] = ticket.UpdatedAt;
                                        return null;
                                    },
                                    3,
                                    "Failed to sync settlement ticket: " + ticket.Id);
                                settlementTicketsFound++;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }

                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(meta.AfterCursor))
                    break;

                cp.AfterCursor = meta.AfterCursor;
                ZenLogger.Debug(LogSource, "Fetching next page with cursor: {0}", meta.AfterCursor);

                response = await ExecuteWithRetryAsync<ICursorPagination<Ticket>>(
                    async () => await _client.Tickets.GetAllAsync(cp),
                    3,
                    "Failed to get new page of tickets (settlement sync)");

                if (response == null)
                {
                    ZenLogger.Error(LogSource, "Aborting settlement sync due to repeated page failures.");
                    syncAborted = true;
                    break;
                }

                meta = response.Meta;
            }

            int settlementsAdded = _zt.SettlementsAdded;
            int settlementsUpdated = _zt.SettlementsUpdated;

            ZenLogger.Info(LogSource, "Settlement sync complete. Scanned {0} tickets, found {1} settlement tickets. Added: {2}, Updated: {3}",
                ticketsProcessed, settlementTicketsFound, settlementsAdded, settlementsUpdated);

            if (settlementsAdded > 0 || settlementsUpdated > 0)
                SendSettlementSyncEmail(ticketsProcessed, settlementTicketsFound, settlementsAdded, settlementsUpdated, syncAborted);
            else
                ZenLogger.Info(LogSource, "No settlement changes - skipping email notification.");
        }

        private void SendSettlementSyncEmail(int ticketsScanned, int settlementTicketsFound, int settlementsAdded, int settlementsUpdated, bool syncAborted)
        {
            try
            {
                string subject = syncAborted
                    ? "[ZenSync] Settlement Sync ABORTED - " + DateTime.Now.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm")
                    : "[ZenSync] Settlement Sync Complete - " + DateTime.Now.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm");

                string body = string.Format(
@"ZenSync Settlement Request Synchronization Report

===================================================

Sync Status: {0}
Completed At: {1}

Summary:
--------
Tickets Scanned: {2}
Settlement Tickets Found: {3}
Settlement Records Added: {4}
Settlement Records Updated: {5}

---
This is an automated notification from ZenSync.",
                    syncAborted ? "ABORTED" : "SUCCESS",
                    DateTime.Now.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"),
                    ticketsScanned,
                    settlementTicketsFound,
                    settlementsAdded,
                    settlementsUpdated);

                Mail mail = new Mail("uam_sendgrid");
                mail.SendSMTPMail(
                    _notificationRecipients,
                    null,
                    null,
                    subject,
                    body,
                    null,
                    false,
                    true,
                    "zensync@unlock.com");

                ZenLogger.Info(LogSource, "Settlement sync email sent to {0}", _notificationRecipients);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                ZenLogger.Error(LogSource, "Failed to send settlement sync email: {0}", ex.Message);
            }
        }

        private async Task ProcessTicketWithRetryAsync(Ticket ticket, long prevTicketId)
        {
            await ExecuteWithRetryAsync<object>(
                async () =>
                {
                    bool needsUpdate = TicketNeedsUpdate(ticket.Id, ticket.UpdatedAt);
                    if (needsUpdate)
                    {
                        await _zt.SyncTicket(ticket.Id);
                        _defaultsCache[ticket.Id] = ticket.UpdatedAt;
                    }
                    return null;
                },
                3,
                "Failed to get Ticket after ticket: " + prevTicketId);
        }

        private async Task<T> ExecuteWithRetryAsync<T>(Func<Task<T>> op, int maxRetries, string failureMessage)
        {
            int delay = 1000;
            for (int attempt = 0; attempt < maxRetries; attempt++)
            {
                try
                {
                    return await op();
                }
                catch (Exception ex)
                {
                    ZenLogger.Warning(LogSource, "Attempt {0} failed: {1}", attempt + 1, ex.Message);
                    if (attempt == (maxRetries - 1))
                    {
                        ZenLogger.Error(LogSource, failureMessage, ex);
                        break;
                    }
                    await Task.Delay(delay);
                    delay *= 2;
                }
            }
            return default(T);
        }

        public bool TicketNeedsUpdate(string server, long ticket_id, DateTime updated_at)
        {
            return TicketNeedsUpdate(ticket_id, updated_at);
        }

        public bool TicketNeedsUpdate(long ticket_id, DateTime updated_at)
        {
            DateTime cachedUpdateTime;
            if (_defaultsCache != null && _defaultsCache.TryGetValue(ticket_id, out cachedUpdateTime))
            {
                return Math.Abs((cachedUpdateTime - updated_at).TotalMinutes) > 30 && updated_at > cachedUpdateTime;
            }
            return true;
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: ZenLib\ZenLogger.cs ---
namespace ZenLib
{
    public static class ZenLogger
    {
        public enum LogLevel
        {
            Debug,
            Info,
            Warning,
            Error
        }
        public static LogLevel MinimumLevel { get; set; } = LogLevel.Info;
        public static Action<LogLevel, string, string> CustomLogHandler { get; set; }

        public static void Debug(string source, string message)
        {
            Log(LogLevel.Debug, source, message);
        }

        public static void Debug(string source, string message, params object[] args)
        {
            Log(LogLevel.Debug, source, string.Format(message, args));
        }

        public static void Info(string source, string message)
        {
            Log(LogLevel.Info, source, message);
        }

        public static void Info(string source, string message, params object[] args)
        {
            Log(LogLevel.Info, source, string.Format(message, args));
        }

        public static void Warning(string source, string message)
        {
            Log(LogLevel.Warning, source, message);
        }

        public static void Warning(string source, string message, params object[] args)
        {
            Log(LogLevel.Warning, source, string.Format(message, args));
        }

        public static void Error(string source, string message)
        {
            Log(LogLevel.Error, source, message);
        }

        public static void Error(string source, string message, params object[] args)
        {
            Log(LogLevel.Error, source, string.Format(message, args));
        }

        public static void Error(string source, string message, Exception ex)
        {
            Log(LogLevel.Error, source, message + " - Exception: " + ex.Message);
        }

        private static void Log(LogLevel level, string source, string message)
        {
            if (level < MinimumLevel)
                return;

            string timestamp = DateTime.Now.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss");
            string levelStr = level.ToString().ToUpper().PadRight(7);
            string formattedMessage = string.Format("[{0}] [{1}] [{2}] {3}", timestamp, levelStr, source, message);

            
            ConsoleColor originalColor = Console.ForegroundColor;
            switch (level)
            {
                case LogLevel.Debug:
                    Console.ForegroundColor = ConsoleColor.Gray;
                    break;
                case LogLevel.Info:
                    Console.ForegroundColor = ConsoleColor.White;
                    break;
                case LogLevel.Warning:
                    Console.ForegroundColor = ConsoleColor.Yellow;
                    break;
                case LogLevel.Error:
                    Console.ForegroundColor = ConsoleColor.Red;
                    break;
            }

            Console.WriteLine(formattedMessage);
            Console.ForegroundColor = originalColor;

            
            CustomLogHandler?.Invoke(level, source, message);
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: BigDoughLib\Class1.cs ---
namespace BigDoughLib
{
    public class BigDoughLib
    {
        public static List<Holder> SaveHolders(string filename, IWriter writer)
        {
            
            
            
            Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.Application app = new Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.Application();
            XLHelper xlh = new XLHelper(app);
            if (null != writer)
                writer("Opening Spreadsheet....");
            xlh.OpenSheet(filename);
            xlh.DeleteRowRange(1, 6);
            xlh.DeleteRowRange(2, 2);
            
            xlh.DeleteColumn("AE");

            string used_range_address = xlh.UsedRangeAddress("Accounts");
            XLTable tbl = new XLTable(xlh, used_range_address);
            if (null != writer)
                writer("Converting to DataTable");
            
            List<Holder> holders = new List<Holder>();

            if (null != writer)
                writer("Parsing Data...");
            foreach (var v in tbl.AllRows("CUSIP"))
            {

                Holder h = new Holder();
                h.account = v["Account Name"];
                h.position_date = System.Convert.ToDateTime(v["Position Date"]);
                h.cusip = v["CUSIP"];
                h.par_held = System.Convert.ToDouble(v["Par Held USD, mm"]);
                h.par_change = System.Convert.ToDouble(v["Par Change USD, mm"]);
                if(v.ContainsField("Aggregate Position Date (Selected Bonds)"))
                    h.aggregate_position_date = System.Convert.ToDateTime(v["Aggregate Position Date (Selected Bonds)"]);

                holders.Add(h);
            }

            xlh.Quit();

            return holders;
        }

        public static int WriteToDatabase(string server, List<Holder> holders, IWriter writer,Nullable<int> load_id)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.InsertHolder @cusip=@cusip, @account=@account, @position_date=@position_date, @par_held=@par_held, @par_change=@par_change, @aggregate_position_date=@aggregate_position_date, @load_id=@load_id";

            ETA eta = new ETA(holders.Count, writer);

            foreach (Holder h in holders)
            {
                Query q = new Query(sql, server);
                q.AddParameter("@cusip", h.cusip);
                q.AddParameter("@account", h.account);
                q.AddParameter("@position_date", h.position_date);
                q.AddParameter("@par_held", h.par_held);
                q.AddParameter("@par_change", h.par_change);
                q.AddParameter("@aggregate_position_date", h.aggregate_position_date);
                q.AddParameter("@load_id", load_id);
                q.Execute();
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
            }
            return holders.Count;
        }

    }

    public class Holder
    {
        public string account;
        public DateTime position_date;
        public string cusip;
        public Nullable<double> par_held;
        public Nullable<double> par_change;
        public Nullable<DateTime> aggregate_position_date;
    }
}


--- FILE: BigDoughLib\Loader.cs ---
namespace BigDoughLib
{
    public class Loader
    {
        public static int HandleLoad(string server, string search_path, bool archive, IWriter writer)
        {
            
            
            
            
            
            Nullable<int> load_id = null;
            int loaded = 0;
            foreach (string s in Directory.GetFiles(search_path,"*.xls"))
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Loading: " + s);
                List<Holder> holders = BigDoughLib.SaveHolders(s, Console.WriteLine);
                
                load_id = GetLoadIDfromFilename(s);

                loaded += BigDoughLib.WriteToDatabase(server, holders, Console.WriteLine, load_id);
                
                if (archive)
                {
                    bool file_ready = UtilsLib.FileLib.IsFileReady(s, 120, 1);
                    if (!file_ready)
                        throw new Exception("File Not Ready! - " + s);
                    string archive_path = Path.GetDirectoryName(s) + @"\Archive";
                    UtilsLib.FileLib.ArchiveFile(archive_path, s, "M.d.yy - H.mmss", true,null,false,true);
                }
            }
            return loaded;
        }
        public static Nullable<int> GetLoadIDfromFilename(string filename)
        {
            Nullable<int> answer = null;
            if(filename.Contains("Load") && filename.Split('-').Length == 5 && filename.Split('-')[4].Trim().Split(' ').Length == 2)
            {
                string f = Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(filename);
                string end = f.Split('-')[4].Trim().Split(' ')[1];
                int last;
                bool succes = Int32.TryParse(end, out last);
                if (succes)
                    return last;
            }
            return null;
        }
    }


}

namespace BigDoughLib
{
    public class PortfolioLoader : DBLHelper.GenericBase, IDBLoader
    {
        public PortfolioLoader(string server) : base(server)
        {

        }

        public static void MarkAsAttemptedParse(string server, int holder_account_id)
        {
            string sql = "update HolderAccounts set last_portfolio_attempt_parse = GetDate() where id = @holder_account_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@holder_account_id", holder_account_id);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public void PopulateCusipsQueued()
        {
            if(null != _writer)
                _writer("Downloading All Cusips....");
            string sql = "select distinct cusip from Assets a where a.cusip is not null ";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            var list = q.ExecuteList<string>();

            cusips_queued.AddRange(list);


            sql = "select distinct cusip from BBGDataQueue a where a.cusip is not null ";
            q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            var already_queued = q.ExecuteList<string>();

            cusips_queued.AddRange(already_queued.Except(cusips_queued));
        }
        
        public bool just_queue = false;
        public List<string> cusips_queued = new List<string>();
        public List<string> cusips_actually_queued = new List<string>();
        private XLHelper xlh = null;
        private List<string> only_products = null;
        public DBOutputHelper ParseAndLoad()
        {

            
            just_queue = System.Convert.ToBoolean(base._parms["ONLYQUEUE"]);
            bool visible_excel = true;
            bool use_bbg = true;
            if (base._parms.ContainsKey("USEBBG"))
                use_bbg = System.Convert.ToBoolean(base._parms["USEBBG"]);
            if (base._parms.ContainsKey("HIDEEXCEL"))
                visible_excel = !System.Convert.ToBoolean(base._parms["HIDEEXCEL"]);
            if (base._parms.ContainsKey("ONLYPRODUCTS"))
            {
                only_products = new List<string>(base._parms["ONLYPRODUCTS"].ToString().Split(','));
            }
            if(just_queue)
                PopulateCusipsQueued();
            xlh = new XL.XLHelper(null);
            xlh.CreateNewApp();
            if (null != _writer)
                _writer("Opening Spreadsheet....");
            xlh.OpenSheetReadOnly(base._input);
            
            
            string ws = "InvestorHistory(2)";
            xlh.ActivateSheet(ws);
            
            xlh.ToggleShowApp(visible_excel);

            
            string mail_override_added = "ADDED:" + Environment.NewLine;
            string mail_override_errors = "Couldn't add:" + Environment.NewLine;
            string fund_name = xlh.GetRange<string>(ws, "A1", false);
            int? bd_holder_account = null;
            int? account_id = null;

            
            if (just_queue == false)
            {

                bd_holder_account = BatCaveLib.Holders.GetHolderAccountIdFromBDName(_server, fund_name);
                if (null == bd_holder_account)
                {
                    bd_holder_account =
                        BatCaveLib.Holders.InsertUpdateHolderAccount(_server, null, fund_name, 1158, 11, null, null,
                            true);
                }

                MarkAsAttemptedParse(_server, bd_holder_account.Value);
                if (null != bd_holder_account)
                    BatCaveLib.Portfolios.DeleteAllPortfolios(_server, bd_holder_account.Value, 2);

                account_id = BatCaveLib.Holders.GetCaveAccountIdFromBDName(_server, fund_name);
                
                
                if (null == account_id)
                    account_id = 1158;

            }


            string last_col = xlh.LastUsedColumn(ws, null);
            int rowcheck = 3;
            string check = xlh.GetRange<string>("InvestorHistory(2)", "A2", false, null, false);
            if (!String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(check))
                rowcheck = 2;



            int last_row = xlh.LastUsedRow(ws, "A");
            int last_column_num = xlh.LastUsedColumnNumber(ws, null);
            string last_row_1_header = null;
            for (int i = 1; i != last_column_num; i++)
            {
                string column_letter = UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.ColumnNumberToLetter(i);
                string range = $"{column_letter}{1}";
                string row_1_header = xlh.GetRange<string>(ws, range, true);

                string col_val = $"{column_letter}{rowcheck}";
                string row_3_header = xlh.GetRange<string>(ws, col_val, true);
                if (!String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(row_1_header))
                {
                    last_row_1_header = row_1_header;
                }

                if (!String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(last_row_1_header))
                {
                    string new_header = $"{row_3_header}-{last_row_1_header}";
                    xlh.WriteRange(ws, col_val, new_header);
                }

            }

            if (null != _writer)
            {
                _writer("Grabbing Rows...");
            }
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "A" + rowcheck + ":" + last_col + last_row);
            var rows = xlt.AllRows("CUSIP");

            if (null != _writer)
            {
                _writer("Done Grabbing Rows...");
            }

            
            







            var date_columns = xlt._header_indexes;

            
            int how_many = 0;

            foreach (var date_run in date_columns)
            {
                if (!date_run.Key.Contains("Par-"))
                    continue;
                DateTime asOf;
                if (!DateTime.TryParse(date_run.Key.Replace("Par-", ""), out asOf))
                {
                    continue;
                }

                how_many += 1;
            }

            UtilsLib.ETA eta = new UtilsLib.ETA(rows.Count()*how_many, _writer);
            
            List<DateTime> completed_date_runs = new List<DateTime>();
            
            foreach (var date_run in date_columns)
            {
                
                if (!date_run.Key.Contains("Par-"))
                    continue;
                DateTime asOf;
                if (!DateTime.TryParse(date_run.Key.Replace("Par-", ""), out asOf))
                {
                    continue;
                }
                
                
                


                
                
                
                
                

                
                

                
                if(just_queue && completed_date_runs.Count > 0)
                    break;

                if (null != _writer)
                {
                    _writer("Processing: " + asOf);
                }
                int? portfolio_id = null;
                if (!just_queue)
                {
                    portfolio_id = BatCaveLib.Portfolios.GetPortfolioID(_server, account_id.Value, asOf, 2);

                    if (null == portfolio_id)
                    {
                        portfolio_id = BatCaveLib.Portfolios.InsertUpdatePortfolio(_server, account_id.Value, asOf,
                            fund_name, null, false, bd_holder_account, 2);
                    }
                }


                int loaded_bonds = 0;
                foreach (XLTable.XLTableRow row in rows)
                {
                    string cusip = row["CUSIP"].ToString();
                    string bond_type = row["Security Group"];

                    if (null != only_products)
                    {
                        if(!only_products.Contains(bond_type))
                            continue;
                    }

                    if (just_queue && !String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(cusip))
                    {
                        if (!cusips_queued.Contains(cusip))
                        {
                            string t = Assets.MT.GetTickerOrQueueIfNot(_server, cusip);

                            if (null != t && t.Contains("QUEUED"))
                            {
                                if (null != _writer)
                                    _writer("Added To Queue: " + cusip);
                                cusips_actually_queued.Add(cusip);
                            }

                            cusips_queued.Add(cusip);
                        }
                        continue;
                    }
      

                    string ticker = MT.Ticker(_server, cusip, false, false);

                    if (null == ticker)
                    {
                        string ticker_from_alt = MT.InsertUpdateBondLookup(_server, cusip, ticker);
                        if (null == ticker && null != ticker_from_alt)
                        {
                            ticker = ticker_from_alt;
                        }
                    }

                    if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(ticker) && use_bbg == false)
                    {
                        continue;
                    } 
                    if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(ticker))
                    {
                        
                        List<string> needed_fields = new List<string>();
                        needed_fields.Add("ticker");
                        needed_fields.Add("bbg_id");
                        needed_fields.Add("cusip");
                        try
                        {
                            var helper = MT.InsertUpdateIfNeeded(_server, cusip, false, false, needed_fields, true);
                            
                            if (helper.tickers.ContainsKey(cusip))
                                ticker = helper.tickers[cusip];
                        }
                        catch (Exception n)
                        {
                            mail_override_errors += cusip + Environment.NewLine;
                            continue;
                        }

                        string cusip_alt = MT.Cusip(_server, ticker, false, false);
                        if (cusip != cusip_alt)
                        {
                            MT.InsertUpdateBondLookup(_server, cusip, ticker);
                        }

                    }
                    Database.DBCache.GetInstance().Pool.Clear();
                    double? oface = null;
                    double oface_tmp = 0;
                    if(Double.TryParse(row[date_run.Key],out oface_tmp))
                        oface = oface_tmp;

                    eta.IncrementAndReport();
                    
                    if(null == oface || oface == 0.0) 
                        continue;

                    if(String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(ticker))
                        mail_override_errors += cusip + Environment.NewLine;
                    else
                    {
                        if(!just_queue)
                            BatCaveLib.Portfolios.InsertPortfolioDetail(_server, portfolio_id.Value, ticker, oface, null, null);
                        loaded_bonds++;
                    }
                    
                }

                if (loaded_bonds == 0 && null != portfolio_id)
                {
                    BatCaveLib.Portfolios.DeletePortfolio(_server, portfolio_id.Value);
                }

                completed_date_runs.Add(asOf);

            }

            Database.DBCache.GetInstance().Pool.Clear();
            System.GC.Collect();
            
            xlh.Quit(5000);
            DBOutputHelper oh = new DBOutputHelper();
            oh.rows = rows.Count() - 1;
            if (just_queue)
            {
                mail_override_added = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, cusips_actually_queued);
            }
            oh.email_body_override = mail_override_errors + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine + mail_override_added;
            return oh;
        }

        public void FinishUp()
        {
            if(null != xlh)
            {
                xlh.Quit(5000);
            }
        }


    }
}

namespace BigDoughLib
{
    public class Scraper
    {

        string _user;
        string _password;
        string _server;
        string _download_folder;

        public Scraper(string user, string password, string server, string download_folder)
        {
            _user = user;
            _password = password;
            _server = server;
            _download_folder = download_folder;
        }

        List<string> _cusips = new List<string>();

        public int total_cusips
        {
            get { return _cusips.Count; }
        }

        public void AddCusip(string cusip)
        {
            if (!_cusips.Contains(cusip))
                _cusips.Add(cusip);
        }


        public void LoadUpcomingBWICCusips(int limit, string sql)
        {
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            List<string> cusips = q.ExecuteList<string>("cusip", 0);

            if (cusips.Count > limit)
                cusips.RemoveRange(limit, cusips.Count - limit);

            _cusips = cusips;
        }

        public void LoadUpcomingAccounts(int limit, string sql)
        {
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            List<string> cusips = q.ExecuteList<string>("name", 0);

            
            if (cusips.Count > limit)
                cusips.RemoveRange(limit, cusips.Count - limit);

            _cusips = cusips;
        }

        public Nullable<int> load_id = null;

        public void PopulateLoadId()
        {
            this.load_id = Database.Common.GetNextId(_server, "holderload_id");
        }

        public static void MarkAsAttemptedParse(string server, int fund_id,DateTime? start, DateTime? end)
        {
            string sql = "update HolderAccounts set last_portfolio_attempt_scrape_start = @start, last_portfolio_attempt_scrape_end = @end where id = @fund_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@fund_id", fund_id);
            q.AddParameter("@start", start);
            q.AddParameter("@end", end);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public void RecordLoadAttempt()
        {

            foreach (string cusip in _cusips)
            {
                RecordSingleLoad(cusip, load_id.Value);
            }

        }

        public void RecordSingleLoad(string cusip, int holderload_id)
        {
            string sql = "insert into HolderLoads (cusip,requested,holderload_id) VALUES (@cusip,1,@holderload_id)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@cusip", cusip);
            q.AddParameter("@holderload_id", holderload_id);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public void Exit()
        {
            if (null != driver)
                driver.Quit();
        }

        ChromeDriver driver = null;
        ChromeOptions _options = null;

            _options = new ChromeOptions();

            }
            _options.AddUserProfilePreference("disable -popup-blocking", "true");
        }

                    var logout = driver.FindElementById("ctrlLogin_btnDeleteLockedSession");

        public void DeleteAnyPortfolios()
        {

            Console.WriteLine("[BEGIN] Downloading All Portfolios...");
            try
            {
                var frame = driver.FindElements(By.TagName("hostFrame"));
                driver.SwitchTo().Frame("hostFrame");

            catch (Exception n)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Frame Doesn't Exist");
            }

            Console.WriteLine("BEGIN Deleting All Portfolios...");

            var s = driver.FindElements(By.ClassName("remove-column"));
            foreach (var q in s)
            {
                if (q.Displayed && q.Text == "×")
                {
                    q.Click();
                    System.Threading.Thread.Sleep(1000);
                    FindAndClick("OK", "OK", 1500);
                    
            

            

            


            
            
            
            
            


            
            


            
            LogoutBD();

            string hack_folder = @"C:\Users\DFoster\Downloads";
            foreach (string file in System.IO.Directory.GetFiles(hack_folder, "*.xls"))
            {
                DateTime modified = System.IO.File.GetCreationTimeUtc(file);
                TimeSpan ts = DateTime.UtcNow - modified;
                if (ts.TotalMinutes < 5)
                {
                    string file_local = Path.GetFileName(file);
                    string full = Path.Combine(this._download_folder, file_local);
                    File.Move(file, full);
                }
            }
             if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(this._download_folder))
            {
                if (System.IO.Directory.GetFiles(this._download_folder,"*.xls").Length == 1)
                {
                    string file = System.IO.Directory.GetFiles(this._download_folder)[0];
                    DateTime modified = System.IO.File.GetCreationTimeUtc(file);
                    TimeSpan ts = DateTime.UtcNow - modified;
                    if (ts.TotalMinutes < 5)
                    {
                        bool is_file_ready = UtilsLib.FileLib.IsFileReady(file, 30, 5);
                        if(is_file_ready)
                        {
                            string raw = System.IO.Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(file);
                            string ext = System.IO.Path.GetExtension(file);
                            string new_file = String.Format("BigDoughLoad - {0:M-d-yy h.mm.ss tt} - Load {1}", DateTime.Now, this.load_id);
                            string new_full_file = Path.Combine(this._download_folder, new_file) + ext;
                            string path_combine = Path.Combine(this._download_folder, new_full_file);
                            System.IO.File.Move(file, path_combine);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
