--- FILE: BigDoughLib\SQL\LawHorn.sql ---
select distinct a.cusip
  from 
    Assets a
    left join HolderLoads hl on a.cusip = hl.cusip
    where
    hl.cusip is null
    and a.cusip not like 'BCC%'
    and a.ticker like 'TPMT%'
    group by a.cusip


--- FILE: BigDoughLib\SQL\UpcomingAccounts.sql ---
select * 
  from 
    HolderAccounts ha 
    where 
      ha.account_id is not null 
      and 
      (
        (ha.last_portfolio_attempt_scrape_start is null and ha.last_portfolio_attempt_parse is null)
        or
        (ha.last_portfolio_attempt_scrape_start < dateadd(month,-1,GetDate()) and (ha.last_portfolio_attempt_parse is null or ha.last_portfolio_attempt_parse < dateadd(month,-1,GetDate()) ))
        
      )
      AND ha.current_aum is not null
	  AND HA.current_aum > 0
  order by ha.current_aum asc


--- FILE: BigDoughLib\SQL\UpcomingCusips.sql ---
declare @bwics table
(
  last_bwic smalldatetime
  , ticker varchar(30)
  , cusip varchar(9)
  , bond_label_1 varchar(30)
  , last_update smalldatetime
  , product_id int
)

insert into @bwics (last_bwic,ticker,cusip,bond_label_1,last_update,product_id)
select max(b.bid_time) [last_bwic],bwd.ticker,a.cusip,a.bond_label_1,a.last_bbg_update,a.product_id
from
  BWICs b
  join BWICDetail bwd on b.id = bwd.bwic_id
  join Assets a on a.ticker=bwd.ticker
  group by bwd.ticker,a.cusip,bond_label_1,last_bbg_update,product_id


  
declare @needed table
(
  cusip varchar(9)
  , last_update smalldatetime
  , bond_label_1 varchar(40)
  , last_bwic_modified smalldatetime
  , last_bd_update smalldatetime
  , priority int
  , note varchar(30)
  , product_id float
  , added_to_database smalldatetime
)


insert into @needed (cusip,last_bwic_modified,bond_label_1,last_update,note,product_id) select cusip, case when b.last_bwic > dateadd(wk,-1,GetDate()) then b.last_bwic else null end,bond_label_1,last_update,'BWIC',product_id from @bwics b


insert into @needed (cusip,last_update,bond_label_1,note,product_id,added_to_database)
select distinct a.cusip,max(a.last_bbg_update) [last_update],a.bond_label_1, 'ASSETS',product_id,added_to_database

  from 
    Assets a
    

    
    where

    
    
    
    not exists (select * from @needed h where h.cusip = a.cusip)
    and a.product_id in (1,2,3,4,8,10,15,13,5,7)
    group by 
      a.cusip
      , a.bond_label_1
      , a.product_id
      , added_to_database
    
   update n SET LAST_BD_UPDATE = HL.UPDATE_TIME FROM @needed n join HolderLoads hl on hl.cusip = N.cusip
   
   UPDATE @needed SET PRIORITY = 1 where cast(last_bwic_modified as date) >= dbo.Today()
   UPDATE @needed SET PRIORITY = 2 where cast(last_update as date) = dbo.Today() and (product_id not IN (7,13) and cast(added_to_database as date) = dbo.Today())
   
   
   update @needed set priority = 2.5 WHERE PRODUCT_ID = 1 and priority is null
   update @needed set priority = 3 WHERE PRODUCT_ID = 2 and priority is null
   update @needed set priority = 4 WHERE PRODUCT_ID = 3 and priority is null
   update @needed set priority = 5 WHERE PRODUCT_ID = 4 and priority is null
   update @needed set priority = 6 WHERE PRODUCT_ID = 10 and priority is null
   update @needed set priority = 7 WHERE PRODUCT_ID = 17 and priority is null
   update @needed set priority = 8 WHERE PRODUCT_ID = 8 and priority is null
   
   update @needed set priority = 13 WHERE PRODUCT_ID = 5 and priority is null
   update @needed set priority = 14 WHERE PRODUCT_ID = 7 and priority is null
   UPDATE @needed SET PRIORITY = 12 WHERE priority is null
   
  delete n from @needed n where exists (select * from HolderLoads h where h.cusip = n.cusip)
  delete n from @needed n where cusip like 'BCC%'
 


 
   
 select * from @needed where cusip is not null order by priority asc
 
 
 
    
select COUNT(*) [remaining],bond_label_1 from @needed group by bond_label_1 order by count(*) desc


--- FILE: BigDoughLib\Utils.cs ---
namespace BigDoughLib
{
    public class Utils
    {
        public static int PruneLoads(string server,List<string> cusips, int? top)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.PruneBDHolders @cusips=@cusips, @top=@top";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@cusips", cusips);
            q.AddParameter("@top", top);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count;
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: MUNILib\MSRBLoader.cs ---
namespace MUNILib
{
    public class MSRBLoader : DBLHelper.GenericBase, IDBLoader
    {

        public MSRBLoader(string server) : base(server)
        {

        }

        private XLHelper xlh = null;
        bool trace_format = false;
        DateTime? create_time = null;
        public DBOutputHelper ParseAndLoad()
        {
            List<string> errors = new List<string>();
            trace_format = base._parms.ContainsKey("@FORMAT");

            xlh = new XLHelper(null);
            xlh.CreateNewApp();
            if (null != _writer)
                _writer("Opening Spreadsheet....");
            xlh.OpenSheetReadOnly(base._input);
            string ws = "Worksheet";
            xlh.ActivateSheet(ws);

            xlh.ToggleShowApp(true);
            _writer += xlh.WriteStatusBar;
            int last_row = xlh.LastUsedRow(ws, "A");

            string cusip_field = "CUSIP";
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "A1:P" + last_row);

            if (trace_format)
            {
                cusip_field = "SECURITY";
                xlt.HeadersToUpper();
            }

            var all_rows = xlt.AllRows(cusip_field);
            ETA eta = new ETA(all_rows.Count, _writer);

            create_time = System.IO.File.GetCreationTime(base._input);
            

            foreach (var row in all_rows)
            {
                double? price = null;
                double? yield = null;
                double? spread_cnv = null;
                string size = null;
                string buy_sell = null;
                string cusip = null;
                string date_raw = null;
                double? cface = null;
                double? oface = null;
                int? num_trades = null;
                int? total_volume = null;
                string ticker = null;
                if (!trace_format)
                {

                    cusip = row["CUSIP"];
                    
                    yield = row.GetNullable<double>("Yield", new List<string>(new string[] {"--"}));
                    spread_cnv = row.GetNullable<double>("Spd Conv");
                    size = row["Sz (M)"];
                    
                    buy_sell = row["R"];
                    price = row.GetNullable<double>("Price");
                    date_raw = row["Time"];
                    int oface_tmp;
                    if (int.TryParse(size, out oface_tmp))
                        oface = oface_tmp;
                }
                else
                {
                    ticker = row[cusip_field];
                    if(null == cusip)
                        cusip = ticker;
                    size = row["ORIG FACE(M)"];
                    string cface_str = xlt.ContainsColumn("CUR FACE(M)") ? row["CUR FACE(M)"] : row["CURR FACE(M)"];
                    cface = System.Convert.ToDouble(cface_str.Replace("+",""));
                    oface = System.Convert.ToDouble(size.Replace("+", ""));

                    price = row.GetNullable<double>("PRICE");
                    date_raw = row["TIME"];
                    total_volume = xlt.ContainsColumn("VOL(M)") ? row.GetNullable<int>("VOL(M)") : row.GetNullable<int>("TOTAL VOLUME(M)");
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    num_trades = xlt.ContainsColumn("TRADES") ? row.GetNullable<int>("TRADES") : row.GetNullable<int>("TRADES#");
                }

                

                
                DateTime d;
                if (date_raw.Contains(":"))
                    date_raw = $"{create_time.Value.Date:MM/dd/yyyy} {date_raw}";
                DateTime trade_time = System.Convert.ToDateTime(date_raw);
                if (trade_time > DateTime.Today)
                    trade_time = trade_time.AddYears(-1);

                

                if (null == ticker)
                {
                    
                    var updated = Assets.MT.InsertUpdateIfNeeded(_server, cusip, false, false, null, true);
                    ticker = Assets.MT.Ticker(_server, cusip, false, false);
                }

                DateTime before = base._parms.ContainsKey("@UPDATEBEFORE") ? System.Convert.ToDateTime(base._parms["@UPDATEBEFORE"]) : DateTime.MinValue;

                DateTime? last_update = Assets.MT.GetAssetValue<DateTime>(_server, cusip, "last_bbg_update", false, false);
                string name = null;
                if(Validate.IsTicker(cusip))
                    name = cusip;
                else
                    name = Assets.MT.GetAssetValueNullable<string>(_server, cusip, "name", false, false);
                if ((before != DateTime.MinValue && (null != last_update && last_update < before)) || String.IsNullOrEmpty(name))
                {
                    Assets.MT.InsertUpdateIfNeeded(_server, cusip, false, false, null, false);
                }

                if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(ticker))
                {

                    
                    if(!errors.Contains(cusip))
                        errors.Add(cusip);
                    continue;
                }
                string benchmark = null;
                if(null != ticker && ticker.Contains("QUEUE"))
                    ticker = cusip;
                else
                {
                    if(!trace_format)
                        benchmark = Assets.MT.GetAssetValueNullable<string>(_server, cusip, "yas_benchmark", false, false);
                    if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(benchmark))
                    {
                        benchmark = benchmark.Split(' ')[0];
                        bool exists = Assets.MT.TickerInAssetsTable(_server, benchmark);
                        if (!exists)
                        {
                            string cusip_check_digit = Validate.CalcCusipCheckDigit(benchmark);
                            benchmark = cusip_check_digit;
                            Assets.MT.InsertUpdateIfNeeded(_server, benchmark, false, false, null, true);
                        }
                    }
                }





                BatCaveLib.Trace.InsertUpdateTrade(_server, ticker, oface, cface, price, num_trades, total_volume, trade_time, size, yield, spread_cnv, buy_sell);
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
            }

            xlh.Quit();
            var output = new DBOutputHelper();
            output.rows = all_rows.Count();
            if (errors.Count() > 0)
            {
                string message = "Couldn't Add: " + Environment.NewLine + String.Join(Environment.NewLine, errors);
                output.email_body_override = message;
            }

            
            
            
            
                
            
            return output;
        }


        public static List<string> CusipsNeedUpdating(string server, List<string> cusips,DateTime before)
        {
            string sql =
                "select distinct cusip from Assets a join @cusips c on c.item = a.cusip and a.last_bbg_udpate <= @before";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@cusips", cusips);
            q.AddParameter("@before", before);
            return q.ExecuteList<string>("cusip");
        }
    }

        public static string Find4506(string server, string asset_id, IEnumerable<string> search_keys, string dest_folder_if_found)
        {
            string temp_path = Path.GetTempPath();
            foreach (string search_key in search_keys)
            {
                var files = DownloadFiles(server, asset_id, new string[] { search_key }, temp_path).Distinct();
                foreach (string file in files)
                {
                    int? complete_4506c = CreditLib.TaxLib.ApplicationHasComplete4506C(file);
                    if(null != complete_4506c)
                    {
                        return CreditLib.TaxLib.Trim4506IfNeeded(file,dest_folder_if_found);                            
                    }
                    
                    File.Delete(file);
                }
            }
            return null;
        }

        public static List<string> DownloadFiles(string server, string asset_id, IEnumerable<string> search_keys, string dest_folder)
        {
            int doc_count = 0;
            List<string> results = new List<string>();
            DataTable ap_ids = MaxLib.Assets.FindApplicationProfileID(server, asset_id);
            foreach (DataRow row in ap_ids.Rows)
            {
                Directory.CreateDirectory(dest_folder);
                foreach (string search_key in search_keys)
                {
                    List<int> doc_ids = MaxDocVaultLib.MaxDocVault
                        .SearchForDocument(row["id"].ToString(), search_key).Result;

                    if (!doc_ids.Any()) continue;

                    foreach (var doc_id in doc_ids)
                    {
                        string file = MaxDocVaultLib.MaxDocVault
                            .DownloadByDocumentID(row["id"].ToString(), dest_folder, doc_id).Result;

                        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(file) && File.Exists(file))
                        {
                            results.Add(file);
                            doc_count++;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            return results;
        }

        public static List<string> DownloadFilesByRecordingStatus(string server, string asset_id, string recording_status, string dest_folder)
        {
            int doc_count = 0;
            List<string> results = new List<string>();
            DataTable ap_ids = MaxLib.Assets.FindApplicationProfileID(server, asset_id);
            foreach (DataRow row in ap_ids.Rows)
            {
                Directory.CreateDirectory(dest_folder);
                List<int> doc_ids = MaxDocVaultLib.MaxDocVault
                    .SearchForDocumentByRecordingStatus(row["id"].ToString(), recording_status).Result;

                if (!doc_ids.Any()) continue;

                foreach (var doc_id in doc_ids)
                {
                    string file = MaxDocVaultLib.MaxDocVault
                        .DownloadByDocumentID(row["id"].ToString(), dest_folder, doc_id).Result;

                    if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(file) && File.Exists(file))
                    {
                        results.Add(file);
                        doc_count++;
                    }
                }
            }
            return results;
        }

        
        public static Dictionary<string, string> FindThirdPartyReviewPackages(
            string server,
            IEnumerable<string> asset_ids,
            string destinationFolder)
        {
            var results = new Dictionary<string, string>();
            if (asset_ids == null) return results;

            Directory.CreateDirectory(destinationFolder);
            string temp_path = Path.GetTempPath();
            string[] searchTerms = { "Third Party Review Package" };

            foreach (var asset_id in asset_ids)
            {
                string finalPath = null;
                try
                {
                    var downloaded = DownloadFiles(server, asset_id, searchTerms, temp_path)
                        .Where(f => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(f) && File.Exists(f))
                        .Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                        .ToList();

                    var first = downloaded.FirstOrDefault();
                    if (first != null)
                    {
                        string ext = Path.GetExtension(first);
                        
                        string target = Path.Combine(destinationFolder,
                            $"{asset_id}_ThirdPartyReviewPackage{ext}");

                        
                        File.Copy(first, target, true);

                        
                        var info = new FileInfo(target);
                        if (info.Length > 0)
                        {
                            finalPath = target;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            File.Delete(target);
                        }
                    }
                }
                catch
                {
                    finalPath = null;
                }
                results[asset_id] = finalPath;
            }
            return results;
        }

        
        public static Dictionary<string, List<string>> FindRecordedSecurityInstrument(
            string server,
            IEnumerable<string> asset_ids,
            string destinationFolder)
        {
            var results = new Dictionary<string, List<string>>();
            if (asset_ids == null) return results;

            Directory.CreateDirectory(destinationFolder);
            string temp_path = Path.GetTempPath();
            string[] searchTerms = { "Recorded" };
            string[] fallbackSearchTerms = { "_DOT" };

            foreach (var asset_id in asset_ids)
            {
                var copiedForAsset = new List<string>();
                try
                {
                    var downloaded = DownloadFiles(server, asset_id, searchTerms, temp_path)
                        .Where(f => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(f) && File.Exists(f))
                        .Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                        .ToList();

                    
                    var matches = downloaded
                        .Where(f => 
                        {
                            string fileName = Path.GetFileName(f);
                            return fileName.IndexOf("recorded", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) >= 0
                                && fileName.IndexOf("unrecorded", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) < 0;
                        })
                        .ToList();

                    
                    if (matches.Count == 0)
                    {
                        var fallbackDownloaded = DownloadFiles(server, asset_id, fallbackSearchTerms, temp_path)
                            .Where(f => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(f) && File.Exists(f))
                            .Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                            .ToList();

                        matches = fallbackDownloaded
                            .Where(f =>
                            {
                                string fileName = Path.GetFileName(f);
                                return fileName.IndexOf("_DOT", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) >= 0;
                            })
                            .ToList();
                    }

                    if (matches.Count > 0)
                    {
                        
                        if (matches.Count == 1)
                        {
                            var file = matches[0];
                            string ext = Path.GetExtension(file);
                            string target = Path.Combine(destinationFolder, $"{asset_id}{ext}");

                            File.Copy(file, target, true);
                            copiedForAsset.Add(target);

                            
                            try { File.Delete(file); } catch { }
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            
                            string assetDir = Path.Combine(destinationFolder, asset_id);
                            Directory.CreateDirectory(assetDir);

                            foreach (var file in matches)
                            {
                                string fileName = Path.GetFileName(file);
                                string target = Path.Combine(assetDir, fileName);

                                
                                if (File.Exists(target))
                                {
                                    string name = Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(fileName);
                                    string ext = Path.GetExtension(fileName);
                                    int idx = 1;
                                    while (File.Exists(target))
                                    {
                                        target = Path.Combine(assetDir, $"{name}_{idx}{ext}");
                                        idx++;
                                    }
                                }

                                File.Copy(file, target, true);
                                copiedForAsset.Add(target);

                                
                                try { File.Delete(file); } catch { }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                catch
                {
                    
                }
                results[asset_id] = copiedForAsset;
            }

            
            try
            {
                var notFound = results.Where(kvp => kvp.Value == null || kvp.Value.Count == 0)
                                      .Select(kvp => kvp.Key)
                                      .ToList();
                if (notFound.Count > 0)
                {
                    string notFoundPath = Path.Combine(destinationFolder, "Assets_Not_Found.txt");
                    File.WriteAllLines(notFoundPath, notFound);
                }
            }
            catch { }

            return results;
        }

        
        public static Dictionary<string, List<string>> FindRecordedPackage(
            string server,
            IEnumerable<string> asset_ids,
            string destinationFolder)
        {
            var results = new Dictionary<string, List<string>>();
            if (asset_ids == null) return results;

            Directory.CreateDirectory(destinationFolder);
            string temp_path = Path.GetTempPath();

            foreach (var asset_id in asset_ids)
            {
                var copiedForAsset = new List<string>();
                try
                {
                    var downloaded = DownloadFilesByRecordingStatus(server, asset_id, "recorded", temp_path)
                        .Where(f => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(f) && File.Exists(f))
                        .Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                        .ToList();

                    if (downloaded.Count > 0)
                    {
                        
                        
                        if (downloaded.Count == 2)
                        {
                            var disclosureFile = downloaded.FirstOrDefault(f =>
                                Path.GetFileName(f).IndexOf("Disclosure", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) >= 0);
                            if (disclosureFile != null)
                            {
                                var otherFile = downloaded.First(f => f != disclosureFile);
                                try { File.Delete(otherFile); } catch { }
                                downloaded = new List<string> { disclosureFile };
                            }
                        }

                        if (downloaded.Count == 1)
                        {
                            var file = downloaded[0];
                            string ext = Path.GetExtension(file);
                            string target = Path.Combine(destinationFolder, $"{asset_id}{ext}");

                            File.Copy(file, target, true);
                            copiedForAsset.Add(target);

                            try { File.Delete(file); } catch { }
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            string assetDir = Path.Combine(destinationFolder, asset_id);
                            Directory.CreateDirectory(assetDir);

                            foreach (var file in downloaded)
                            {
                                string fileName = Path.GetFileName(file);
                                string target = Path.Combine(assetDir, fileName);

                                if (File.Exists(target))
                                {
                                    string name = Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(fileName);
                                    string ext = Path.GetExtension(fileName);
                                    int idx = 1;
                                    while (File.Exists(target))
                                    {
                                        target = Path.Combine(assetDir, $"{name}_{idx}{ext}");
                                        idx++;
                                    }
                                }

                                File.Copy(file, target, true);
                                copiedForAsset.Add(target);

                                try { File.Delete(file); } catch { }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                catch
                {
                    
                }
                results[asset_id] = copiedForAsset;
            }

            
            try
            {
                var notFound = results.Where(kvp => kvp.Value == null || kvp.Value.Count == 0)
                                      .Select(kvp => kvp.Key)
                                      .ToList();
                if (notFound.Count > 0)
                {
                    string notFoundPath = Path.Combine(destinationFolder, "Assets_Not_Found.txt");
                    File.WriteAllLines(notFoundPath, notFound);
                }
            }
            catch { }

            return results;
        }

    }

using static CommonInterfaces.Constants;
namespace MaxDocVaultLib
{
    public class JWT
    {
        public string token { get; set; }
    }

    public class UserDocuments
    {
        public int id { get; set; }
        public string single_file { get; set; }
        public object deleted_at { get; set; }
        public DateTime created_at { get; set; }
        public DateTime modified_at { get; set; }
        public string uuid { get; set; }
        public object kind { get; set; }
        public string tag { get; set; }
        public string original_filename { get; set; }
        public int? size { get; set; }
        public bool customer_visible { get; set; }
        public object source { get; set; }
        public object type { get; set; }
        public object category { get; set; }
        public object document { get; set; }
        public object upload_finished_at { get; set; }
        public int application_profile { get; set; }
        public int? snapshot { get; set; }
        public string recording_status { get; set; }
    }

    public enum ErrorType
    {
        FileException = 0,
        FolderException = 1,
        InvalidCharacters = 2,
    }

    public class MaxDocVault
    {
        public static Configuration LoadConfigFile()
        {
            var configFile = "A:/03 - Applications/MaxLib/web.config";

            if (!File.Exists(configFile))
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Web Config File is missing!");
                return null;
            }
            else
            {
                var configMap = new ExeConfigurationFileMap { ExeConfigFilename = configFile };
                return ConfigurationManager.OpenMappedExeConfiguration(configMap, ConfigurationUserLevel.None);
            }
        }

        public static string GetToken()
        {
                string response = null;
                var appSettings = LoadConfigFile();
                var url = appSettings.AppSettings.Settings["token_url"].Value.ToString();
                var data = new NameValueCollection();
                data["username"] = appSettings.AppSettings.Settings["username"].Value.ToString();
                data["password"] = appSettings.AppSettings.Settings["password"].Value.ToString();

                using (var wb = new WebClient())
                {
                    byte[] response_bytes = wb.UploadValues(url, "POST", data);
                    response = System.Text.Encoding.UTF8.GetString(response_bytes);
                }

                JWT jwt = JsonConvert.DeserializeObject<JWT>(response);
                return jwt.token;
        }

        public static async void DownloadAllDocuments(string asset_id, string ap_id, string dest_folder)
        {
            string token = GetToken();
            string errorFile = Path.Combine(dest_folder, $"{asset_id}_ErrorLog.txt");
            var appSettings = LoadConfigFile();

            var client = new HttpClient();
            var httpRequestMessage = new HttpRequestMessage
            {
                Method = HttpMethod.Get,
                RequestUri = new Uri(String.Concat(appSettings.AppSettings.Settings["docvault_url"].Value, ap_id)),
                Headers = {
                    { HttpRequestHeader.Authorization.ToString(), "JWT " + token },
                    { HttpRequestHeader.ContentType.ToString(), "application/json" }
                }
            };

            var sendTask = client.SendAsync(httpRequestMessage, HttpCompletionOption.ResponseHeadersRead);
            var response = sendTask.Result.EnsureSuccessStatusCode();
            Stream httpStream = await response.Content.ReadAsStreamAsync();

            using (var sreader = new StreamReader(httpStream))
            {
                using (JsonTextReader jreader = new JsonTextReader(sreader))
                {
                    while (jreader.Read())
                    {
                        if (jreader.TokenType == JsonToken.StartObject)
                        {
                            
                            var userdoc = new JsonSerializer().Deserialize<UserDocuments>(jreader);
                            string base_name = userdoc.original_filename;

                            if (UtilsLib.FileLib.ContainsInvalidCharacters(base_name))
                            {
                                base_name = UtilsLib.Clean.CleanFilename(base_name, true);
                                AddToErrorLog(errorFile, ErrorType.InvalidCharacters, null, userdoc.original_filename, base_name, asset_id);
                            }

                            if (!UtilsLib.FileLib.ContainsInvalidCharacters(base_name)) 
                            {
                                switch (userdoc.tag)
                                {
                                    case null:
                                    case "null":
                                    case "":
                                        using (WebClient wc = new WebClient())
                                            try { wc.DownloadFile(userdoc.single_file, Path.Combine(dest_folder, base_name)); }
                                            catch (WebException ex)
                                            {
                                                if (ex.Status == WebExceptionStatus.ProtocolError && ex.Response != null)
                                                    AddToErrorLog(errorFile, ErrorType.FileException, ex.Message.ToString(), userdoc.original_filename, base_name, asset_id);
                                                continue;
                                            }
                                        break;
                                    case "Post-Closing Docs":
                                        Directory.CreateDirectory(Path.Combine(dest_folder, "Closing Docs - Fully Executed"));
                                        using (WebClient wc = new WebClient())
                                            try { wc.DownloadFile(userdoc.single_file, Path.Combine(dest_folder, "Closing Docs - Fully Executed", base_name)); }
                                            catch (WebException ex)
                                            {
                                                if (ex.Status == WebExceptionStatus.ProtocolError && ex.Response != null)
                                                    AddToErrorLog(errorFile, ErrorType.FileException, ex.Message.ToString(), userdoc.original_filename, base_name, asset_id);
                                                continue;
                                            }
                                        break;
                                    case "AVM Docs":
                                        Directory.CreateDirectory(Path.Combine(dest_folder, "AVM Docs"));
                                        using (WebClient wc = new WebClient())
                                            if (String.Compare(base_name, "bkfs") == 0)
                                            {
                                                try { wc.DownloadFile(userdoc.single_file, Path.Combine(dest_folder, "AVM Docs", "Black Knight - AVM.pdf")); }
                                                catch (WebException ex)
                                                {
                                                    if (ex.Status == WebExceptionStatus.ProtocolError && ex.Response != null)
                                                        AddToErrorLog(errorFile, ErrorType.FileException, ex.Message.ToString(), userdoc.original_filename, base_name, asset_id);
                                                    continue;
                                                }
                                            }
                                            else
                                            {
                                                try { wc.DownloadFile(userdoc.single_file, Path.Combine(dest_folder, userdoc.tag, userdoc.original_filename)); }
                                                catch (WebException ex)
                                                {
                                                    if (ex.Status == WebExceptionStatus.ProtocolError && ex.Response != null)
                                                        AddToErrorLog(errorFile, ErrorType.FileException, ex.Message.ToString(), userdoc.original_filename, base_name, asset_id);
                                                    continue;
                                                }
                                            }
                                        break;
                                    case "Deleted":
                                    case "Expired":
                                    case "Expired / Not Needed":
                                    case "Deal Files/Expired / Not Needed": break;
                                    default:
                                        try { Directory.CreateDirectory(Path.Combine(dest_folder, userdoc.tag)); }
                                        catch (ArgumentException ae)
                                        {
                                            AddToErrorLog(errorFile, ErrorType.FolderException, Path.Combine(dest_folder, userdoc.tag), base_name, null, asset_id);
                                            continue;
                                        }
                                        using (WebClient wc = new WebClient())
                                        try { wc.DownloadFile(userdoc.single_file, Path.Combine(dest_folder, userdoc.tag, userdoc.original_filename)); }
                                        catch (WebException ex)
                                        {
                                            if (ex.Status == WebExceptionStatus.ProtocolError && ex.Response != null)
                                                AddToErrorLog(errorFile, ErrorType.FileException, ex.Message.ToString(), userdoc.original_filename, base_name, asset_id);
                                            continue;
                                        }
                                        break;
                                }
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                AddToErrorLog(errorFile, ErrorType.InvalidCharacters, null, userdoc.original_filename, base_name, asset_id);
                                continue;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        public static async void DownloadAllDocuments(string asset_id, string ap_id, string dest_folder, string filetype_only)
        {
            string token = GetToken();
            string errorFile = Path.Combine(dest_folder, $"{asset_id}_ErrorLog.txt");
            var appSettings = LoadConfigFile();

            var client = new HttpClient();
            var httpRequestMessage = new HttpRequestMessage
            {
                Method = HttpMethod.Get,
                RequestUri = new Uri(String.Concat(appSettings.AppSettings.Settings["docvault_url"].Value, ap_id)),
                Headers = {
                    { HttpRequestHeader.Authorization.ToString(), "JWT " + token },
                    { HttpRequestHeader.ContentType.ToString(), "application/json" }
                }
            };

            var sendTask = client.SendAsync(httpRequestMessage, HttpCompletionOption.ResponseHeadersRead);
            var response = sendTask.Result.EnsureSuccessStatusCode();
            Stream httpStream = await response.Content.ReadAsStreamAsync();

            using (var sreader = new StreamReader(httpStream))
            {
                using (JsonTextReader jreader = new JsonTextReader(sreader))
                {
                    while (jreader.Read())
                    {
                        if (jreader.TokenType == JsonToken.StartObject)
                        {
                            
                            var userdoc = new JsonSerializer().Deserialize<UserDocuments>(jreader);
                            string base_name = userdoc.original_filename;


                            if (UtilsLib.FileLib.ContainsInvalidCharacters(base_name))
                            {
                                base_name = UtilsLib.Clean.CleanFilename(base_name, true, true);
                                AddToErrorLog(errorFile, ErrorType.InvalidCharacters, userdoc.original_filename, base_name, null, null);
                            }
                            if (String.Compare(Path.GetExtension(base_name), filetype_only, true) != 0)
                                continue;

                            if (!UtilsLib.FileLib.ContainsInvalidCharacters(base_name)) 
                            {
                                switch (userdoc.tag)
                                {
                                    case "Deleted":
                                    case "Expired":
                                    case "Expired / Not Needed":
                                    case "Deal Files/Expired / Not Needed": break;
                                    default:
                                        try { Directory.CreateDirectory(Path.Combine(dest_folder)); }
                                        catch (ArgumentException ae) { AddToErrorLog(errorFile, ErrorType.FolderException, Path.Combine(dest_folder, userdoc.tag), base_name, null, asset_id); }
                                        using (WebClient wc = new WebClient())
                                            try { wc.DownloadFile(userdoc.single_file, Path.Combine(dest_folder, String.Concat(asset_id, "_", base_name))); }
                                            catch (WebException ex)
                                            {
                                                if (ex.Status == WebExceptionStatus.ProtocolError && ex.Response != null)
                                                    AddToErrorLog(errorFile, ErrorType.FileException, ex.Message.ToString(), userdoc.original_filename, base_name, asset_id);
                                                continue;
                                            }
                                        break;
                                }
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                AddToErrorLog(Path.Combine(dest_folder, "FileDownloadError.txt"), ErrorType.InvalidCharacters, null, userdoc.original_filename, base_name, null);
                                continue;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        public static async void DownloadClosingStatement(string asset_id)
        {
            string token = GetToken();
            var client = new HttpClient();
            var httpRequestMessage = new HttpRequestMessage
            {
                Method = HttpMethod.Get,
                RequestUri = new Uri(string.Format("https:
                Headers = {
                    { HttpRequestHeader.Authorization.ToString(), "JWT " + token },
                    { HttpRequestHeader.ContentType.ToString(), "application/json" }
                }
            };
            try
            {
                var sendTask = client.SendAsync(httpRequestMessage, HttpCompletionOption.ResponseHeadersRead);
                var response = sendTask.Result.EnsureSuccessStatusCode();
                var httpStream = await response.Content.ReadAsStreamAsync();
                using (var fileStream = File.Create(string.Format("C:/temp/Disclosure - Closing Statement - {0} - {1}.pdf", asset_id, DateTime.Now.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd"))))
                {
                    httpStream.CopyTo(fileStream);
                    fileStream.Flush();
                }
            }
            catch (HttpRequestException ex) {
                AddToErrorLog($"C:/temp/ErrorLog_{DateTime.Now.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd")}.txt", ErrorType.FileException, ex.Message.ToString(), null, null, asset_id);
            }
        }

        public static async Task<bool> UpdateSubstageToPendingRecording(string asset_id)
        {
            string token = GetToken();
            var client = new HttpClient();
            bool result = false;

            var jsonContent = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(new Dictionary<string, string>
            {
                { "application_state", "pending-recording" },
            });

            var updateurl = new Uri(string.Format("https:
            var request = new HttpRequestMessage(new HttpMethod("PATCH"), updateurl);
            request.Headers.Authorization = new System.Net.Http.Headers.AuthenticationHeaderValue("JWT", token);
            request.Content = new StringContent(jsonContent, Encoding.UTF8, "application/json");
            var response = await client.SendAsync(request);
            if (response.IsSuccessStatusCode) result = true; else result = false;
            return result;
        }

        public static async Task<List<int>> SearchForDocument(string ap_id, string search_key)
        {
            string token = GetToken();
            List<int> files_found = new List<int>();
            var appSettings = LoadConfigFile();

            var client = new HttpClient();
            var httpRequestMessage = new HttpRequestMessage
            {
                Method = HttpMethod.Get,
                RequestUri = new Uri(String.Concat(appSettings.AppSettings.Settings["docvault_url"].Value, ap_id)),
                Headers = {
                    { HttpRequestHeader.Authorization.ToString(), "JWT " + token },
                    { HttpRequestHeader.ContentType.ToString(), "application/json" }
                }
            };

            var sendTask = client.SendAsync(httpRequestMessage, HttpCompletionOption.ResponseHeadersRead);
            var response = sendTask.Result.EnsureSuccessStatusCode();
            Stream httpStream = await response.Content.ReadAsStreamAsync();

            using (var sreader = new StreamReader(httpStream))
            {
                using (JsonTextReader jreader = new JsonTextReader(sreader))
                {
                    while (jreader.Read())
                    {
                        if (jreader.TokenType == JsonToken.StartObject)
                        {
                            
                            var userdoc = new JsonSerializer().Deserialize<UserDocuments>(jreader);
                            string base_name = userdoc.original_filename;
                            if (base_name?.IndexOf(search_key, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) >= 0)
                                files_found.Add(userdoc.id);                               
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            return files_found;
        }

        public static async Task<List<int>> SearchForDocumentByRecordingStatus(string ap_id, string recording_status)
        {
            string token = GetToken();
            List<int> files_found = new List<int>();
            var appSettings = LoadConfigFile();

            var client = new HttpClient();
            var httpRequestMessage = new HttpRequestMessage
            {
                Method = HttpMethod.Get,
                RequestUri = new Uri(String.Concat(appSettings.AppSettings.Settings["docvault_url"].Value, ap_id)),
                Headers = {
                    { HttpRequestHeader.Authorization.ToString(), "JWT " + token },
                    { HttpRequestHeader.ContentType.ToString(), "application/json" }
                }
            };

            var sendTask = client.SendAsync(httpRequestMessage, HttpCompletionOption.ResponseHeadersRead);
            var response = sendTask.Result.EnsureSuccessStatusCode();
            Stream httpStream = await response.Content.ReadAsStreamAsync();

            using (var sreader = new StreamReader(httpStream))
            {
                using (JsonTextReader jreader = new JsonTextReader(sreader))
                {
                    while (jreader.Read())
                    {
                        if (jreader.TokenType == JsonToken.StartObject)
                        {
                            var userdoc = new JsonSerializer().Deserialize<UserDocuments>(jreader);
                            if (string.Equals(userdoc.recording_status, recording_status, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                                files_found.Add(userdoc.id);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            return files_found;
        }

        public static async Task<string> DownloadByDocumentID(string ap_id, string dest_folder, int req_document_id)
        {
            System.Net.ServicePointManager.SecurityProtocol = System.Net.SecurityProtocolType.Tls12;
            string token = GetToken();
            string errorFile = Path.Combine(dest_folder, "FileDownloadError.txt");
            var appSettings = LoadConfigFile();
            string final_name = null;
            var client = new HttpClient();
            var httpRequestMessage = new HttpRequestMessage
            {
                Method = HttpMethod.Get,
                RequestUri = new Uri(String.Concat(appSettings.AppSettings.Settings["docvault_url"].Value, ap_id)),
                Headers = {
                    { HttpRequestHeader.Authorization.ToString(), "JWT " + token },
                    { HttpRequestHeader.ContentType.ToString(), "application/json" }
                }
            };

            var sendTask = client.SendAsync(httpRequestMessage, HttpCompletionOption.ResponseHeadersRead);
            var response = sendTask.Result.EnsureSuccessStatusCode();
            Stream httpStream = await response.Content.ReadAsStreamAsync();

            using (var sreader = new StreamReader(httpStream))
            {
                using (JsonTextReader jreader = new JsonTextReader(sreader))
                {
                    while (jreader.Read())
                    {
                        if (jreader.TokenType == JsonToken.StartObject)
                        {
                            
                            var userdoc = new JsonSerializer().Deserialize<UserDocuments>(jreader);
                            int document_id = userdoc.id;
                            if (document_id == req_document_id)
                            {
                                string base_name = userdoc.original_filename;
                                if (UtilsLib.FileLib.ContainsInvalidCharacters(base_name))
                                {
                                    base_name = UtilsLib.Clean.CleanFilename(base_name, true);
                                    AddToErrorLog(errorFile, ErrorType.InvalidCharacters, null, userdoc.original_filename, base_name, null);

                                    using (StreamWriter writer = new StreamWriter(errorFile, true))
                                        writer.WriteLine($"{DateTime.Now.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss")} - The file named: ", userdoc.original_filename, " was changed to ", base_name, " due to invalid characters in the filename.");
                                }
                                if (!UtilsLib.FileLib.ContainsInvalidCharacters(base_name)) 
                                {
                                    using (WebClient wc = new WebClient())
                                        try 
                                        {
                                            final_name = Path.Combine(dest_folder, base_name);
                                            wc.DownloadFile(userdoc.single_file, final_name); 
                                        }
                                        catch (WebException ex)
                                        {
                                            if (ex.Status == WebExceptionStatus.ProtocolError && ex.Response != null)
                                                AddToErrorLog(errorFile, ErrorType.FileException, ex.Message.ToString(), userdoc.original_filename, base_name, null);
                                            continue;
                                        }
                                    break;
                                }
                                else
                                {
                                    AddToErrorLog(errorFile, ErrorType.InvalidCharacters, null, userdoc.original_filename, base_name, null);
                                    continue;
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            return final_name;
        }

        public static void AddToErrorLog(string error_file, ErrorType error, string exception, string problem_file, string base_name, string asset_id)
        {            
            switch (error)
            {
                case ErrorType.InvalidCharacters:
                    using (StreamWriter writer = new StreamWriter(error_file, true))
                        writer.WriteLine($"{DateTime.Now}{(asset_id.IsNullOrEmpty() ? "" : " - " + asset_id)} - The file named: {problem_file} was changed to {base_name} due to invalid characters in the filename.");
                    break;
                case ErrorType.FileException:
                    using (StreamWriter writer = new StreamWriter(error_file, true))
                    {
                        writer.WriteLine($"{DateTime.Now}{(asset_id.IsNullOrEmpty() ? "" : " - " + asset_id)} - The file named: {problem_file} could not be downloaded due to the following exception:");
                        writer.WriteLine(exception);
                    }
                    break;
                case ErrorType.FolderException:
                    using (StreamWriter writer = new StreamWriter(error_file, true))
                    {
                        writer.WriteLine($"{DateTime.Now}{(asset_id.IsNullOrEmpty() ? "" : " - " + asset_id)} - The folder named: {problem_file} could not be created due to the following exception:");
                        writer.WriteLine(exception);
                    }
                    break;
            }
        }

        public static async void UploadDocument(string ap_id)
        {
            var token = GetToken();
            var client = new HttpClient();
            
            

            MultipartFormDataContent content = new MultipartFormDataContent();

            

            StreamContent streamContent = new StreamContent(new FileStream(@"C:\temp\test2.pdf", FileMode.Open, FileAccess.Read));
            var fileContent = new ByteArrayContent(streamContent.ReadAsByteArrayAsync().Result);

            

            var dict = new Dictionary<string, string>
            {
                { "application_profile", ap_id },
                { "tag", "z-Raw Data" },
                { "single_file", fileContent.ReadAsStringAsync().Result }
            };

            var json = Newtonsoft.Json.JsonConvert.SerializeObject(dict);
            File.WriteAllText(@"C:\temp\test.json", json.ToString());
            var httpContent = new StringContent(json, Encoding.ASCII, "application/json");
            content.Add(httpContent);
            var httpClient = new HttpClient();
            httpClient.DefaultRequestHeaders.TryAddWithoutValidation("Content-Type", "application/json");
            httpClient.DefaultRequestHeaders.TryAddWithoutValidation("Authorization", "JWT " + token);

            var httpRequestMessage = new HttpRequestMessage
            {
                Method = HttpMethod.Post,
                RequestUri = new Uri(string.Format("https:
                Headers = {
                    { HttpRequestHeader.Authorization.ToString(), "JWT " + token },
                    { HttpRequestHeader.ContentType.ToString(), "application/json" }
                },
                Content = content
            };

            
            
            

            var response = httpClient.PostAsJsonAsync("https:
            Console.WriteLine(response);
        }

	, INTEREST_RATE AS RATE
	, UNPAID_BALANCE_AMOUNT AS BALANCE
	, LIEN_POSITION

	, T.NAME AS LENDER_LOOKUP

FROM

	, MORTGAGE_PRODUCT_TYPE AS DEBTTYPE_LOOKUP
	, INTEREST_RATE AS RATE
	, UNPAID_BALANCE_AMOUNT AS BALANCE

	, concat('''',CAST(ACCOUNT_OPENED_ON AS varchar(30))) AS ACCOUNT_OPEN_DATE

	, T.NAME AS LENDER_LOOKUP
	, EXTERNAL_ID as ASSET_ID
	, coalesce(MONTHLY_PAYMENT_AMOUNT,MONTHLY_PAYMENT_AMOUNT_CALCULATED) as PAYMENT

WHERE 
	EXTERNAL_ID = @asset_id


--- FILE: MaxLib\SQL\Max_Get_Payoffs.sql ---
SELECT app.EXTERNAL_ID, sum(case when expense.name = 'Concession' then -1.0 else 1.0 end * amount) AS FEES_PAID_BY_UNLOCK
FROM raw.fivetran_maxapp_max_prod_public.api_application app
LEFT JOIN raw.fivetran_maxapp_max_prod_public.api_expense expense ON app.ID =expense.APPLICATION_ID
WHERE app.EXTERNAL_ID = @max_id
AND (expense._FIVETRAN_DELETED IS NULL and expense.deleted_at is null and paid_to is not null)
AND paid_to not in ('clear_capital') 
and ((expense.name in ('Concession','Appraisal Cost','Appraisal  Cost','BPO','Appraisal Fee','Appraisal')) or (expense.name = 'Concession' and expense.paid_to is null))
GROUP BY app.EXTERNAL_ID


--- FILE: MaxLib\SQL\Max_Overrides.sql ---
SELECT (OVERRIDES.EXCHANGE_RATE + OVERRIDES.EXCHANGE_RATE_ADJUSTMENT) AS EXCHANGE_RATE_ADJ
FROM raw.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.api_application app
LEFT JOIN RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_OVERRIDES OVERRIDES ON app.ID  =OVERRIDES.APPLICATION_ID  
WHERE app.DELETED_AT IS NULL 
and app.EXTERNAL_ID = @max_id


--- FILE: MaxLib\SQL\MAX_Referral_Emails.sql ---
select 'old' AS 'schema', referral.EMAIL AS referral_email, referral.name AS referral_name
FROM raw.FIVETRAN_MAXAPP_MAX_PROD_PUBLIC.api_application app
left join raw.FIVETRAN_MAXAPP_MAX_PROD_PUBLIC.API_APPLICATIONPARTY ap on ap.application_id = app.id  AND APPLICATION_PARTY_TYPE = 'party'
left join raw.FIVETRAN_MAXAPP_MAX_PROD_PUBLIC.api_party  as referral on ap.party_id = referral.id AND referral.DELETED_AT IS NULL 
WHERE app.EXTERNAL_ID = @max_id
UNION 
select 'new' AS 'schema', referral.EMAIL AS referral_email, referral.name AS referral_name
FROM raw.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.api_application app
left join raw.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_APPLICATIONPARTY ap on ap.application_id = app.id  AND APPLICATION_PARTY_TYPE = 'party'
left join raw.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.api_party  as referral on ap.party_id = referral.id AND referral.DELETED_AT IS NULL 
WHERE app.EXTERNAL_ID = @max_id


--- FILE: MaxLib\SQL\Max_Referral_Info.sql ---
SELECT referral.EMAIL, REFERRAL.NAME
FROM raw.fivetran_maxapp_max_prod_public.api_application app
left join RAW.FIVETRAN_MAXAPP_MAX_PROD_PUBLIC.API_APPLICATIONPARTY ap on ap.application_id = app.id AND APPLICATION_PARTY_TYPE = 'party'
left join raw.fivetran_maxapp_max_prod_public.api_party as referral on ap.PARTY_ID  = referral.id AND referral.DELETED_AT IS NULL AND referral._FIVETRAN_DELETED IS NULL
WHERE app.EXTERNAL_ID = @max_id


--- FILE: MaxLib\Utils.cs ---
namespace MaxLib
{
    public static class Utils
    {

        public static void AddToBadgerGraphQL(string server, string max_id, string user_name)
        {
            string access_token = GraphQLProgram.GetAccessTokenAsync(Constants.GQL.username, Constants.GQL.password).Result;
            GraphQLProgram programInstance = new GraphQLProgram(access_token);
            RunMaxSPAll runMaxSPAll = new RunMaxSPAll(programInstance._client);

            List<string> assetIds = new List<string> { max_id };
            runMaxSPAll.ProcessAssetsAsync(assetIds).Wait();
        }

        public static DataTable AddToBadger(string server, string max_id, string user_name)
        {
            string sql = "sp_MAX_Badger_Import_All @max_id, @p_UserName";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@max_id", max_id);
            q.AddParameter("@p_UserName", user_name);
            DataTable sp_MAX_Badger_Import_All_dt = q.ExecuteTable();
            return sp_MAX_Badger_Import_All_dt;
        }

        public static void AddSecondToBadger(string server, string max_id, string user_name, bool add_asset, bool ignore_applicant = true)
        {
            string sql;
            Query q;
            if (add_asset)
            {
                sql = "exec sp_MAX_Badger_Import_Asset_Table @max_id, @p_UserName";
                q = new Query(sql, server);
                q.AddParameter("@max_id", max_id);
                q.AddParameter("@p_UserName", user_name);
                q.Execute();
            }

            sql = "exec sp_MAX_Badger_Import_All @max_id, @p_UserName,@p_IgnoreApplicantCheck";
            q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@max_id", max_id);
            q.AddParameter("@p_UserName", user_name);
            q.AddParameter ("@p_IgnoreApplicantCheck", ignore_applicant);
            q.Execute();

            sql = "exec sp_MAX_Badger_Import_Closing @max_id";
            q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@max_id", max_id);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public static bool IsMaxId(string max_id)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(max_id))
                return false;
            double d;
            if (max_id.Length == 14 && Double.TryParse(max_id, out d))
            {
                return true;
            }
            return false;
        }
        public static DataTable GetReferralInformation(string server, string max_id)
        {
            string sql = "select pipe.Max_id, pipe.opp_source_email, pipe.opp_source_txt, pipe.partner_account_txt, commission, pipe.investment_payment,";
            sql += " round(ISNULL(commission,0)*ISNULL(pipe.investment_payment,0),2) as FINDERS_FEE";
            sql += " from vPipeline pipe left join ReferralCommissionInfo commission on commission.email_full = pipe.opp_source_email";
            sql += " where pipe.Max_id  = @max_id";

            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@max_id", max_id);
            DataTable results = q.ExecuteTable();
            return results;

        }
        public static DataTable GetMaxApplicationStateChangesForToday(string server)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT ID, EXTERNAL_ID, APPLICATION_STATE_MODIFIED_AT , APPLICATION_STATE FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_APPLICATION app";
            sql += " WHERE app.APPLICATION_STATE_MODIFIED_AT  >= CURRENT_DATE()";
            
            sql += " AND APPLICATION_STATE  in('pending-final-approval-uw', 'pending-final-terms', 'pending-ics-signature', 'pending-final-approval-uam', 'pending-ics-delivery', 'pending-doc-draw', 'pending-signature', 'pending-ics-signature', 'pending-recording', 'pending-escrow-disbursement')";

            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            DataTable results = q.ExecuteTable();
            return results;
        }
        

        public static DataTable UpdateBadgerApplicationState_new(DataTable dt, string server)
        {
            
            dt.Columns.Add("Message", typeof(string));
            dt.Columns.Add("APPLICATION_STATE_Prior", typeof(string));
            dt.Columns.Add("Has_Changed", typeof(string));
            dt.Columns.Add("Name", typeof(string));
            


            string sql, new_state, app_id, external_id;
            foreach (DataRow row in dt.Rows)
            {
                app_id = row["id"].ToString();
                new_state = row["APPLICATION_STATE"].ToString();
                sql = "exec sp_MAX_Badger_IntraDay_Application_Status_Update @app_id, @new_state";
                Query q = new Query(sql, server);
                q.AddParameter("@app_id", app_id);
                q.AddParameter("@new_state", new_state);
                DataTable tmpresults = q.ExecuteTable();
                row["Message"] = tmpresults.Rows[0]["Message"].ToString();
                row["APPLICATION_STATE_Prior"] = tmpresults.Rows[0]["APPLICATION_STATE_Prior"].ToString();
                row["Has_Changed"] = tmpresults.Rows[0]["Has_Changed"].ToString();
                row["Name"] = tmpresults.Rows[0]["Name"].ToString();
            }

            return dt;
        }

        public static void UpdateBadgerApplicationState(DataTable dt, string server)
        {
            string sql, new_state, app_id;
            foreach (DataRow row in dt.Rows)
            {
                app_id = row["id"].ToString();
                new_state = row["APPLICATION_STATE"].ToString();
                if (new_state.Trim().Length > 0)
                {
                    sql = "update API_APPLICATION set APPLICATION_STATE = @new_state, APPLICATION_STATE_MODIFIED_AT = dbo.GetDateNY() where id = @app_id";
                    Query q = new Query(sql, server);
                    q.AddParameter("@app_id", app_id);
                    q.AddParameter("@new_state", new_state);
                    DataTable tmpresults = q.ExecuteTable();

                }

            }

        }

        public static void MaxSync_API_XXXX_By_Max_ID(string ID_Value, string SourceTbl, string DestTbl, string keyColumnName, string colList, string SnowFlakeServer, string SQLServer)
        {
            StringBuilder SQL_Str_Delete = new StringBuilder();
            SQL_Str_Delete.AppendFormat("delete from {0} where {1} = @ID_Value", DestTbl, keyColumnName);

            Query q_DeleteFromBadger = new Query(SQL_Str_Delete.ToString(), SQLServer);
            q_DeleteFromBadger.AddParameter("@ID_Value", ID_Value);
            DataTable dt = q_DeleteFromBadger.ExecuteTable();

            StringBuilder SQL_Str_SnowFlake = new StringBuilder();
            SQL_Str_SnowFlake.AppendFormat("select {0} from {1} where {2} = @ID_Value", colList, SourceTbl, keyColumnName);

            Query q_SnowFlake = new Query(SQL_Str_SnowFlake.ToString(), SnowFlakeServer);
            q_SnowFlake.AddParameter("@ID_Value", ID_Value);
            DataTable tbl = q_SnowFlake.ExecuteTable();

            List<Query> insert_statements = Database.DBUtils.GenerateInsertStatements(DestTbl, tbl, true).inserts_all;
            insert_statements.ForEach(n => n.SetConnection(SQLServer));
            Query.BulkExecute(insert_statements);
        }

namespace BankLib
{
    public class Accounts
    {
        public static bool AccountExists(string server,int bankacct_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vBankAccts b where bankacct_id = @bankacct_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@bankacct_id", bankacct_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count > 0;      
        }

        public static DateTime LastUpdated(string server, int bankacct_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vBankAccts b where bankacct_id = @bankacct_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@bankacct_id", bankacct_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<DateTime>("balance_date");
        }

        public static DataTable GetAllAccounts(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vBankAccts order by abs(balance) desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static double GetUnlockBankBalance(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select sum(balance) from vBankAccts where is_unlock=1";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<double>();
        }


        public static DateTime GetUnlockEarliestLoad(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select min(balance_date) from vBankAccts where is_unlock=1";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<DateTime>();
        }


        public static double GetBalance(string server, int bankacct_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vBankAccts b where bankacct_id = @bankacct_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@bankacct_id", bankacct_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<double>("balance");
        }


        public static void CreateAccount(string server,int bankacct_id, string name)
        {
            string sql = "insert into BankAccts (id,name) values (@bankacct_id,@name)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@bankacct_id", bankacct_id);
            q.AddParameter("@name", name);
            q.Execute();
        }
        public static void UpdateBalance(string server, int bankacct_id,decimal balance,DateTime asOf)
        {
            string sql = "update BankAccts set buxfer_balance=@balance, buxfer_date = @asOf where id = @bankacct_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@bankacct_id", bankacct_id);
            q.AddParameter("@balance", balance);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.Execute();
        }
    }

--- FILE: BankLib\BankActivity.cs ---
namespace BankLib
{
    public static class BankActivity
    {

        

        public static int? GetBankAccountId(string server, string account_number)
        {
            account_number = account_number.ToUpper();
            string sql = $"select id from dbo.BankAccts b where UPPER(b.acct_num) = '{account_number}'";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int?>();
        }

        public static int? GetBankTransactionTypeId(string server, string transactionType)
        {
            transactionType = transactionType.ToUpper();
            string sql = $"select top 1 id from BankActivityTransactionTypes where upper(transaction_type) ='{transactionType}'" +
                $"or UPPER(transaction_type_alternate_name_list) like '%{transactionType}' ";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int?>();
        }

        public static int? GetBankActivityID(string server, int account_id, double amount, bool latest)
        {
            string sql = $"select {(latest ? "max(id)" : "id")} from dbo.BankActivity b where b.account_id = '{account_id}' and b.amount = {amount}";
            Query query = new Query(sql, server);
            return query.ExecuteSingle<int?>();
        }

        public static int CreateNewLoadIdGeneric(string server, DateTime? asOf, int loadtype_id, string file_name, string file_type, string info, DateTime last_write_time)
        {
            string sql = "insert into BankActivityLoads (asOf,file_name,file_type,info,loadtype_id,last_write_time) output inserted.id values (@asOf,@file_name, @file_type, @info,@loadtype_id,@last_write_time)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.AddParameter("@file_name", file_name);
            q.AddParameter("@file_type", file_type);
            q.AddParameter("@info", info);
            q.AddParameter("@loadtype_id", loadtype_id);
            q.AddParameter("@last_write_time", last_write_time);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int>("id");
        }

        public static void InsertBankActivityLoad(string server, int loadId, DateTime? loadTime, DateTime? fileCreateDate, int? rowCount, string fileName)
        {
            string sql = "insert into BankActivityLoads (id,load_time,file_create_date, row_count,file_name)  values (@load_id, @load_time,@file_create_date, @row_count,@file_name)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            
            q.AddParameter("@load_id", loadId);
            q.AddParameter("@load_time", loadTime);
            q.AddParameter("@file_create_date", fileCreateDate);
            q.AddParameter("@row_count", rowCount);
            q.AddParameter("@file_name", fileName);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public static void InsertBankActivity(string server, int load_id, DateTime transaction_date, int account_id,
            int transaction_type_id, double amount, string description, string  supplementary_details, string note, DateTime update_time, string update_by)
        {
            string sql = "insert into BankActivity (load_id, transaction_date, account_id, transaction_type_id, amount, description, supplementary_details, note, update_time,update_by) "
                + " values (@load_id, @transaction_date, @account_id, @transaction_type_id, @amount, @description, @supplementary_details, @note, @update_time, @update_by)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            
            q.AddParameter("@load_id", load_id);
            q.AddParameter("@transaction_date", transaction_date);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@transaction_type_id", transaction_type_id);                
            q.AddParameter("@amount", amount);
            q.AddParameter("@description", description);
            q.AddParameter("@supplementary_details", supplementary_details);
            q.AddParameter("@note", note);
            q.AddParameter("@update_time", update_time);
            q.AddParameter("@update_by", update_by);
            q.Execute();
        }
    }

--- FILE: BankLib\Loader.cs ---
namespace BankLib
{
    public class Loader
    {
        BuxferClient _client = null;

        public Loader(string user,string pass)
        {
            _client = new BuxferClient(user, pass);
        }


        public bool StartLoad(string server,string mail_profile,string notify,string post_cmd)
        {
            var accounts = _client.GetAccounts().Result;

            int updated = 0;
            bool updated_something = false;

            double old_balance = 0;
            double new_balance = 0;
            foreach (var account in accounts)
            {
                string msg = $"Account Name: {account.Name} - ${account.Balance:0,###}";
                Console.WriteLine(msg);


                DateTime? db_last_updated = null;


                DateTime last_updated = account.LastSynced.Value.AddHours(3);
                old_balance += BankLib.Accounts.GetBalance(server, account.Id);
                if (null == db_last_updated && last_updated > db_last_updated)
                {
                    updated_something = true;
                }

                BankLib.Accounts.UpdateBalance(server, account.Id, account.Balance, last_updated);
                new_balance += System.Convert.ToDouble(account.Balance);
                
                {
                    bool exists = BankLib.Accounts.AccountExists(server, account.Id);
                    if (!exists)
                    {
                        BankLib.Accounts.CreateAccount(server, account.Id, account.Name);
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        db_last_updated = BankLib.Accounts.LastUpdated(server, account.Id);
                    }
                    
                }
            }


            int total_days = 14;
            
            DateTime first_date = DateTime.Today;
            for (int i = 0; i != total_days; i++)
            {
                TransactionFilter f = new TransactionFilter();
                
                
                f.StartDate = first_date.AddDays(-i-1);
                f.EndDate = f.StartDate.Value.AddDays(+1);
                
                
                if (f.EndDate.Value > DateTime.Today)
                    continue;

                
                Console.WriteLine($"Processing: {f.EndDate.Value:M/d/yyyy}");
                

                var transactions = _client.GetTransactions(f).Result;
                

                List<int> processed_accounts = new List<int>();
  
                foreach (Transaction trans in transactions.Entities)
                
                {



                    string trans_str = $"{trans.Date:M/d/yyyy} ${trans.Amount:#,##0} - {trans.Description}";
                    Console.WriteLine(trans_str);
                    if(trans.Description.ToUpper().Contains("O3All".ToUpper()))
                    {

                    }
                    if(trans.Id == 164605978 || trans.Id == 164905925)
                    {

                    }
                    bool trans_exist = BankLib.Transactions.TransactionExists(server, trans.Id);
                    bool trans_exist_ignore = BankLib.Transactions.TransactionIgnoredExists(server, trans.Id);
                    if (!trans_exist && !trans_exist_ignore)
                    {
                        updated++;
                        BankLib.Transactions.InsertTransaction(server, trans.Id, trans.AccountId, trans.Date, trans.Amount, trans.Description, trans.IsPending, trans.Status.ToString(), trans.Type.ToString(),null);
                    }
                }
            }


            if (Math.Abs(updated) > 1 || updated_something)
            {
                updated_something = true;
                Console.WriteLine("Processing Transactions...");
                BankLib.Transactions.ProcessBankTrans(server);
                Console.WriteLine("All Done!");
                Mail m = new Mail(mail_profile);
                double change = new_balance - old_balance;
                DataTable transactions = BankLib.Transactions.GetTransactionsSingleDate(server, DateTime.Today);
                List<IFormatHelper> t = Database.RRHelper.GetFormats(server);
                string html_body = HTMLUtils.ToHtml(transactions, t);
                m.SendSMTPMail(notify, null, null, $"Bank Accounts Updated (OLD: {old_balance / 1000.0:0}k / NEW: {new_balance / 1000.0:0}k) | NET CHANGE: {change / 1000.0:0}k", html_body, null, true, true, null, MailPriority.Normal);
                if (null != post_cmd)
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Processing: {post_cmd}");
                    UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.StartProcess(post_cmd, null);
                    
                }

            }

            return updated_something;

        }
    }
}


--- FILE: BankLib\MondayHelper.cs ---
namespace BankLib
{
    public class MondayHelper
    {
        public static void UpdatePipeline(List<long> pipelines)
        {

            
            {
                
                var monday = new MondayLib.MondayHelper(MondayLib.CONSTANTS.Boards.PIPELINE, MondayLib.CONSTANTS.API_KEY, null);
                
                
                foreach (long pipeline in pipelines)
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Syncing: {pipeline}");
                    
                    var result = monday._client.GetItem(pipeline).Result;

                    
                    if (result.ColumnValues.Where(n => n.Id == "status3").Single().ValueText == "Pending Escrow Disbursement")
                    {
                        monday.UpdateBoardDropdown(MondayLib.CONSTANTS.Boards.PIPELINE, pipeline, "status3", 18);
                    }
                }

            }
        }
    }
}
