namespace BankLib
{
    public static class Transactions
    {
        public static bool TransactionExists(string server,int banktrans_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vBankTrans b where b.banktrans_id = @banktrans_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@banktrans_id", banktrans_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count > 0;
        }
 
        public static bool TransactionIgnoredExists(string server, int banktrans_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vBankTransSupp b where b.banktrans_id = @banktrans_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@banktrans_id", banktrans_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count > 0;
        }

        public static DataTable GetTransactionsSingleDate(string server, DateTime date)
        {
            string sql = "select b.nice_name,date,amount,descr,is_pending,status,type,net_amount from vBankTransEx b  where b.date = @date";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@date", date);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable FindTransactions(string server, double net_amount,double fuzzy,long? bankacct_id)
        {
            string sql = "select b.banktrans_id,b.nice_name [acct],date,amount,descr,is_pending,status,type,net_amount,convert(bit,case when abs(net_amount) = @net_amount then 1 else 0 end) [exact_match] from vBankTransEx b  where (abs(net_amount) = @net_amount or abs(net_amount) between @net_amount-@fuzzy and @net_amount+@fuzzy) and (@bankacct_id is null or bankacct_id = @bankacct_id)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@net_amount", net_amount);
            q.AddParameter("@fuzzy", fuzzy);
            q.AddParameter("@bankacct_id", bankacct_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetAllTransactions(string server)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT * FROM vBankTransEx order by date desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }
        public static DataTable GetAllFRBTransactions(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select frbinv_id,a.account_number,transaction_date,amount,transaction_description,null [is_pending],net_amount,a.nice_name,is_unlock from vFRBInvEx t join vBankAccts a on t.account_number = a.account_number where t.transaction_date >= dateadd(m,-1,GetDate()) order by transaction_date desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static void ProcessBankTrans(string server)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.ProcessBankTrans";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.Execute();
        }
        public static void InsertTransaction(string server,int banktrans_id, int bankacct_id, DateTime date,decimal amount,string descr, bool is_pending,string status,string type,int? to_account_id)
        {
            string sql = "insert into BankTrans (id,bankacct_id,date,amount,descr,is_pending,status,type,to_account_id) values (@banktrans_id,@bankacct_id,@date,@amount,@descr,@is_pending,@status,@type,@to_account_id)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@banktrans_id", banktrans_id);
            q.AddParameter("@bankacct_id", bankacct_id);
            q.AddParameter("@date", date);
            q.AddParameter("@amount", amount);
            q.AddParameter("@descr", descr);
            q.AddParameter("@is_pending", is_pending);
            q.AddParameter("@status", status);
            q.AddParameter("@type", type);
            q.AddParameter("@to_account_id", to_account_id);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public static DataTable GetIncomingSGTransactions(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select banktrans_id, [date], amount, descr, is_pending, status from vBankTransEx where (descr like '%INCOMING WIRE SALUDA GD ALT LN T R%' or descr like '%Saluda Gd Alt Ln Tr 21-1%' or descr like '%Sgtc Hei Asset Fun%')";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }
    }

namespace MTSettlementTransLib
{
    public interface ISettlementRepository
    {
        List<int> GetUnprocessedSettlementIds();
        SettlementDetail GetSettlementDetail(int settlementId);
        string GetAccountGuid(string accountName);
        void EnsureBookTypeExists();
        int CreateLoad(System.DateTime loadTime, string csvPath, string assetIds, bool latest = true);
        void InsertTransaction(int loadId, MTSettlementTransRow row);
        void UpdateLoadFilePath(int loadId, string csvPath);

--- FILE: MTSettlementTransLib\Loads.cs ---
namespace MTSettlementTransLib
{
    internal static class Loads
    {
        internal const string LoadType = "MTSettlementTransLoads";
        internal static int CreateNewLoadId(string server, DateTime createdAt,
            string source, string csvPath)
        {
            int loadId = Common.GetNextId(server, LoadType);

            string sql =
                "INSERT INTO MTSettlementTransLoads (load_id, created_at, source, path) " +
                "VALUES (@load_id, @created_at, @source, @path)";

            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@load_id", loadId);
            q.AddParameter("@created_at", createdAt);
            q.AddParameter("@source", source);
            q.AddParameter("@path", string.IsNullOrEmpty(csvPath) ? (object)DBNull.Value : csvPath);
            q.Execute();

            return loadId;
        }
        internal static bool LoadExists(string server, int loadId)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT load_id FROM MTSettlementTransLoads WHERE load_id = @load_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@load_id", loadId);
            return q.RecordExists();
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: MTSettlementTransLib\MTSettlementTransConfig.cs ---
namespace MTSettlementTransLib
{
    public class MTSettlementTransConfig
    {
        public string OutputRootFolder { get; set; }
        public int? BatchSize { get; set; }
        public bool DryRun { get; set; }
        public string Server { get; set; }

        public void Validate()
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(Server))
                throw new InvalidOperationException("MTSettlementTransConfig.Server must be set.");
            if (!DryRun && string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(OutputRootFolder))
                throw new InvalidOperationException("MTSettlementTransConfig.OutputRootFolder must be set when DryRun is false.");
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: MTSettlementTransLib\MTSettlementTransProcessor.cs ---
namespace MTSettlementTransLib
{
    public class MTSettlementTransProcessor
    {
        private static readonly ILog Log =
            LogManager.GetLogger(typeof(MTSettlementTransProcessor));

        private const string UnlockAccountName = "UAM Omnibus Collections";
        private const string WsfAccountName    = "WSFS Collections";
        private const string RefundAccountName = "UAM Customer Refund";
        private const string SGLT8Collections   = "SGLT8 Collections";
        private const string WireTypeName      = "Wire";
        private const string BookTypeName      = "Book";
        private const string FixedDirection    = "Credit";

        private readonly MTSettlementTransConfig _config;
        private readonly ISettlementRepository  _repo;

        
        public MTSettlementTransProcessor(MTSettlementTransConfig config)
            : this(config, new SettlementRepository(config.Server)) { }
        public MTSettlementTransProcessor(MTSettlementTransConfig config,
            ISettlementRepository repo)
        {
            _config = config ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(config));
            _repo   = repo   ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(repo));
        }

        
        public ProcessResult ProcessNewSettlements()
        {
            _config.Validate();

            Log.Info("MTSettlementTrans processing started.");

            
            if (!_config.DryRun)
                _repo.EnsureBookTypeExists();

            
            string unlockGuid = _repo.GetAccountGuid(UnlockAccountName);
            string wsfsGuid   = _repo.GetAccountGuid(WsfAccountName);
            string refundGuid = _repo.GetAccountGuid(RefundAccountName);
            string sglt8Guid  = _repo.GetAccountGuid(SGLT8Collections);

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(unlockGuid))
                throw new InvalidOperationException(
                    $"No AccountGuid found in MTSettlementAccounts for '{UnlockAccountName}'. " +
                    "Cannot proceed without a valid originating account.");

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(wsfsGuid))
                throw new InvalidOperationException(
                    $"No AccountGuid found in MTSettlementAccounts for '{WsfAccountName}'. " +
                    "Cannot proceed without a valid counterparty account.");

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(refundGuid))
                throw new InvalidOperationException(
                    $"No AccountGuid found in MTSettlementAccounts for '{RefundAccountName}'. " +
                    "Cannot proceed without a valid refund counterparty account.");

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(sglt8Guid))
                throw new InvalidOperationException(
                    $"No AccountGuid found in MTSettlementAccounts for '{SGLT8Collections}'. " +
                    "Cannot proceed without a valid SGLT-8 counterparty account.");

            
            List<int> settlementIds = _repo.GetUnprocessedSettlementIds();
            List<int> partialPaymentIds = _repo.GetUnprocessedPartialPaymentIds();
            int totalScanned = settlementIds.Count;
            int partialPaymentsScanned = partialPaymentIds.Count;

            if (_config.BatchSize.HasValue && settlementIds.Count > _config.BatchSize.Value)
                settlementIds = settlementIds.GetRange(0, _config.BatchSize.Value);

            if (_config.BatchSize.HasValue && partialPaymentIds.Count > _config.BatchSize.Value)
                partialPaymentIds = partialPaymentIds.GetRange(0, _config.BatchSize.Value);

            Log.Info($"Settlements scanned: {totalScanned}  |  to process this run: {settlementIds.Count}");
            Log.Info($"Partial payments scanned: {partialPaymentsScanned}  |  to process this run: {partialPaymentIds.Count}");

            if (settlementIds.Count == 0 && partialPaymentIds.Count == 0)
            {
                Log.Info("No unprocessed settlements or partial payments found. Exiting.");
                return new ProcessResult 
                { 
                    TotalScanned = totalScanned,
                    PartialPaymentsScanned = partialPaymentsScanned
                };
            }

            
            var allRows            = new List<MTSettlementTransRow>();
            var skippedIds         = new List<int>();
            var skippedPartialPaymentIds = new List<int>();
            var eligibleAssetIds   = new List<string>();

            foreach (int sid in settlementIds)
            {
                SettlementDetail detail = _repo.GetSettlementDetail(sid);
                if (detail == null)
                {
                    Log.Warn($"  Settlement {sid}: no detail found in vSettlementsEx — skipping.");
                    skippedIds.Add(sid);
                    continue;
                }

                if (!ValidateAmounts(sid, detail))
                {
                    skippedIds.Add(sid);
                    continue;
                }

                List<MTSettlementTransRow> rows = BuildRows(sid, detail,
                    unlockGuid, wsfsGuid, refundGuid, sglt8Guid);
                allRows.AddRange(rows);

                
                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(detail.AssetId))
                    eligibleAssetIds.Add(detail.AssetId);
            }

            
            foreach (int ppid in partialPaymentIds)
            {
                PartialPaymentDetail detail = _repo.GetPartialPaymentDetail(ppid);
                if (detail == null)
                {
                    Log.Warn($"  PartialPayment {ppid}: no detail found in vPartialPayments — skipping.");
                    skippedPartialPaymentIds.Add(ppid);
                    continue;
                }

                if (!ValidatePartialPaymentAmount(ppid, detail))
                {
                    skippedPartialPaymentIds.Add(ppid);
                    continue;
                }

                MTSettlementTransRow row = BuildPartialPaymentRow(ppid, detail,
                    unlockGuid, wsfsGuid, sglt8Guid);
                allRows.Add(row);

                
                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(detail.AssetId))
                    eligibleAssetIds.Add(detail.AssetId);
            }

            int eligibleCount = settlementIds.Count - skippedIds.Count;
            int eligiblePartialPayments = partialPaymentIds.Count - skippedPartialPaymentIds.Count;
            Log.Info($"Settlements eligible for load: {eligibleCount}  |  skipped: {skippedIds.Count}");
            Log.Info($"Partial payments eligible for load: {eligiblePartialPayments}  |  skipped: {skippedPartialPaymentIds.Count}");
            Log.Info($"Total CSV rows to write: {allRows.Count}");

            if (allRows.Count == 0)
            {
                Log.Info("No CSV rows generated — nothing to persist.");
                return new ProcessResult
                {
                    TotalScanned    = totalScanned,
                    TotalSkipped    = skippedIds.Count,
                    PartialPaymentsScanned = partialPaymentsScanned,
                    PartialPaymentsSkipped = skippedPartialPaymentIds.Count
                };
            }

            
            if (_config.DryRun)
            {
                Log.Info("[DRY RUN] Would write CSV and persist records — no changes made.");
                return new ProcessResult
                {
                    TotalScanned    = totalScanned,
                    TotalProcessed  = eligibleCount,
                    TotalSkipped    = skippedIds.Count,
                    PartialPaymentsScanned   = partialPaymentsScanned,
                    PartialPaymentsProcessed = eligiblePartialPayments,
                    PartialPaymentsSkipped   = skippedPartialPaymentIds.Count,
                    CsvRowCount     = allRows.Count
                };
            }

            
            DateTime runTime = DateTime.Now;

            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            string csvPath = null;
            int loadId = -1;
            string assetIdsCsv = string.Join(",", eligibleAssetIds);

            using (var scope = new TransactionScope(TransactionScopeOption.Required,
                new TransactionOptions
                {
                    IsolationLevel = IsolationLevel.ReadCommitted,
                    Timeout        = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5)
                }))
            {
                try
                {
                    
                    loadId = _repo.CreateLoad(runTime, null, assetIdsCsv);
                    csvPath = SettlementCsvWriter.BuildOutputPath(
                        _config.OutputRootFolder, loadId, runTime);

                    
                    _repo.UpdateLoadFilePath(loadId, csvPath);
                    Log.Info($"  Load created: load_id={loadId}  path={csvPath}");

                    
                    SettlementCsvWriter.Write(csvPath, allRows);
                    Log.Info($"  CSV written: {allRows.Count} rows → {csvPath}");

                    
                    foreach (int sid in settlementIds)
                    {
                        if (skippedIds.Contains(sid)) continue;

                        var rowsForSid = allRows.FindAll(r => r.SettlementId == sid);
                        foreach (var row in rowsForSid)
                            _repo.InsertTransaction(loadId, row);

                        _repo.MarkSettlementProcessed(sid, loadId);
                        Log.Info($"  Settlement {sid}: {rowsForSid.Count} transaction row(s) inserted, marked processed.");
                    }

                    
                    foreach (int ppid in partialPaymentIds)
                    {
                        if (skippedPartialPaymentIds.Contains(ppid)) continue;

                        var rowsForPpid = allRows.FindAll(r => r.PartialPaymentId == ppid);
                        foreach (var row in rowsForPpid)
                            _repo.InsertTransaction(loadId, row);

                        _repo.MarkPartialPaymentProcessed(ppid, loadId);
                        Log.Info($"  PartialPayment {ppid}: {rowsForPpid.Count} transaction row(s) inserted, marked processed.");
                    }

                    scope.Complete();
                    Log.Info($"MTSettlementTrans processing complete. load_id={loadId}  csv={csvPath}  rows={allRows.Count}");
                }
                catch (Exception ex)
                {
                    Log.Error($"Processing failed for load_id={loadId} — transaction rolled back.", ex);

                    
                    if (csvPath != null && System.IO.File.Exists(csvPath))
                    {
                        try { System.IO.File.Delete(csvPath); }
                        catch (Exception deleteEx)
                        {
                            Log.Warn($"Could not delete partial CSV file '{csvPath}': {deleteEx.Message}");
                        }
                    }
                    throw;
                }
            }

            return new ProcessResult
            {
                TotalScanned    = totalScanned,
                TotalProcessed  = eligibleCount,
                TotalSkipped    = skippedIds.Count,
                PartialPaymentsScanned   = partialPaymentsScanned,
                PartialPaymentsProcessed = eligiblePartialPayments,
                PartialPaymentsSkipped   = skippedPartialPaymentIds.Count,
                CsvRowCount     = allRows.Count,
                LoadId          = loadId,
                CsvPath         = csvPath,
                Rows            = allRows
            };
        }

        
        internal static List<MTSettlementTransRow> BuildRows(
            int settlementId,
            SettlementDetail detail,
            string unlockGuid,
            string wsfsGuid,
            string refundGuid,
            string sglt8Guid)
        {
            var rows = new List<MTSettlementTransRow>();

            if (detail.RefundAmount != 0m)
            {
                
                rows.Add(new MTSettlementTransRow
                {
                    OriginatingAccountId    = unlockGuid,
                    CounterpartyAccountId   = refundGuid,
                    Type                    = BookTypeName,
                    Amount                  = detail.RefundAmount,
                    Direction               = FixedDirection,
                    RemittanceInformation   = string.Empty,
                    SettlementId            = settlementId,
                    AssetId                 = detail.AssetId,
                    Metadata                = new Dictionary<string, string> { { "asset_id", detail.AssetId } }
                });
            }

            
            bool isSglt8 = detail.AccountId == 14;
            string outboundGuid = isSglt8 ? sglt8Guid : wsfsGuid;

            
            rows.Add(new MTSettlementTransRow
            {
                OriginatingAccountId    = unlockGuid,
                CounterpartyAccountId   = outboundGuid,
                Type                    = WireTypeName,
                Amount                  = detail.NetSettlementPayment,
                Direction               = FixedDirection,
                RemittanceInformation   = detail.ObiWireInformation + detail.AssetId,
                SettlementId            = settlementId,
                AssetId                 = detail.AssetId,
                AccountName             = detail.AccountName,
                Metadata                = new Dictionary<string, string> { { "asset_id", detail.AssetId } }
            });

            return rows;
        }

        

        private static bool ValidateAmounts(int settlementId, SettlementDetail detail)
        {
            bool valid = true;

            if (detail.NetSettlementPayment < 0m)
            {
                Log.Warn($"  Settlement {settlementId}: net_settlement_payment is negative " +
                         $"({detail.NetSettlementPayment}) — skipping.");
                valid = false;
            }
            if (detail.RefundAmount < 0m)
            {
                Log.Warn($"  Settlement {settlementId}: refund_amount is negative " +
                         $"({detail.RefundAmount}) — skipping.");
                valid = false;
            }

            return valid;
        }

        private static bool ValidatePartialPaymentAmount(int partialPaymentId, PartialPaymentDetail detail)
        {
            if (detail.PayoffAmount < 0m)
            {
                Log.Warn($"  PartialPayment {partialPaymentId}: payoff_amount is negative " +
                         $"({detail.PayoffAmount}) — skipping.");
                return false;
            }
            return true;
        }

        
        internal static MTSettlementTransRow BuildPartialPaymentRow(
            int partialPaymentId,
            PartialPaymentDetail detail,
            string unlockGuid,
            string wsfsGuid,
            string sglt8Guid)
        {
            
            bool isSglt8 = detail.AccountId == 14;
            string outboundGuid = isSglt8 ? sglt8Guid : wsfsGuid;

            return new MTSettlementTransRow
            {
                OriginatingAccountId    = unlockGuid,
                CounterpartyAccountId   = outboundGuid,
                Type                    = WireTypeName,
                Amount                  = detail.PayoffAmount + detail.PartialPaymentCosts,
                Direction               = FixedDirection,
                RemittanceInformation   = detail.ObiWireInformation + detail.AssetId,
                PartialPaymentId        = partialPaymentId,
                AssetId                 = detail.AssetId,
                AccountName             = detail.AccountName,
                Metadata                = new Dictionary<string, string> { { "asset_id", detail.AssetId } }
            };
        }
    }

    
    public class ProcessResult
    {
        public int  TotalScanned   { get; set; }
        public int  TotalProcessed { get; set; }
        public int  TotalSkipped   { get; set; }
        public int  PartialPaymentsScanned   { get; set; }
        public int  PartialPaymentsProcessed { get; set; }
        public int  PartialPaymentsSkipped   { get; set; }
        public int  CsvRowCount    { get; set; }
        public int  LoadId         { get; set; }
        public string CsvPath      { get; set; }
        public List<MTSettlementTransRow> Rows { get; set; }
    }
}


--- FILE: MTSettlementTransLib\MTSettlementTransRow.cs ---
namespace MTSettlementTransLib
{
    public class MTSettlementTransRow
    {
        public string OriginatingAccountId { get; set; }
        public string CounterpartyAccountId { get; set; }
        public string Type { get; set; }
        private decimal _amount;
        public decimal Amount
        {
            get => _amount;
            set => _amount = Math.Floor(value * 100m) / 100m;
        }
        public string Direction { get; set; } = "Credit";
        public string RemittanceInformation { get; set; }
        public int? SettlementId { get; set; }
        public int? PartialPaymentId { get; set; }
        public string AssetId { get; set; }
        public string AccountName { get; set; }
        public Dictionary<string, string> Metadata { get; set; }
        public string Description
        {
            get
            {
                if (Type == "Book")
                    return $"{AssetId} - Refund Book Transfer";
                if (Type == "Wire")
                {
                    if (PartialPaymentId.HasValue)
                        return $"{AssetId} - Partial Payment Sweep to {AccountName}";
                    return $"{AssetId} - Collections Account Sweep to {AccountName}";
                }
                return string.Empty;
            }
        }
    }
}

        public string AssetId { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string AccountName { get; set; }
        public string ObiWireInformation { get; set; }
    }
}

--- FILE: MTSettlementTransLib\SettlementCsvWriter.cs ---
namespace MTSettlementTransLib
{
    public static class SettlementCsvWriter
    {
        private static readonly string[] Headers =
        {
            "originating_account_id",
            "counterparty_account_id",
            "type",
            "amount",
            "direction",
            "remittance_information",
            "description",
            "metadata"
        };
        public static string BuildFileName(DateTime runTime, int loadId)
        {
            return $"MTSettlementTrans_{runTime:yyyyMMdd}_Load-{loadId}.csv";
        }
        public static string BuildOutputPath(string outputRootFolder, int loadId,
            DateTime runTime)
        {
            string loadFolder = Path.Combine(outputRootFolder, $"Load-{loadId}");
            Directory.CreateDirectory(loadFolder);
            return Path.Combine(loadFolder, BuildFileName(runTime, loadId));
        }
        public static void Write(string filePath, IEnumerable<MTSettlementTransRow> rows)
        {
            if (filePath == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(filePath));
            if (rows == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(rows));

            using (var sw = new StreamWriter(filePath, append: false,
                encoding: new UTF8Encoding(encoderShouldEmitUTF8Identifier: true)))
            {
                sw.WriteLine(string.Join(",", Headers));
                foreach (var row in rows)
                    sw.WriteLine(BuildRow(row));
            }
        }

        
        private static string SerializeMetadata(Dictionary<string, string> metadata)
        {
            if (metadata == null || metadata.Count == 0) return string.Empty;

            var sb = new StringBuilder();
            bool first = true;
            foreach (var kvp in metadata)
            {
                if (!first) sb.Append("|");
                sb.Append(kvp.Key).Append(":").Append(kvp.Value);
                first = false;
            }
            return sb.ToString();
        }

        private static string BuildRow(MTSettlementTransRow row)
        {
            long amountInCents = (long)Math.Round(row.Amount * 100m, MidpointRounding.AwayFromZero);

            return string.Join(",",
                Escape(row.OriginatingAccountId),
                Escape(row.CounterpartyAccountId),
                Escape(row.Type),
                amountInCents.ToString(),
                Escape(row.Direction),
                Escape(row.RemittanceInformation),
                Escape(row.Description),
                Escape(SerializeMetadata(row.Metadata)));
        }
        private static string Escape(string value)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(value)) return string.Empty;
            if (value.Contains(",") || value.Contains("\"") || value.Contains("\n"))
                return "\"" + value.Replace("\"", "\"\"") + "\"";
            return value;
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: MTSettlementTransLib\SettlementRepository.cs ---
namespace MTSettlementTransLib
{
    public class SettlementRepository : ISettlementRepository
    {
        private readonly string _server;

        public SettlementRepository(string server)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(server))
                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(server));
            _server = server;
        }

        

        public List<int> GetUnprocessedSettlementIds()
        {
            string sql = "SELECT id FROM Settlements WHERE mtst_load_id IS NULL ORDER BY id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();

            var ids = new List<int>();
            if (tbl == null) return ids;
            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
                ids.Add(Convert.ToInt32(row["id"]));
            return ids;
        }

        public SettlementDetail GetSettlementDetail(int settlementId)
        {
            string sql =
                "SELECT ex.settlement_id, ex.asset_id, ex.account_id, ex.net_settlement_payment, " +
                "       ex.refund_amount, acc.obi_wire_information, acc.[name] AS account_name " +
                "FROM vSettlementsEx ex " +
                "JOIN vAccounts acc ON acc.account_id = ex.account_id " +
                "WHERE ex.settlement_id = @settlement_id";

            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@settlement_id", settlementId);
            DataRow row = q.ExecuteTableSingleRow();
            if (row == null) return null;

            return new SettlementDetail
            {
                SettlementId = Convert.ToInt32(row["settlement_id"]),
                AssetId = row["asset_id"] == DBNull.Value ? string.Empty : row["asset_id"].ToString(),
                AccountId = Convert.ToInt32(row["account_id"]),
                NetSettlementPayment = Convert.ToDecimal(row["net_settlement_payment"]),
                RefundAmount = Convert.ToDecimal(row["refund_amount"]),
                ObiWireInformation = row["obi_wire_information"] == DBNull.Value
                    ? null
                    : row["obi_wire_information"].ToString(),
                AccountName = row["account_name"] == DBNull.Value
                    ? null
                    : row["account_name"].ToString()
            };
        }

        public string GetAccountGuid(string accountName)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT MTAccountGuid FROM MTSettlementAccounts WHERE AccountName = @name";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@name", accountName);
            DataRow row = q.ExecuteTableSingleRow();
            if (row == null || row["MTAccountGuid"] == DBNull.Value)
                return null;
            return row["MTAccountGuid"].ToString();
        }

        

        public void EnsureBookTypeExists()
        {
            string checkSql = "SELECT COUNT(1) FROM MTSettlementTypes WHERE TypeName = 'Book'";
            Query check = new Query(checkSql, _server);
            int count = check.ExecuteSingle<int>();
            if (count > 0) return;

            int nextId = Common.GetNextId(_server, "MTSettlementTypes");
            string insertSql =
                "INSERT INTO MTSettlementTypes (id, TypeName, Description) " +
                "VALUES (@id, 'Book', 'Refund Transfer')";
            Query insert = new Query(insertSql, _server);
            insert.AddParameter("@id", nextId);
            insert.Execute();
        }

        public int CreateLoad(DateTime loadTime, string csvPath, string assetIds = null, bool latest = true)
        {
            int loadId = Common.GetNextId(_server, "MTSettlementTransLoads");
            string sql =
                "INSERT INTO MTSettlementTransLoads (id, load_time, file_name, asset_ids, latest) " +
                "VALUES (@load_id, @load_time, @file_name, @asset_ids, @latest)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@load_id", loadId);
            q.AddParameter("@load_time", loadTime);
            q.AddParameter("@file_name", csvPath ?? (object)DBNull.Value);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_ids", assetIds ?? (object)DBNull.Value);
            q.AddParameter("@latest", latest);
            q.Execute();
            return loadId;
        }

        public void InsertTransaction(int loadId, MTSettlementTransRow row)
        {
            string metadataJson = null;
            if (row.Metadata != null && row.Metadata.Count > 0)
            {
                var serializer = new JavaScriptSerializer();
                metadataJson = serializer.Serialize(row.Metadata);
            }

            string sql =
                "INSERT INTO MTSettlementTrans " +
                "  (load_id, originating_account_id, counterparty_account_id, " +
                "   type, amount, direction, remittance_information, settlement_id, partialpayment_id, asset_id, description, metadata) " +
                "VALUES " +
                "  (@load_id, @originating_account_id, @counterparty_account_id, " +
                "   @type, @amount, @direction, @remittance_information, @settlement_id, @partialpayment_id, @asset_id, @description, @metadata)";

            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@load_id", loadId);
            q.AddParameter("@originating_account_id", row.OriginatingAccountId);
            q.AddParameter("@counterparty_account_id", row.CounterpartyAccountId);
            q.AddParameter("@type", row.Type);
            q.AddParameter("@amount", row.Amount);
            q.AddParameter("@direction", row.Direction);
            q.AddParameter("@remittance_information", row.RemittanceInformation);
            q.AddParameter("@settlement_id", row.SettlementId.HasValue ? (object)row.SettlementId.Value : DBNull.Value);
            q.AddParameter("@partialpayment_id", row.PartialPaymentId.HasValue ? (object)row.PartialPaymentId.Value : DBNull.Value);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", row.AssetId);
            q.AddParameter("@description", row.Description);
            q.AddParameter("@metadata", metadataJson ?? (object)DBNull.Value);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public void UpdateLoadFilePath(int loadId, string csvPath)
        {
            string sql = "UPDATE MTSettlementTransLoads SET file_name = @file_name WHERE id = @load_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@load_id", loadId);
            q.AddParameter("@file_name", csvPath ?? (object)DBNull.Value);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public void MarkSettlementProcessed(int settlementId, int loadId)
        {
            string sql =
                "UPDATE Settlements SET mtst_load_id = @load_id WHERE id = @settlement_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@load_id", loadId);
            q.AddParameter("@settlement_id", settlementId);
            q.Execute();
        }

        

        public List<int> GetUnprocessedPartialPaymentIds()
        {
            string sql = "SELECT id FROM PartialPayments WHERE mtst_load_id IS NULL ORDER BY id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();

            var ids = new List<int>();
            if (tbl == null) return ids;
            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
                ids.Add(Convert.ToInt32(row["id"]));
            return ids;
        }

        public PartialPaymentDetail GetPartialPaymentDetail(int partialPaymentId)
        {
            string sql =
                "SELECT pp.partialpayment_id, pp.asset_id, pp.account_id, pp.payoff_amount, pp.partialpayment_costs, " +
                " acc.obi_wire_information, acc.[name] AS account_name " +
                "FROM vPartialPayments pp " +
                "JOIN vAccounts acc ON acc.account_id = pp.account_id " +
                "WHERE pp.partialpayment_id = @partial_payment_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@partial_payment_id", partialPaymentId);
            DataRow row = q.ExecuteTableSingleRow();
            if (row == null) return null;

            return new PartialPaymentDetail
            {
                PartialPaymentId = Convert.ToInt32(row["partialpayment_id"]),
                AssetId = row["asset_id"] == DBNull.Value ? string.Empty : row["asset_id"].ToString(),
                AccountId = Convert.ToInt32(row["account_id"]),
                PayoffAmount = Convert.ToDecimal(row["payoff_amount"]),
                PartialPaymentCosts = Convert.ToInt32(row["partialpayment_costs"]),
                ObiWireInformation = row["obi_wire_information"] == DBNull.Value
                    ? null
                    : row["obi_wire_information"].ToString(),
                AccountName = row["account_name"] == DBNull.Value
                    ? null
                    : row["account_name"].ToString()
            };
        }

        public void MarkPartialPaymentProcessed(int partialPaymentId, int loadId)
        {
            string sql =
                "UPDATE PartialPayments SET mtst_load_id = @load_id WHERE id = @partial_payment_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.AddParameter("@load_id", loadId);
            q.AddParameter("@partial_payment_id", partialPaymentId);
            q.Execute();
        }
    }

    internal static class Transactions
    {
        internal static void InsertTransaction(string server, int loadId,
            MTSettlementTransRow row)
        {
            string sql =
                "INSERT INTO MTSettlementTrans " +
                "  (load_id, originating_account_id, counterparty_account_id, " +
                "   type, amount, direction, remittance_information, settlement_id, asset_id) " +
                "VALUES " +
                "  (@load_id, @originating_account_id, @counterparty_account_id, " +
                "   @type, @amount, @direction, @remittance_information, @settlement_id, @asset_id)";

            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@load_id", loadId);
            q.AddParameter("@originating_account_id", row.OriginatingAccountId);
            q.AddParameter("@counterparty_account_id", row.CounterpartyAccountId);
            q.AddParameter("@type", row.Type);
            q.AddParameter("@amount", row.Amount);
            q.AddParameter("@direction", row.Direction);
            q.AddParameter("@remittance_information",
                string.IsNullOrEmpty(row.RemittanceInformation)
                    ? (object)DBNull.Value
                    : row.RemittanceInformation);
            q.AddParameter("@settlement_id", row.SettlementId);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", row.AssetId ?? (object)DBNull.Value);
            q.Execute();
        }
        internal static int CountByLoad(string server, int loadId)
        {
            string sql =
                "SELECT COUNT(1) FROM MTSettlementTrans WHERE load_id = @load_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@load_id", loadId);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int>();
        }
    }

--- FILE: ModernTreasuryLib\Backfill.cs ---
namespace ModernTreasuryLib
{
    public class Backfill
    {
        
        public static async Task RunAsync(DataTable assets)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();
            if (assets == null || assets.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No assets supplied for backfill.");
                return;
            }

            foreach (DataRow row in assets.Rows)
            {
                if (!row.Table.Columns.Contains("asset_id"))
                    continue;

                string assetId = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                string pipelineLabel = row.Table.Columns.Contains("customer_pipeline_label_max") ? row["customer_pipeline_label_max"].ToString() : null;

                
                decimal oface = GetDecimalWithTextFallback(row, "oface", "oface_text");
                decimal purchaseProceeds = GetDecimalWithTextFallback(row, "purchase_proceeds", "purchase_proceeds_text");
                decimal gainOnSale = CalculateGainOnSale(purchaseProceeds, oface);

                
                string fileNum = GetString(row, "file_num") ?? GetString(row, "file_number") ?? GetString(row, "FILE NUMBER");
                string effectiveDate = GetString(row, "effective_date") ?? GetString(row, "EFF_DATE");
                string fundingDate = GetString(row, "funding_date") ?? GetString(row, "VALUE_DATE_INPUT");

                
                string tradeId = GetString(row, "trade_id");
                string accountId = GetString(row, "account_id");
                string tradeDate = GetString(row, "trade_date");
                string settleDate = GetString(row, "settle_date");
                decimal price = GetDecimal(row, "price");
                string investorMemoAccountName = GetString(row, "investor_memo_account_name");
                string investor_contra_memo_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.backfill_contra_account_id;

                
                string investorMemoCategoryId = null;
                if (row.Table.Columns.Contains("investor_mt_account_id") && row["investor_mt_account_id"] != DBNull.Value)
                    investorMemoCategoryId = row["investor_mt_account_id"].ToString();

                
                string investorIPMemoCategoryId = null;
                if (row.Table.Columns.Contains("investor_IP_mt_account_id") && row["investor_IP_mt_account_id"] != DBNull.Value)
                    investorIPMemoCategoryId = row["investor_IP_mt_account_id"].ToString();

                
                string assetCategoryId = await ModernTreasury_Draw.CreateLedgerAssetCategoryAsync(assetId, pipelineLabel, fundingDate);
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(assetCategoryId))
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create category for Asset {assetId}");
                    continue;
                }
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_category", assetCategoryId, "category", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + assetCategoryId, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m,fundingDate);

                
                string subCategoryId_funding = await ModernTreasuryUtils.CreateLedgerSubCategoryAsync("Funding", assetCategoryId, assetId);
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_funding_subcategory", subCategoryId_funding, "subcategory", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + subCategoryId_funding, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m, fundingDate);
                string subCategoryId_trades = await ModernTreasuryUtils.CreateLedgerSubCategoryAsync("Trades", assetCategoryId, assetId);
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_trades_subcategory", subCategoryId_trades, "subcategory", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + subCategoryId_trades, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m, fundingDate);

                
                var tradesCategoryIds = new List<string> { subCategoryId_trades };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(investorMemoCategoryId)) tradesCategoryIds.Add(investorMemoCategoryId);

                
                var fundingCategoryIds = new List<string> { subCategoryId_funding };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(investorIPMemoCategoryId)) fundingCategoryIds.Add(investorIPMemoCategoryId);


                
                var ipAccountMetadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fileNum)) ipAccountMetadata["file_num"] = fileNum;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(effectiveDate)) ipAccountMetadata["effective_date"] = effectiveDate;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fundingDate)) ipAccountMetadata["funding_date"] = fundingDate;             
                ipAccountMetadata["investment_payment"] = oface.ToString();

                var tradeAccountMetadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tradeId)) tradeAccountMetadata["trade_id"] = tradeId;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(accountId)) tradeAccountMetadata["account_id"] = accountId;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tradeDate)) tradeAccountMetadata["trade_date"] = tradeDate;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(settleDate)) tradeAccountMetadata["settle_date"] = settleDate;
                if (price > 0m) tradeAccountMetadata["price"] = price.ToString();
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(investorMemoAccountName)) tradeAccountMetadata["investor_memo_account_name"] = investorMemoAccountName;
                tradeAccountMetadata["investment_payment"] = oface.ToString();
                tradeAccountMetadata["initiated_by"] = "Backfill.cs";
                tradeAccountMetadata["modern_treasury_view"] = "backfill";

                
                string investmentPaymentId = await CreateInvestmentPaymentLedgerAccountAsync(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, pipelineLabel, fundingCategoryIds, oface, ipAccountMetadata);
                string gainOnSaleId = null;
                string purchaseProceedsId = null;
                if (purchaseProceeds > 0)
                {
                    gainOnSaleId = await CreateGainOnSaleLedgerAccountAsync(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, pipelineLabel, new List<string> { subCategoryId_trades }, gainOnSale, tradeAccountMetadata);
                    purchaseProceedsId = await CreatePurchaseProceedsLedgerAccountAsync(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, pipelineLabel, tradesCategoryIds, purchaseProceeds, tradeAccountMetadata);
                }

                
                string ltIPId = await CreateInvestmentPaymentLedgerTransactionAsync(assetId, pipelineLabel, investmentPaymentId, investor_contra_memo_account_id, oface, fileNum, effectiveDate, fundingDate);
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ltIPId)) Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create Investment Payment ledger transaction for Asset {assetId}");

                if (purchaseProceeds > 0 && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(purchaseProceedsId) && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(gainOnSaleId))
                {
                    string ltPPId = await CreatePurchaseProceedsInverseTransactionAsync(assetId, pipelineLabel, purchaseProceedsId, investmentPaymentId, gainOnSaleId, purchaseProceeds, oface, gainOnSale, tradeId, accountId, tradeDate, settleDate, price, investorMemoAccountName);
                    if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ltPPId)) Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create Purchase Proceeds inverse ledger transaction for Asset {assetId}");
                }
            }
        }

        
        public static async Task RunAsyncOriginations(DataTable assets)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();
            if (assets == null || assets.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No assets supplied for originations backfill.");
                return;
            }

            foreach (DataRow row in assets.Rows)
            {
                if (!row.Table.Columns.Contains("asset_id"))
                    continue;

                string assetId = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                string pipelineLabel = row.Table.Columns.Contains("customer_pipeline_label_max") ? row["customer_pipeline_label_max"].ToString() : null;

                decimal oface = GetDecimalWithTextFallback(row, "oface", "oface_text");
                string fileNum = GetString(row, "file_num") ?? GetString(row, "file_number") ?? GetString(row, "FILE NUMBER");
                string effectiveDate = GetString(row, "effective_date") ?? GetString(row, "EFF_DATE");
                string fundingDate = GetString(row, "funding_date") ?? GetString(row, "VALUE_DATE_INPUT");
                string investor_contra_memo_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.backfill_contra_account_id;

                string assetCategoryId = await ModernTreasury_Draw.CreateLedgerAssetCategoryAsync(assetId, pipelineLabel, null);
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(assetCategoryId))
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create category for Asset {assetId}");
                    continue;
                }
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_category", assetCategoryId, "category", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + assetCategoryId, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m, fundingDate);

                string subCategoryId_funding = await ModernTreasuryUtils.CreateLedgerSubCategoryAsync("Funding", assetCategoryId, assetId);
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_funding_subcategory", subCategoryId_funding, "subcategory", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + subCategoryId_funding, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m, fundingDate);

                var ipAccountMetadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fileNum)) ipAccountMetadata["file_num"] = fileNum;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(effectiveDate)) ipAccountMetadata["effective_date"] = effectiveDate;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fundingDate)) ipAccountMetadata["funding_date"] = fundingDate;                
                ipAccountMetadata["investment_payment"] = oface.ToString();

                string investmentPaymentId = await CreateInvestmentPaymentLedgerAccountAsync(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, pipelineLabel, new List<string> { subCategoryId_funding }, oface, ipAccountMetadata);

                string ltIPId = await CreateInvestmentPaymentLedgerTransactionAsync(assetId, pipelineLabel, investmentPaymentId, investor_contra_memo_account_id, oface, fileNum, effectiveDate, fundingDate);
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ltIPId)) Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create Investment Payment ledger transaction for Asset {assetId}");
            }
        }

        
        public static async Task RunAsyncSettlements(DataTable assets)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();
            if (assets == null || assets.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No assets supplied for settlement backfill.");
                return;
            }

            foreach (DataRow row in assets.Rows)
            {
                if (!row.Table.Columns.Contains("asset_id"))
                    continue;

                string assetId = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                string pipelineLabel = row.Table.Columns.Contains("customer_pipeline_label_max") ? row["customer_pipeline_label_max"].ToString() : null;

                decimal netSettlementPayment = GetDecimal(row, "net_settlement_payment");
                string fileNum = GetString(row, "file_num") ?? GetString(row, "file_number") ?? GetString(row, "FILE NUMBER");
                string effectiveDate = GetString(row, "effective_date") ?? GetString(row, "EFF_DATE");
                string fundingDate = GetString(row, "funding_date") ?? GetString(row, "VALUE_DATE_INPUT");
                decimal oface = GetDecimalWithTextFallback(row, "oface", "oface_text");
                string investor_contra_memo_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.backfill_contra_account_id;
                string finalDispositionDate = GetString(row, "final_disposition_date") ?? GetString(row, "FINAL_DISPOSITION_DATE");
                string settlementType = GetString(row, "settlement_type") ?? GetString(row, "SETTLEMENT_TYPE");
                string settlementReason = GetString(row, "settlement_reason") ?? GetString(row, "SETTLEMENT_REASON");
                string settlementAccount = GetString(row, "settlement_account") ?? GetString(row, "SETTLEMENT_ACCOUNT");


                string assetCategoryId = await ModernTreasury_Draw.CreateLedgerAssetCategoryAsync(assetId, pipelineLabel, null);
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(assetCategoryId))
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create category for Asset {assetId}");
                    continue;
                }
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_category", assetCategoryId, "category", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + assetCategoryId, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m, fundingDate);

                string subCategoryId_funding = await ModernTreasuryUtils.CreateLedgerSubCategoryAsync("Funding", assetCategoryId, assetId);
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_funding_subcategory", subCategoryId_funding, "subcategory", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + subCategoryId_funding, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m, fundingDate);

                var ipAccountMetadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fileNum)) ipAccountMetadata["file_num"] = fileNum;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(effectiveDate)) ipAccountMetadata["effective_date"] = effectiveDate;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fundingDate)) ipAccountMetadata["funding_date"] = fundingDate;                
                ipAccountMetadata["investment_payment"] = oface.ToString();

                string investmentPaymentId = await CreateInvestmentPaymentLedgerAccountAsync(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, pipelineLabel, new List<string> { subCategoryId_funding }, oface, ipAccountMetadata);

                
                string ltIPId = await CreateInvestmentPaymentLedgerTransactionAsync(assetId, pipelineLabel, investmentPaymentId, investor_contra_memo_account_id, oface, fileNum, effectiveDate, fundingDate);
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ltIPId)) Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create Investment Payment ledger transaction for Asset {assetId}");

                
                string subCategoryId_settlement = await ModernTreasuryUtils.CreateLedgerSubCategoryAsync("Settlement", assetCategoryId, assetId);
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_settlement_subcategory", subCategoryId_settlement, "subcategory", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, netSettlementPayment, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + subCategoryId_settlement, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m, fundingDate);

                
                var settlementAccountMetadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fileNum)) settlementAccountMetadata["file_num"] = fileNum;
                settlementAccountMetadata["investment_payment"] = oface.ToString();
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(effectiveDate)) settlementAccountMetadata["effective_date"] = effectiveDate;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fundingDate)) settlementAccountMetadata["funding_date"] = fundingDate;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(finalDispositionDate)) settlementAccountMetadata["final_disposition_date"] = finalDispositionDate;
                if (netSettlementPayment > 0m) settlementAccountMetadata["net_settlement_payment"] = netSettlementPayment.ToString();
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(settlementType)) settlementAccountMetadata["settlement_type"] = settlementType;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(settlementReason)) settlementAccountMetadata["settlement_reason"] = settlementReason;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(settlementAccount)) settlementAccountMetadata["settlement_account"] = settlementAccount;

                string settlementAccountId = await CreateSettlementLedgerAccountAsync(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, pipelineLabel, new List<string> { subCategoryId_settlement }, netSettlementPayment, settlementAccountMetadata);

                
                string ltSettleId = await CreateInvestorLedgerAccountSettlementTransactionsAsync(
                    assetId,
                    pipelineLabel,
                    investmentPaymentId,
                    settlementAccountId,
                    investor_contra_memo_account_id,
                    oface,
                    fileNum,
                    effectiveDate,
                    fundingDate,
                    finalDispositionDate,
                    netSettlementPayment,
                    settlementType,
                    settlementReason
                );
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ltSettleId)) Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create Settlement ledger transaction for Asset {assetId}");
            }
        }

        
        public static async Task RunAsyncPartialPayments(DataTable assets)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();
            if (assets == null || assets.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No assets supplied for partial payment backfill.");
                return;
            }

            foreach (DataRow row in assets.Rows)
            {
                if (!row.Table.Columns.Contains("asset_id"))
                    continue;

                string assetId = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                string pipelineLabel = row.Table.Columns.Contains("customer_pipeline_label_max") ? row["customer_pipeline_label_max"].ToString() : null;

                
                decimal oface = GetDecimalWithTextFallback(row, "oface", "oface_text");
                decimal purchaseProceeds = GetDecimalWithTextFallback(row, "purchase_proceeds", "purchase_proceeds_text");
                decimal gainOnSale = CalculateGainOnSale(purchaseProceeds, oface);

                
                string fileNum = GetString(row, "file_num") ?? GetString(row, "file_number") ?? GetString(row, "FILE NUMBER");
                string effectiveDate = GetString(row, "effective_date") ?? GetString(row, "EFF_DATE");
                string fundingDate = GetString(row, "funding_date") ?? GetString(row, "VALUE_DATE_INPUT");

                
                string tradeId = GetString(row, "trade_id");
                string accountId = GetString(row, "account_id");
                string tradeDate = GetString(row, "trade_date");
                string settleDate = GetString(row, "settle_date");
                decimal price = GetDecimal(row, "price");
                string investorMemoAccountName = GetString(row, "investor_memo_account_name");
                string investor_contra_memo_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.backfill_contra_account_id;

                
                string valueDate = GetString(row, "value_date") ?? GetString(row, "VALUE_DATE");
                string endingFactor = GetString(row, "ending_factor") ?? GetString(row, "ENDING_FACTOR");
                decimal endingInvestmentPayment = GetDecimal(row, "ending_investment_payment");
                if (endingInvestmentPayment == 0m) endingInvestmentPayment = GetDecimal(row, "ENDING_INVESTMENT_PAYMENT");
                decimal endingPurchaseProceeds = GetDecimal(row, "ending_purchase_proceeds");
                if (endingPurchaseProceeds == 0m) endingPurchaseProceeds = GetDecimal(row, "ENDING_PURCHASE_PROCEEDS");

                
                string investorMemoCategoryId = null;
                if (row.Table.Columns.Contains("investor_mt_account_id") && row["investor_mt_account_id"] != DBNull.Value)
                    investorMemoCategoryId = row["investor_mt_account_id"].ToString();

                
                string investorIPMemoCategoryId = null;
                if (row.Table.Columns.Contains("investor_IP_mt_account_id") && row["investor_IP_mt_account_id"] != DBNull.Value)
                    investorMemoCategoryId = row["investor_IP_mt_account_id"].ToString();


                
                string assetCategoryId = await ModernTreasury_Draw.CreateLedgerAssetCategoryAsync(assetId, pipelineLabel, null);
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(assetCategoryId))
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create category for Asset {assetId}");
                    continue;
                }
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_category", assetCategoryId, "category", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + assetCategoryId, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m, fundingDate);

                
                string subCategoryId_funding = await ModernTreasuryUtils.CreateLedgerSubCategoryAsync("Funding", assetCategoryId, assetId);
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_funding_subcategory", subCategoryId_funding, "subcategory", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + subCategoryId_funding, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m, fundingDate);
                string subCategoryId_trades = await ModernTreasuryUtils.CreateLedgerSubCategoryAsync("Trades", assetCategoryId, assetId);
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "create_ledger_trades_subcategory", subCategoryId_trades, "subcategory", pipelineLabel, null, assetId, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + subCategoryId_trades, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m, fundingDate);

                
                var tradesCategoryIds = new List<string> { subCategoryId_trades };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(investorMemoCategoryId)) tradesCategoryIds.Add(investorMemoCategoryId);

                
                var fundingCategoryIds = new List<string> { subCategoryId_funding };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(investorIPMemoCategoryId)) fundingCategoryIds.Add(investorIPMemoCategoryId);

                
                var ipAccountMetadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fileNum)) ipAccountMetadata["file_num"] = fileNum;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(effectiveDate)) ipAccountMetadata["effective_date"] = effectiveDate;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fundingDate)) ipAccountMetadata["funding_date"] = fundingDate;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(valueDate)) ipAccountMetadata["value_date"] = valueDate;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(endingFactor)) ipAccountMetadata["ending_factor"] = endingFactor;
                if (endingInvestmentPayment != 0m) ipAccountMetadata["ending_investment_payment"] = endingInvestmentPayment.ToString();
                if (endingPurchaseProceeds != 0m) ipAccountMetadata["ending_purchase_proceeds"] = endingPurchaseProceeds.ToString();                
                ipAccountMetadata["investment_payment_orig"] = oface.ToString();

                var tradeAccountMetadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tradeId)) tradeAccountMetadata["trade_id"] = tradeId;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(accountId)) tradeAccountMetadata["account_id"] = accountId;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tradeDate)) tradeAccountMetadata["trade_date"] = tradeDate;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(settleDate)) tradeAccountMetadata["settle_date"] = settleDate;
                if (price > 0m) tradeAccountMetadata["price"] = price.ToString();
                tradeAccountMetadata["investment_payment_orig"] = oface.ToString();
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(investorMemoAccountName)) tradeAccountMetadata["investor_memo_account_name"] = investorMemoAccountName;
                tradeAccountMetadata["initiated_by"] = "Backfill.cs";
                tradeAccountMetadata["modern_treasury_view"] = "backfill";

                
                string investmentPaymentId = await CreateInvestmentPaymentLedgerAccountAsync(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, pipelineLabel, fundingCategoryIds, oface, ipAccountMetadata);
                string gainOnSaleId = null;
                string purchaseProceedsId = null;
                if (purchaseProceeds > 0)
                {
                    gainOnSaleId = await CreateGainOnSaleLedgerAccountAsync(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, pipelineLabel, new List<string> { subCategoryId_trades }, gainOnSale, tradeAccountMetadata);
                    purchaseProceedsId = await CreatePurchaseProceedsLedgerAccountAsync(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, pipelineLabel, tradesCategoryIds, purchaseProceeds, tradeAccountMetadata);
                }

                
                string ltIPId = await CreateInvestmentPaymentLedgerTransactionAsync(assetId, pipelineLabel, investmentPaymentId, investor_contra_memo_account_id, oface, fileNum, effectiveDate, fundingDate);
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ltIPId)) Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create Investment Payment ledger transaction for Asset {assetId}");

                if (purchaseProceeds > 0 && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(purchaseProceedsId) && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(gainOnSaleId))
                {
                    string ltPPId = await CreatePurchaseProceedsInverseTransactionAsync(assetId, pipelineLabel, purchaseProceedsId, investmentPaymentId, gainOnSaleId, purchaseProceeds, oface, gainOnSale, tradeId, accountId, tradeDate, settleDate, price, investorMemoAccountName);
                    if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ltPPId)) Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create Purchase Proceeds inverse ledger transaction for Asset {assetId}");
                }

                
                decimal currentIP = (purchaseProceeds > 0) ? 0m : oface; 
                decimal currentPP = (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(purchaseProceedsId)) ? purchaseProceeds : 0m;

                
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(purchaseProceedsId) && endingPurchaseProceeds != 0m)
                {
                    purchaseProceedsId = await CreatePurchaseProceedsLedgerAccountAsync(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, pipelineLabel, tradesCategoryIds, purchaseProceeds);
                }

                var entries = new JArray();
                
                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(investmentPaymentId) && endingInvestmentPayment < currentIP)
                {
                    decimal reduceIP = currentIP - endingInvestmentPayment;
                    int ipAdj = ToInt(reduceIP);
                    entries.Add(new JObject { ["amount"] = ipAdj, ["direction"] = "credit", ["ledger_account_id"] = investmentPaymentId });
                    entries.Add(new JObject { ["amount"] = ipAdj, ["direction"] = "debit",  ["ledger_account_id"] = investor_contra_memo_account_id });
                }
                
                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(purchaseProceedsId) && endingPurchaseProceeds < currentPP)
                {
                    decimal reducePP = currentPP - endingPurchaseProceeds;
                    int ppAdj = ToInt(reducePP);
                    entries.Add(new JObject { ["amount"] = ppAdj, ["direction"] = "credit", ["ledger_account_id"] = purchaseProceedsId });
                    entries.Add(new JObject { ["amount"] = ppAdj, ["direction"] = "debit",  ["ledger_account_id"] = investor_contra_memo_account_id });
                }

                if (entries.Count > 0)
                {
                    var metadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
                    if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(valueDate)) metadata["value_date"] = valueDate;
                    if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(endingFactor)) metadata["ending_factor"] = endingFactor;
                    if (endingInvestmentPayment != 0m) metadata["ending_investment_payment"] = endingInvestmentPayment.ToString();
                    if (endingPurchaseProceeds != 0m) metadata["ending_purchase_proceeds"] = endingPurchaseProceeds.ToString();
                    metadata["investment_payment_orig"] = oface.ToString();

                    foreach (JObject e in entries) e["metadata"] = metadata.DeepClone();

                    var ltAdjust = new JObject
                    {
                        ["description"] = $"Backfill Partial Payment Adjustments for Asset {assetId}",
                        ["status"] = "posted",
                        ["ledger_entries"] = entries
                    };

                    try
                    {
                        string body = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ltAdjust);
                        string ltId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
                        string url = "https:

                        decimal totalAbs = 0m;
                        foreach (JObject e in entries) totalAbs += (int)e["amount"] / 100m;

                        ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "backfill_create_partial_payment_adjustments_ledger_transaction", ltId, "ledger_transaction", pipelineLabel, "_Backfill_PartialPayment_Adjust", assetId, totalAbs, url, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m, fundingDate);
                    }
                    catch (Exception ex)
                    {
                        Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create Partial Payment adjustment ledger transaction for Asset {assetId}. {ex.Message}");
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        
        
        public static async Task RunAddLedgerAccountsToCategoryFromExcelAsync(DataTable excelTable)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();
            if (excelTable == null || excelTable.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No rows supplied for AddLedgerAccountsToCategory.");
                return;
            }

            
            string FindColumn(params string[] candidates)
            {
                foreach (var cand in candidates)
                {
                    if (excelTable.Columns.Contains(cand)) return cand;
                    foreach (DataColumn col in excelTable.Columns)
                        if (string.Equals(col.ColumnName, cand, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                            return col.ColumnName;
                }
                return null;
            }

            string assetCol = FindColumn("asset_id");
            string categoryCol = FindColumn("target_category_id", "category_id", "ledger_account_category_id");
            string typeCol = FindColumn("ledger_account_type", "ledgerAccountType", "type");

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(assetCol) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(categoryCol) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(typeCol))
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Missing required columns. Need asset_id, target_category_id, ledger_account_type.");
                return;
            }

            
            var groups = new Dictionary<string, DataTable>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

            foreach (DataRow row in excelTable.Rows)
            {
                if (row == null) continue;
                string assetId = row[assetCol]?.ToString()?.Trim();
                string categoryId = row[categoryCol]?.ToString()?.Trim();
                string typeRaw = row[typeCol]?.ToString()?.Trim();
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(assetId) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(categoryId) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(typeRaw))
                    continue;

                
                string norm = typeRaw.Replace(" ", string.Empty).ToLowerInvariant();
                string typeKey = null;
                if (norm == "investmentpayment" || norm == "ip") typeKey = "InvestmentPayment";
                else if (norm == "purchaseproceeds" || norm == "pp") typeKey = "PurchaseProceeds";
                else
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Skipping row with unsupported ledger_account_type '{typeRaw}' for asset {assetId}.");
                    continue;
                }

                if (!groups.TryGetValue(typeKey, out var dt))
                {
                    dt = new DataTable();
                    dt.Columns.Add("asset_id", typeof(string));
                    dt.Columns.Add("target_category_id", typeof(string));
                    groups[typeKey] = dt;
                }
                groups[typeKey].Rows.Add(assetId, categoryId);
            }

            foreach (var kvp in groups)
            {
                string typeKey = kvp.Key; 
                DataTable subset = kvp.Value;
                try
                {
                    await ModernTreasuryUtils.AddLedgerAccountsToCategoryAsync(MTDrawGlobals.server, subset, typeKey);
                    Console.WriteLine($"Processed {subset.Rows.Count} rows for type {typeKey}.");
                }
                catch (Exception ex)
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Failed to add ledger accounts for type {typeKey}. {ex.Message}");
                }
            }
        }

        
        private static async Task<string> CreateInvestmentPaymentLedgerAccountAsync(string server, string assetId, string pipelineLabel, List<string> categoryIds, decimal amountForMap, JObject metadata)
        {
            string targetLedger = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.unlock_ledger_id;
            string accountLabel = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_label + assetId + Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.investment_payment_label;
            string ledgerAccountName = assetId + Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.investment_payment_label;

            var ledgerAccount = new JObject
            {
                ["name"] = ledgerAccountName,
                ["currency"] = "USD",
                ["normal_balance"] = "debit",
                ["ledger_account_category_ids"] = JArray.FromObject(categoryIds),
                ["ledger_id"] = targetLedger,
                ["description"] = accountLabel
            };
            if (metadata != null && metadata.HasValues) ledgerAccount["metadata"] = metadata;
            string body = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ledgerAccount);
            string id = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
            ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, assetId, "backfill_create_ledger_account_investment_payment", id, "ledger_account", pipelineLabel, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.investment_payment_label, assetId, amountForMap, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_url_prefix + id, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m, null);
            return id;
        }

        private static async Task<string> CreatePurchaseProceedsLedgerAccountAsync(string server, string assetId, string pipelineLabel, List<string> categoryIds, decimal amountForMap, JObject metadata)
        {
            string targetLedger = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.unlock_ledger_id;

            string id = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
            ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, assetId, "create_ledger_account_purchase_proceeds", id, "ledger_account", pipelineLabel, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.purchase_proceeds_label, assetId, amountForMap, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_url_prefix + id, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m, null);
