        }
        private static Task<string> CreatePurchaseProceedsLedgerAccountAsync(string server, string assetId, string pipelineLabel, List<string> categoryIds, decimal amountForMap)
            => CreatePurchaseProceedsLedgerAccountAsync(server, assetId, pipelineLabel, categoryIds, amountForMap, null);

        private static async Task<string> CreateSettlementLedgerAccountAsync(string server, string assetId, string pipelineLabel, List<string> categoryIds, decimal amountForMap, JObject metadata)
        {
            string targetLedger = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.unlock_ledger_id;
            string accountLabel = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_label + assetId + " Settlement";
            string ledgerAccountName = assetId + Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.settlement_label;

            var ledgerAccount = new JObject
            {
                ["name"] = ledgerAccountName,
                ["currency"] = "USD",
                ["normal_balance"] = "debit",
                ["ledger_account_category_ids"] = JArray.FromObject(categoryIds),
                ["ledger_id"] = targetLedger,
                ["description"] = accountLabel
            };
            if (metadata != null && metadata.HasValues) ledgerAccount["metadata"] = metadata;
            string body = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ledgerAccount);
            string id = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
            ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, assetId, "backfill_create_ledger_account_settlement", id, "ledger_account", pipelineLabel, "settlement", assetId, amountForMap, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_url_prefix + id, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m, null);
            return id;
        }
        private static Task<string> CreateSettlementLedgerAccountAsync(string server, string assetId, string pipelineLabel, List<string> categoryIds, decimal amountForMap)
            => CreateSettlementLedgerAccountAsync(server, assetId, pipelineLabel, categoryIds, amountForMap, null);

        
        private static async Task<string> CreateInvestmentPaymentLedgerTransactionAsync(string assetId, string pipelineLabel, string investmentPaymentAccountId, string contraLedgerAccountId, decimal amount, string fileNum, string effectiveDate, string fundingDate)
        {
            if (amount <= 0m) return null;
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(investmentPaymentAccountId) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(contraLedgerAccountId))
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Missing ledger account id(s) for Asset {assetId} Investment Payment backfill.");
                return null;
            }

            int amountInt = ToInt(amount);
            var metadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fileNum)) metadata["file_num"] = fileNum;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(effectiveDate)) metadata["effective_date"] = effectiveDate;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fundingDate)) metadata["funding_date"] = fundingDate;
            metadata["investment_payment"] = amount.ToString();
            metadata["initiated_by"] = "Backfill.cs";
            metadata["modern_treasury_view"] = "backfill";

            var ltIP = new JObject
            {
                ["description"] = $"Backfill Investment Payment for Asset {assetId}",
                ["status"] = "posted",
                ["ledger_entries"] = new JArray
                {
                    new JObject { ["amount"] = amountInt, ["direction"] = "debit",  ["ledger_account_id"] = investmentPaymentAccountId, ["metadata"] = metadata },
                    new JObject { ["amount"] = amountInt, ["direction"] = "credit", ["ledger_account_id"] = contraLedgerAccountId }
                }
            };

            string ltIPBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ltIP);
            string ltIPId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
            string ltIPUrl = "https:

            ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "backfill_create_investment_payment_ledger_transaction", ltIPId, "ledger_transaction", pipelineLabel, "_Backfill_IP", assetId, amount, ltIPUrl, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m, null);
            return ltIPId;
        }

        private static async Task<string> CreatePurchaseProceedsInverseTransactionAsync(
            string assetId,
            string pipelineLabel,
            string purchaseProceedsAccountId,
            string investmentPaymentAccountId,
            string gainOnSaleAccountId,
            decimal purchaseProceeds,
            decimal oface,
            decimal gainOnSale,
            string tradeId,
            string accountId,
            string tradeDate,
            string settleDate,
            decimal price,
            string investorMemoAccountName)
        {
            if (purchaseProceeds <= 0m) return null;
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(purchaseProceedsAccountId) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(investmentPaymentAccountId) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(gainOnSaleAccountId))
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Missing ledger account id(s) for Asset {assetId} Purchase Proceeds inverse transaction.");
                return null;
            }

            int ppInt = ToInt(purchaseProceeds);
            int ipInt = ToInt(oface);
            int gosInt = ToInt(gainOnSale);

            var metadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tradeId)) metadata["trade_id"] = tradeId;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(accountId)) metadata["account_id"] = accountId;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tradeDate)) metadata["trade_date"] = tradeDate;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(settleDate)) metadata["settle_date"] = settleDate;
            if (price > 0m) metadata["price"] = price.ToString();
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(investorMemoAccountName)) metadata["investor_memo_account_name"] = investorMemoAccountName;
            metadata["investment_payment"] = oface.ToString();
            metadata["purchase_proceeds"] = purchaseProceeds.ToString();
            metadata["gain_on_sale"] = gainOnSale.ToString();
            metadata["initiated_by"] = "Backfill.cs";
            metadata["modern_treasury_view"] = "backfill";


            var entries = new JArray
            {
                new JObject { ["amount"] = ppInt, ["direction"] = "debit",  ["ledger_account_id"] = purchaseProceedsAccountId, ["metadata"] = metadata.DeepClone() },
                new JObject { ["amount"] = ipInt, ["direction"] = "credit", ["ledger_account_id"] = investmentPaymentAccountId, ["metadata"] = metadata.DeepClone() },
                new JObject { ["amount"] = gosInt, ["direction"] = "credit", ["ledger_account_id"] = gainOnSaleAccountId, ["metadata"] = metadata.DeepClone() }
            };

            if (purchaseProceeds < oface)
            {
                int diffInt = ToInt(oface - purchaseProceeds);
                string contraId = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.backfill_contra_account_id;
                entries.Add(new JObject { ["amount"] = diffInt, ["direction"] = "debit", ["ledger_account_id"] = contraId, ["metadata"] = metadata.DeepClone() });
            }

            var lt = new JObject
            {
                ["description"] = $"Backfill Purchase Proceeds for Asset {assetId}",
                ["status"] = "posted",
                ["ledger_entries"] = entries
            };

            string body = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(lt);
            string ltId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
            string url = "https:

            ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "backfill_create_purchase_proceeds_inverse_ledger_transaction", ltId, "ledger_transaction", pipelineLabel, "_Backfill_PP_Inverse", assetId, purchaseProceeds, url, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m, null);
            return ltId;
        }

        private static async Task<string> CreateInvestorLedgerAccountSettlementTransactionsAsync(
            string assetId,
            string pipelineLabel,
            string investmentPaymentAccountId,
            string settlementAccountId,
            string contraLedgerAccountId,
            decimal oface,
            string fileNum,
            string effectiveDate,
            string fundingDate,
            string finalDispositionDate,
            decimal netSettlementPayment,
            string settlementType,
            string settlementReason)
        {
            if (oface <= 0m && netSettlementPayment <= 0m) return null;
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(investmentPaymentAccountId) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(contraLedgerAccountId) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(settlementAccountId))
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Missing ledger account id(s) for Asset {assetId} Settlement backfill.");
                return null;
            }

            int ofaceInt = ToInt(oface);
            int nspInt = ToInt(netSettlementPayment);

            var metadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fileNum)) metadata["file_num"] = fileNum;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(effectiveDate)) metadata["effective_date"] = effectiveDate;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fundingDate)) metadata["funding_date"] = fundingDate;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(finalDispositionDate)) metadata["final_disposition_date"] = finalDispositionDate;
            if (netSettlementPayment > 0m) metadata["net_settlement_payment"] = netSettlementPayment.ToString();
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(settlementType)) metadata["settlement_type"] = settlementType;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(settlementReason)) metadata["settlement_reason"] = settlementReason;

            var entries = new JArray();
            if (ofaceInt > 0)
            {
                
                entries.Add(new JObject { ["amount"] = ofaceInt, ["direction"] = "debit",  ["ledger_account_id"] = contraLedgerAccountId });
                entries.Add(new JObject { ["amount"] = ofaceInt, ["direction"] = "credit", ["ledger_account_id"] = investmentPaymentAccountId, ["metadata"] = metadata.DeepClone() });
            }
            if (nspInt > 0)
            {
                
                entries.Add(new JObject { ["amount"] = nspInt, ["direction"] = "debit",  ["ledger_account_id"] = settlementAccountId, ["metadata"] = metadata.DeepClone() });
                entries.Add(new JObject { ["amount"] = nspInt, ["direction"] = "credit", ["ledger_account_id"] = contraLedgerAccountId });
            }

            if (entries.Count == 0) return null;

            var lt = new JObject
            {
                ["description"] = $"Backfill Settlement transactions for Asset {assetId}",
                ["status"] = "posted",
                ["ledger_entries"] = entries
            };

            try
            {
                string body = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(lt);
                string ltId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
                string ltUrl = "https:
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "backfill_create_investment_payment_settlement_ledger_transaction", ltId, "ledger_transaction", pipelineLabel, "_Backfill_Settlement", assetId, oface + netSettlementPayment, ltUrl, "Backfill.cs", null, 0m, null);
                return ltId;
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create Settlement ledger transactions for Asset {assetId}. {ex.Message}");
                return null;
            }
        }

        public static async Task AddInvestmentPaymentToCategoryAsync(DataTable assetCategoryTable)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();
            if (assetCategoryTable == null || assetCategoryTable.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No rows supplied.");
                return;
            }

            
            string FindColumn(params string[] candidates)
            {
                foreach (var cand in candidates)
                {
                    if (assetCategoryTable.Columns.Contains(cand)) return cand;
                    foreach (DataColumn col in assetCategoryTable.Columns)
                        if (string.Equals(col.ColumnName, cand, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                            return col.ColumnName;
                }
                return null;
            }

            string assetCol = FindColumn("asset_id");
            string categoryCol = FindColumn("ledger_account_category_id", "category_id", "target_category_id");

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(assetCol) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(categoryCol))
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Required columns not found. Expected 'asset_id' and one of 'ledger_account_category_id', 'category_id', 'target_category_id'.");
                return;
            }

            var seen = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

            foreach (DataRow row in assetCategoryTable.Rows)
            {
                if (row == null) continue;
                string assetId = row[assetCol]?.ToString()?.Trim();
                string targetCategoryId = row[categoryCol]?.ToString()?.Trim();
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(assetId) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(targetCategoryId))
                    continue;

                string dedupKey = assetId + "|" + targetCategoryId;
                if (!seen.Add(dedupKey))
                    continue;

                try
                {
                    string investmentPaymentLedgerAccountId = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_InvestmentPayment_Live(assetId);
                    if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(investmentPaymentLedgerAccountId))
                    {
                        Console.WriteLine($"No Investment Payment ledger account found for asset_id {assetId}.");
                        continue;
                    }

                    
                    string url = $"https:
                    string body = "{}"; 

                    var client = new ModernTreasuryClient2();
                    await client.SendHttpRequestAsync(url, body, "Put");

                    Console.WriteLine($"PUT mapped Investment Payment ledger account {investmentPaymentLedgerAccountId} for asset {assetId} to category {targetCategoryId}.");
                }
                catch (Exception ex)
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Failed to update Investment Payment category for asset {assetId}. {ex.Message}");
                }
            }
        }

        
        private static decimal CalculateGainOnSale(decimal purchaseProceeds, decimal oface)
        {
            decimal diff = Math.Round(purchaseProceeds - oface, 2);
            return diff < 0m ? 0m : diff;
        }

        private static int ToInt(decimal amount) => Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(amount, 2) * 100);

        private static decimal GetDecimal(DataRow row, string col)
        {
            if (!row.Table.Columns.Contains(col) || row[col] == DBNull.Value) return 0m;
            try
            {
                return Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(row[col]), 2);
            }
            catch
            {
                var s = row[col]?.ToString();
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(s)) return 0m;
                s = s.Replace("$", string.Empty).Replace(",", string.Empty).Trim();
                if (decimal.TryParse(s, NumberStyles.Number | NumberStyles.AllowCurrencySymbol, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, out var m))
                    return Math.Round(m, 2);
                if (decimal.TryParse(s, NumberStyles.Number | NumberStyles.AllowCurrencySymbol, CultureInfo.CurrentCulture, out m))
                    return Math.Round(m, 2);
                return 0m;
            }
        }

        private static bool HasNonEmptyValue(DataRow row, string col)
        {
            if (!row.Table.Columns.Contains(col)) return false;
            var v = row[col];
            if (v == null || v == DBNull.Value) return false;
            if (v is string s) return !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(s);
            return true;
        }

        private static decimal GetDecimalWithTextFallback(DataRow row, string primaryCol, string textAltCol)
        {
            if (HasNonEmptyValue(row, primaryCol)) return GetDecimal(row, primaryCol);
            if (HasNonEmptyValue(row, textAltCol)) return GetDecimal(row, textAltCol);
            return 0m;
        }

        private static string GetString(DataRow row, string col)
        {
            if (!row.Table.Columns.Contains(col) || row[col] == DBNull.Value) return null;
            var s = row[col].ToString();
            return string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(s) ? null : s;
        }

        private static async Task<string> AddExistingLedgerAccountTransactionAsync(
            string assetId,
            string pipelineLabel,
            string accountNameFragment,
            decimal amount,
            string fileNum = null,
            string effectiveDate = null,
            string fundingDate = null,
            string tradeId = null,
            string accountId = null,
            string tradeDate = null,
            string settleDate = null,
            decimal price = 0m,
            string investorMemoAccountName = null,
            decimal purchaseProceeds = 0m,
            decimal oface = 0m,
            decimal gainOnSale = 0m)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(assetId) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(accountNameFragment)) return null;
            if (amount <= 0m) return null;

            
            string ledgerAccountId = await ModernTreasuryUtils.FindLedgerAccountIdByNameAndAssetIdAsync(assetId, accountNameFragment);
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(ledgerAccountId))
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"No existing ledger account found for Asset {assetId} with name containing '{accountNameFragment}'.");
                return null;
            }

            string contraLedgerAccountId = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.backfill_contra_account_id;
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(contraLedgerAccountId))
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Contra ledger account id missing; cannot create transaction.");
                return null;
            }

            int amtInt = ToInt(amount);
            var metadata = new JObject { ["asset_id"] = assetId };

            bool isIP = accountNameFragment.IndexOf("Investment Payment", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) >= 0;
            bool isGOS = accountNameFragment.IndexOf("Gain on Sale", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) >= 0;
            bool isPP = accountNameFragment.IndexOf("Purchase Proceeds", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) >= 0;

            if (isIP)
            {
                
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fileNum)) metadata["file_num"] = fileNum;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(effectiveDate)) metadata["effective_date"] = effectiveDate;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fundingDate)) metadata["funding_date"] = fundingDate;
                if (oface > 0m) metadata["investment_payment"] = oface.ToString();
            }
            else if (isGOS || isPP)
            {
                
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tradeId)) metadata["trade_id"] = tradeId;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(accountId)) metadata["account_id"] = accountId;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tradeDate)) metadata["trade_date"] = tradeDate;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(settleDate)) metadata["settle_date"] = settleDate;
                if (price > 0m) metadata["price"] = price.ToString();
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(investorMemoAccountName)) metadata["investor_memo_account_name"] = investorMemoAccountName;
                metadata["initiated_by"] = "Backfill.cs";
                metadata["modern_treasury_view"] = "backfill";
                if (oface > 0m) metadata["investment_payment"] = oface.ToString();
                if (purchaseProceeds > 0m) metadata["purchase_proceeds"] = purchaseProceeds.ToString();
                if (gainOnSale > 0m) metadata["gain_on_sale"] = gainOnSale.ToString();
            }
            else
            {
                
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fileNum)) metadata["file_num"] = fileNum;
                metadata["initiated_by"] = "Backfill.cs";
            }

            var lt = new JObject
            {
                ["description"] = $"Backfill Add Transaction to Existing '{accountNameFragment}' for Asset {assetId}",
                ["status"] = "posted",
                ["ledger_entries"] = new JArray
                {
                    new JObject { ["amount"] = amtInt, ["direction"] = "debit",  ["ledger_account_id"] = ledgerAccountId, ["metadata"] = metadata },
                    new JObject { ["amount"] = amtInt, ["direction"] = "credit", ["ledger_account_id"] = contraLedgerAccountId }
                }
            };

            try
            {
                string body = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(lt);
                string ltId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
                string ltUrl = "https:
                string suffix = "_Backfill_Existing_" + accountNameFragment.Replace(" ", string.Empty);
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, assetId, "backfill_add_existing_ledger_transaction", ltId, "ledger_transaction", pipelineLabel, suffix, assetId, amount, ltUrl, "Backfill.cs", null, amount, fundingDate);
                return ltId;
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create ledger transaction for existing account '{accountNameFragment}' Asset {assetId}. {ex.Message}");
                return null;
            }
        }


    }
}

namespace ModernTreasuryLib
{
    public class Connectors
    {
        public static string GetMTToken()
        {
            var base64auth = Convert.ToBase64String(Encoding.ASCII.GetBytes($"{ModernTreasuryLib.Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UNLOCK_MT_ORGANIZATION_ID}:{ModernTreasuryLib.Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UNLOCK_MT_API_KEY}"));
            return base64auth;
        }


    }
}

using static ModernTreasuryLib.MTApiObjects;
using static ModernTreasuryLib.ModernTreasuryClient;
namespace ModernTreasuryLib
{
    public class MTDrawGlobals
    {
        public static string server = CommonInterfaces.Constants.Database.UAM_SQL_SERVER_LABEL;
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
    }

    public class ModernTreasury_Draw
    {
        public static async Task CreateDrawMTAssetsAsync(DataTable assetsForMT, DataTable ceBreakdownDataForMT, DataTable faBreakdownDataForMT, DataTable faHiBreakdownDataForMT, DataTable funding_value_date)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();

            
            
            
            string FUNDING_DATE_str = DateTime.Parse(funding_value_date.Rows[0]["VALUE_DATE_INPUT"].ToString()).ToString("M/d/yyyy", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);

            
            DataColumn funding_date = assetsForMT.Columns.Add("funding_date", typeof(String));
            foreach (DataRow r in assetsForMT.Rows)
            {
                r["funding_date"] = FUNDING_DATE_str;
            }

            
            DataTable assets_and_fees = assetsForMT.Copy();
            DataColumn file_number = assets_and_fees.Columns.Add("file_number", typeof(String));
            DataColumn appraisal_fee = assets_and_fees.Columns.Add("appraisal_fee", typeof(String));
            DataColumn origination_fee = assets_and_fees.Columns.Add("origination_fee", typeof(String));
            DataColumn concessions = assets_and_fees.Columns.Add("concessions", typeof(String));
            DataColumn total_funding_wire_amount = assets_and_fees.Columns.Add("total_funding_wire_amount", typeof(String));

            foreach (DataRow assetRow in assets_and_fees.Rows)
            {
                string assetId = assetRow["asset_id"].ToString();

                foreach (DataRow ceRow in ceBreakdownDataForMT.Rows)
                {
                    if (ceRow["asset_id"].ToString() == assetId)
                    {
                        assetRow["appraisal_fee"] = ceRow["APPRAISAL FEE AMOUNT"];
                        assetRow["origination_fee"] = ceRow["ORIGINATION FEE"];
                        assetRow["file_number"] = ceRow["FILE NUMBER"];
                        assetRow["concessions"] = ceRow["CONCESSIONS"];
                        assetRow["total_funding_wire_amount"] = ceRow["TOTAL WIRE AMOUNT"];
                    }
                }

                foreach (DataRow faRow in faBreakdownDataForMT.Rows)
                {
                    if (faRow["asset_id"].ToString() == assetId)
                    {
                        assetRow["appraisal_fee"] = faRow["APPRAISAL FEE AMOUNT"];
                        assetRow["origination_fee"] = faRow["ORIGINATION FEE"];
                        assetRow["file_number"] = faRow["FILE NUMBER"];
                        assetRow["concessions"] = faRow["CONCESSIONS"];
                        assetRow["total_funding_wire_amount"] = faRow["TOTAL WIRE AMOUNT"];

                    }
                }

                foreach (DataRow fahiRow in faHiBreakdownDataForMT.Rows)
                {
                    if (fahiRow["asset_id"].ToString() == assetId)
                    {
                        assetRow["appraisal_fee"] = fahiRow["APPRAISAL FEE AMOUNT"];
                        assetRow["origination_fee"] = fahiRow["ORIGINATION FEE"];
                        assetRow["file_number"] = fahiRow["FILE NUMBER"];
                        assetRow["concessions"] = fahiRow["CONCESSIONS"];
                        assetRow["total_funding_wire_amount"] = fahiRow["TOTAL WIRE AMOUNT"];
                    }
                }
            }

            
            DataTable cet_assets_and_fees = assets_and_fees.Clone();
            DataTable fa_assets_and_fees = assets_and_fees.Clone();
            DataTable fa_hi_assets_and_fees = assets_and_fees.Clone();
            

            foreach (DataRow assets_fees_row in assets_and_fees.Rows)
            {
                var titleObj = assets_fees_row["TITLE_ESCROW_COMPANY"];
                var stateObj = assets_fees_row["STATE"];
                if ((titleObj == null || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(titleObj.ToString()))
                    ||
                    (stateObj == null || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(stateObj.ToString()))
                    )
                {
                    continue;
                }
                else
                { 
                    string title = (Convert.ToString(assets_fees_row["TITLE_ESCROW_COMPANY"]) ?? string.Empty).Trim();
                    string state = assets_and_fees.Columns.Contains("STATE") ? (assets_fees_row["STATE"]?.ToString().Trim() ?? string.Empty) : string.Empty;

                    if (string.Equals(title, "ClearEdge Title", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                    {
                        cet_assets_and_fees.ImportRow(assets_fees_row);
                    }
                    
                    else if (string.Equals(title, "First American Title", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                             && string.Equals(state, "HI", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                    {
                        fa_hi_assets_and_fees.ImportRow(assets_fees_row);
                    }
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    else if (string.Equals(title, "First American TItle", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                    {
                        fa_assets_and_fees.ImportRow(assets_fees_row);
                    }
                }
            }


            
            string asset_id_string = "";

            
            decimal totalInvestmentAmount = 0;
            foreach (DataRow row in assets_and_fees.Rows)
            {
                string investmentPaymentAmount = row["investment_payment"].ToString();
                totalInvestmentAmount = totalInvestmentAmount + Convert.ToDecimal(investmentPaymentAmount);
            }


            
            foreach (DataRow row in assets_and_fees.Rows)
            {
                if (asset_id_string != "")
                {
                    asset_id_string = asset_id_string + "," + row["asset_id"].ToString();
                }
                else
                {
                    asset_id_string = asset_id_string + row["asset_id"].ToString();
                }

                string asset_id = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                string pipelineLabel = row["customer_pipeline_label_max"].ToString();
                string investmentPaymentAmount = row["investment_payment"].ToString();
                string orig_fee = row["origination_fee"].ToString();
                string appr_fee = row["appraisal_fee"].ToString();
                string file_num = row["file_number"].ToString();
                string title_escrow_company = row["TITLE_ESCROW_COMPANY"].ToString();
                string concession = row["concessions"].ToString();
                string total_funding_wire = row["total_funding_wire_amount"].ToString();

                
                

                if (asset_id == "97932149957680" || asset_id == "96855346795573")
                {
                    var cool = 1;
                }

                
                string createdDatedCategoryFundingDatesId = await CreateDatedFundingDatesCategoryAsync(FUNDING_DATE_str);
                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(createdDatedCategoryFundingDatesId))
                {
                    bool insert_dated_funding_cat_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id, "create_funding_date_category", createdDatedCategoryFundingDatesId, "category", pipelineLabel, null, asset_id, totalInvestmentAmount, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + createdDatedCategoryFundingDatesId, "Drawflow.cs", title_escrow_company, totalInvestmentAmount, FUNDING_DATE_str);
                    if (insert_dated_funding_cat_done != true)
                    {
                        Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for {FUNDING_DATE_str} funding date category");
                    }
                }
                else

                {
                    break;
                }




                
                string createdCategoryId = await CreateLedgerAssetCategoryAsync(asset_id, pipelineLabel, FUNDING_DATE_str);

                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(createdCategoryId))
                {
                    bool insert_category_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id, "create_ledger_category", createdCategoryId, "category", pipelineLabel, null, asset_id, totalInvestmentAmount, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + createdCategoryId, "Drawflow.cs", title_escrow_company, totalInvestmentAmount, FUNDING_DATE_str);
                    if (insert_category_done)
                    {
                        
                        string subCategoryId_funding = await CreateLedgerFundingSubCategoryAsync("Funding", createdCategoryId, asset_id, pipelineLabel, FUNDING_DATE_str);
                        if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(subCategoryId_funding))
                        {
                            bool insert_subcategory_funding_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id, "create_ledger_funding_subcategory", subCategoryId_funding, "subcategory", pipelineLabel, null, asset_id, 0, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_category_url_prefix + subCategoryId_funding, "Drawflow.cs", title_escrow_company, 0, FUNDING_DATE_str);
                            
                            await CreateLedgerAccountsAsync(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id, pipelineLabel, subCategoryId_funding, investmentPaymentAmount, assets_and_fees, title_escrow_company, FUNDING_DATE_str);
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for asset_id: {asset_id} funding subcategory");
                        }
                                                
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for asset_id: {asset_id}");
                    }
                } 
                else
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create category for asset_id: {asset_id}");
                    
                }


                
                
                if (title_escrow_company == "ClearEdge Title")
                {
                    string createdOriginationFeeEPId = await CreateCETInitialFeeExpectedPaymentAsync(asset_id, orig_fee, "Origination", title_escrow_company);
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(createdOriginationFeeEPId))
                    {
                        bool insert_orgination_fee_EP_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id, "create_initial_expected_payment_origination_fee", createdOriginationFeeEPId, "expected_payment", pipelineLabel, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.origination_fee_label, asset_id, Convert.ToDecimal(orig_fee), Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + createdOriginationFeeEPId, "Drawflow.cs", title_escrow_company, Convert.ToDecimal(orig_fee), FUNDING_DATE_str);
                        if (insert_orgination_fee_EP_done != true)
                        {
                            Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for asset_id: {asset_id} origination fee (initial) expected payment");
                        }
                    }
                    else

                    {
                        break;
                    }

                    
                    string createdAppraisalFeeEPId = await CreateCETInitialFeeExpectedPaymentAsync(asset_id, appr_fee, "Appraisal", title_escrow_company);
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(createdAppraisalFeeEPId))
                    {
                        bool insert_appraisal_fee_EP_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id, "create_initial_expected_payment_appraisal_fee", createdAppraisalFeeEPId, "expected_payment", pipelineLabel, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.appraisal_fee_label, asset_id, Convert.ToDecimal(appr_fee), Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + createdAppraisalFeeEPId, "Drawflow.cs", title_escrow_company, Convert.ToDecimal(appr_fee), FUNDING_DATE_str);
                        if (insert_appraisal_fee_EP_done != true)
                        {
                            Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for asset_id: {asset_id} origination fee (initial) expected payment");
                        }
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        break;
                    }

                    
                    
                    if (Convert.ToDecimal(row["concessions"].ToString()) != 0)
                    {
                        decimal concession_value = Convert.ToDecimal(concession);
                        
                        string patchedOrigForConcessionEPId = await PatchCETOriginationFeeExpectedPaymentForConcessionAsync(asset_id, orig_fee, concession_value, title_escrow_company);
                        if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(patchedOrigForConcessionEPId))
                        {
                            decimal orig_minus_concession = Convert.ToDecimal(orig_fee) - Math.Abs(concession_value);
                            bool insert_concession_fee_update_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id, "update_cet_concessions_origination_fee", patchedOrigForConcessionEPId, "expected_payment", pipelineLabel, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.origination_fee_label, asset_id, Convert.ToDecimal(orig_minus_concession), Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + patchedOrigForConcessionEPId, "Drawflow.cs", title_escrow_company, Convert.ToDecimal(orig_minus_concession), FUNDING_DATE_str);
                            if (insert_concession_fee_update_done != true)
                            {
                                Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for asset_id: {asset_id} origination fee concession adjustment expected payment");
                            }
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
                else if (title_escrow_company == "First American Title")
                {
                    decimal megerd_o_a_fee = Convert.ToDecimal(orig_fee) + Convert.ToDecimal(appr_fee);

                    
                    string createdFAFeeEPId = await CreateFAFeeExpectedPaymentAsync(asset_id, orig_fee, appr_fee, title_escrow_company);
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(createdFAFeeEPId))
                    {
                        bool insert_appraisal_fee_EP_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id, "create_fa_expected_payment_orig_appraisal_combo_fee", createdFAFeeEPId, "expected_payment", pipelineLabel, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.merged_o_a_fee_label, asset_id, Convert.ToDecimal(megerd_o_a_fee), Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + createdFAFeeEPId, "Drawflow.cs", title_escrow_company, Convert.ToDecimal(megerd_o_a_fee), FUNDING_DATE_str);
                        if (insert_appraisal_fee_EP_done != true)
                        {
                            Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for asset_id: {asset_id} fa expected payment");
                        }
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        break;
                    }

                    
                    
                    if (Convert.ToDecimal(row["concessions"].ToString()) != 0)
                    {
                        decimal concession_value = Convert.ToDecimal(concession);
                        
                        string patchedFAForConcessionEPId = await PatchFAExpectedPaymentForConcessionAsync(asset_id, orig_fee, appr_fee, concession_value, title_escrow_company);
                        if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(patchedFAForConcessionEPId))
                        {
                            decimal orig_minus_concession = Convert.ToDecimal(orig_fee) - Math.Abs(concession_value);
                            decimal merged_adjusted = orig_minus_concession + Convert.ToDecimal(appr_fee);
                            bool insert_concession_fee_update_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id, "update_fa_concessions_merged_fee", patchedFAForConcessionEPId, "expected_payment", pipelineLabel, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.merged_o_a_fee_label, asset_id, Convert.ToDecimal(merged_adjusted), Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + patchedFAForConcessionEPId, "Drawflow.cs", title_escrow_company, Convert.ToDecimal(merged_adjusted), FUNDING_DATE_str);
                            if (insert_concession_fee_update_done != true)
                            {
                                Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for asset_id: {asset_id} fa merged orig+appr concession adjustment expected payment");
                            }
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }


                
                if (Convert.ToDecimal(row["concessions"].ToString()) != 0)
                {
                    decimal concession_value = Convert.ToDecimal(concession);
                    
                    string ledgerTransactionForConcessionId = await CreateLedgerTransactionForConcessionAsync(asset_id, orig_fee, concession_value, title_escrow_company);
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(ledgerTransactionForConcessionId))
                    {
                        bool insert_concession_ledger_transaction_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id, "create_ledger_transaction_for_concession", ledgerTransactionForConcessionId, "ledger_transaction", pipelineLabel, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_transaction_label, asset_id, Convert.ToDecimal(concession_value), Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_transaction_url_prefix + ledgerTransactionForConcessionId, "Drawflow.cs", title_escrow_company, Convert.ToDecimal(concession_value), FUNDING_DATE_str);
                        if (insert_concession_ledger_transaction_done != true)
                        {
                            Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for asset_id: {asset_id} origination fee concession adjustment expected payment");
                        }
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }


       


            
            
            int totalIntInvestmentAmount = Convert.ToInt32(totalInvestmentAmount * 100);
            
            DataColumn total_int_investment_amount = assetsForMT.Columns.Add("total_int_investment_amount", typeof(Int32));
            foreach (DataRow r in assetsForMT.Rows)
            {
                r["total_int_investment_amount"] = totalIntInvestmentAmount;
            }

            
            decimal haircutAmount = Convert.ToDecimal(totalInvestmentAmount) * 0.10m; 

            
            DataColumn haircut_amt = assetsForMT.Columns.Add("haircut_amt", typeof(Decimal));
            foreach (DataRow r in assetsForMT.Rows)
            {
                r["haircut_amt"] = haircutAmount;
            }

            
            int haircutIntAmount = Convert.ToInt32(haircutAmount * 100);
            DataColumn haircut_int_amount = assetsForMT.Columns.Add("haircut_int_amount", typeof(Int32));
            foreach (DataRow r in assetsForMT.Rows)
            {
                r["haircut_int_amount"] = haircutIntAmount;
            }

            
            decimal drawAmount = Convert.ToDecimal(totalInvestmentAmount) * 0.90m; 
            
            DataColumn draw_amount = assetsForMT.Columns.Add("draw_amount", typeof(Decimal));
            foreach (DataRow r in assetsForMT.Rows)
            {
                r["draw_amount"] = drawAmount;
            }

            int drawIntAmount = Convert.ToInt32(drawAmount * 100);
            
            DataColumn draw_int_amount = assetsForMT.Columns.Add("draw_int_amount", typeof(Int32));
            foreach (DataRow r in assetsForMT.Rows)
            {
                r["draw_int_amount"] = drawIntAmount;
            }

            
            
            
            

            
            
            string createdHaircutEPId = await CreateHaircutExpectedPaymentAsync(assetsForMT);
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(createdHaircutEPId))
            {
                bool insert_haircut_ep_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, null, "haircut_expected_payment", createdHaircutEPId, "expected_payment", null, null, asset_id_string, haircutAmount, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + createdHaircutEPId, "Drawflow.cs", null, haircutAmount, FUNDING_DATE_str);
                if (insert_haircut_ep_done != true)
                {
                    Console.WriteLine("Failed to insert MT mapping for haircut expected payment");
                }
            }
            else 
            {
                DXMessageBox.Show("Haircut for funding date " + FUNDING_DATE_str + " failed to load in MT");
                
                System.Diagnostics.Process.GetCurrentProcess().Kill();
            }


            
            string createdWarehouseExpectedPaymentId = await CreateWarehouseLineDrawExpectedPaymentAsync(assetsForMT);
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(createdWarehouseExpectedPaymentId))
            {
                bool insert_warehouse_draw_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, null, "warehouse_draw_expected_payment", createdWarehouseExpectedPaymentId, "expected_payment", null, null, asset_id_string, drawAmount, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + createdWarehouseExpectedPaymentId, "Drawflow.cs", null, drawAmount, FUNDING_DATE_str);
                if (insert_warehouse_draw_done != true)
                {
                    Console.WriteLine("Failed to insert MT log for warehouse draw expected payment for funding date "+ FUNDING_DATE_str);
                }
            }
            else
            {
                DXMessageBox.Show("Warehouse Draw for funding date " + FUNDING_DATE_str + " failed to load in MT");
                
                System.Diagnostics.Process.GetCurrentProcess().Kill();

            }
           

            
            
            
            
            

            


            
            
            


            
            

            
            var titleCompanies = new List<(string name, DataTable table)>
            {
                ("cet", cet_assets_and_fees),
                ("fa", fa_assets_and_fees),
                ("fa_hi", fa_hi_assets_and_fees)
                
                
                
            };

            foreach (var tc in titleCompanies)
            {
                
                if (tc.table == null || tc.table.Rows.Count == 0)
                    continue;

                
                string tcAssetIdString = "";
                decimal tcTotalAmount = 0m;
                foreach (DataRow r in tc.table.Rows)
                {
                    string aid = r["asset_id"]?.ToString();
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(aid))
                        tcAssetIdString = string.IsNullOrEmpty(tcAssetIdString) ? aid : tcAssetIdString + "," + aid;

                    decimal ip = 0m;
                    decimal.TryParse((r["investment_payment"] ?? "0").ToString(), out ip);
                    tcTotalAmount += ip;
                }

                
                string createdExpectedPaymentId = await CreateTitleCoWireExpectedPaymentAsync(tc.table, tc.name, FUNDING_DATE_str);
                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(createdExpectedPaymentId))
                {
                    
                    bool insert_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(
                        MTDrawGlobals.server,
                        null,
                        "Title_Co_wire_expected_payment_" + tc.name,
                        createdExpectedPaymentId,
                        "expected_payment",
                        null,
                        null,
                        tcAssetIdString,
                        tcTotalAmount,
                        Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + createdExpectedPaymentId,
                        "Drawflow.cs",
                        tc.name,
                        tcTotalAmount,
                        FUNDING_DATE_str
                    );
                    
                    if (insert_done != true)
                    {
                        Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for title company: {tc.name} {FUNDING_DATE_str}");
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    DXMessageBox.Show("Title Co Funding wire to " + tc.name + " for funding date " + FUNDING_DATE_str + " failed to load in MT");
                    
                    System.Diagnostics.Process.GetCurrentProcess().Kill();

                }
            }

            DXMessageBox.Show("Funding loaded into Modern Treasury for Funding Date: " + FUNDING_DATE_str);

            
            
        }

        private static async Task<string> CreateHaircutExpectedPaymentAsync(DataTable assetsForMT)
        {
            
            string receivingLedgerAccountUF2 = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UF2_funding_ledger_account_id;
            string sendingLedgerAccountUPS = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UPS_Cash_ledger_account_id;
            string TCB_internal_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_ups_account;

            string funding_date = assetsForMT.Rows[0]["funding_date"].ToString();
            int haircutIntAmount = (int)assetsForMT.Rows[0]["haircut_int_amount"];
            int haircutAmountCents = Convert.ToInt32(assetsForMT.Rows[0]["haircut_int_amount"]);
            string formattedHaricutCents = (haircutAmountCents / 100m).ToString("C2", CultureInfo.GetCultureInfo("en-US"));

            MTApiObjects.ExpectedPayment expectedPayment = new MTApiObjects.ExpectedPayment
            {
                ledger_transaction = new MTApiObjects.LedgerTransactionEP
                {
                    description = "Haircut Expected Payment to UF2",
                    ledger_entries = new List<MTApiObjects.LedgerEntryEP>
                    {
                        new MTApiObjects.LedgerEntryEP
                        {
                            amount = haircutIntAmount,
                            direction = "debit",
                            ledger_account_id = receivingLedgerAccountUF2
                        },
                        new MTApiObjects.LedgerEntryEP
                        {
                            amount = haircutIntAmount,
                            direction = "credit",
                            ledger_account_id = sendingLedgerAccountUPS
                        }
                    }
                },
                reconciliation_rule_variables = new List<MTApiObjects.ReconciliationRuleVariables>
                {
                    new MTApiObjects.ReconciliationRuleVariables
                    {
                        internal_account_id = TCB_internal_account_id,
                        direction = "credit",
                        amount_lower_bound = haircutIntAmount,
                        amount_upper_bound = haircutIntAmount
                    }
                },
                metadata = new Dictionary<string, string>()
                {
                    { "transaction_type", "haircut" },
                    { "initiated_by", "Drawflow.cs" },
                    { "haircut_amt", formattedHaricutCents.ToString() },
                    { "funding_date", funding_date },
                    { "type", "WIRE" },
                    { "full_description", "Haircut Expected Payment of " + formattedHaricutCents + " to UF2 for " + funding_date }
                }
            };

            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(expectedPayment);
            Console.WriteLine(requestBody);

            return await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
        }


        private static async Task<string> CreatePaymentOrderTitleCoWireAsync(DataTable assetsForMT)
        {

            string sourceLedgerAccountUF2 = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UF2_funding_ledger_account_id;
            
            string sourceAccountUF2 = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_payments_uf2_funding_account;
            string receivingAccountCET = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.CET_external_account_id;

            int totalIntInvestmentAmount = (int)assetsForMT.Rows[0]["total_int_investment_amount"];

            MTApiObjects.PaymentOrder paymentOrder = new MTApiObjects.PaymentOrder
            {
                ledger_transaction = new MTApiObjects.LedgerTransactionPO
                {
                    ledger_entries = new List<MTApiObjects.LedgerEntryPO>
                    {
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                    }
                },
                nsfs_protected = false,
                type = "wire",
                amount = totalIntInvestmentAmount,
                direction = "credit",
                originating_account_id = sourceAccountUF2,
                receiving_account_id = receivingAccountCET,
                receiving_account_type = "internal_account"
            };

            JObject paymentOrderJo = JObject.FromObject(paymentOrder);

            foreach (DataRow row in assetsForMT.Rows)
            {
                string investment_payment_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_InvestmentPayment_Live(row["asset_id"].ToString());
                decimal indivdual_investment_payment = Convert.ToDecimal(row["investment_payment"].ToString());
                int int_individual_investment_payment = Convert.ToInt32(indivdual_investment_payment * 100);

                JObject ledgerEntryDebit = new JObject
                {
                    ["amount"] = int_individual_investment_payment,
                    ["direction"] = "debit",
                    ["ledger_account_id"] = investment_payment_mtid
                };

                
                ((JArray)paymentOrderJo["ledger_transaction"]["ledger_entries"]).Add(ledgerEntryDebit);

                JObject ledgerEntryCredit = new JObject
                {
                    ["amount"] = int_individual_investment_payment,
                    ["direction"] = "credit",
                    ["ledger_account_id"] = sourceLedgerAccountUF2
                };

                ((JArray)paymentOrderJo["ledger_transaction"]["ledger_entries"]).Add(ledgerEntryCredit);

                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
            }

            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(paymentOrderJo);
            Console.WriteLine(requestBody);
            return await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
        }


        private static async Task<string> CreateTitleCoWireExpectedPaymentAsync(DataTable EPAssetList, string title_co_short_name, string funding_date)
        {
            
            
            
            string sourceLedgerAccountUF2 = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UF2_funding_ledger_account_id;
            
            string sourceAccountUF2 = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uf2_funding_account;
            string receivingAccountCET = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.CET_external_account_id;

            
            decimal epTotalDecimal = 0m;
            int epTotalInt = 0;
            int wireAssetRowCount = EPAssetList?.Rows?.Count ?? 0;

            if (EPAssetList != null && EPAssetList.Rows.Count > 0)
            {
                foreach (DataRow r in EPAssetList.Rows)
                {
                    if (r == null) continue;

                    
                    object obj = r["investment_payment"];
                    if (obj == null || obj == DBNull.Value) continue;

                    decimal value;
                    
                    if (decimal.TryParse(obj.ToString(), NumberStyles.Number, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, out value))
                    {
                        epTotalDecimal += value;
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        
                        var cleaned = obj.ToString().Replace("$", "").Replace(",", "").Trim();
                        if (decimal.TryParse(cleaned, NumberStyles.Number, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, out value))
                        {
                            epTotalDecimal += value;
                        }
                    }
                }

                
                epTotalInt = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(epTotalDecimal * 100m, MidpointRounding.AwayFromZero));
            }

            
            string formattedEpTotalCents = (epTotalInt / 100m).ToString("C2", CultureInfo.GetCultureInfo("en-US"));


            MTApiObjects.ExpectedPayment expectedPayment = new MTApiObjects.ExpectedPayment
            {
                ledger_transaction = new MTApiObjects.LedgerTransactionEP
                {
                    description = title_co_short_name + " wire: 1 of " + wireAssetRowCount + " Assets Funded on " + funding_date.ToString(),
                    ledger_entries = new List<MTApiObjects.LedgerEntryEP>
                    {
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                    }
                },
                reconciliation_rule_variables = new List<MTApiObjects.ReconciliationRuleVariables>
                {
                    new MTApiObjects.ReconciliationRuleVariables
                    {
                        internal_account_id = sourceAccountUF2,
                        direction = "debit",
                        amount_lower_bound = epTotalInt,
                        amount_upper_bound = epTotalInt
                    }
                },
                metadata = new Dictionary<string, string>()
                {
                    { "transaction_type", "Funding Wire to " + title_co_short_name},
                    { "initiated_by", "Drawflow.cs" },
                    { "funding_wire_amount", formattedEpTotalCents.ToString() },
                    { "funding_date", funding_date.ToString() },
                    { "type", "WIRE" },
                    { "full_description", "Funding Wire to " + title_co_short_name + " for " + formattedEpTotalCents + " for " + funding_date.ToString() }
                }
            };

            JObject expectedPaymentJo = JObject.FromObject(expectedPayment);

            foreach (DataRow row in EPAssetList.Rows)
            {
                string investment_payment_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_InvestmentPayment_Live(row["asset_id"].ToString());
                decimal indivdual_investment_payment = Convert.ToDecimal(row["investment_payment"].ToString());
                int int_individual_investment_payment = Convert.ToInt32(indivdual_investment_payment * 100);

                JObject ledgerEntryDebit = new JObject
                {
                    ["amount"] = int_individual_investment_payment,
                    ["direction"] = "debit",
                    ["ledger_account_id"] = investment_payment_mtid
                };

                
                ((JArray)expectedPaymentJo["ledger_transaction"]["ledger_entries"]).Add(ledgerEntryDebit);

                JObject ledgerEntryCredit = new JObject
                {
                    ["amount"] = int_individual_investment_payment,
                    ["direction"] = "credit",
                    ["ledger_account_id"] = sourceLedgerAccountUF2
                };

                ((JArray)expectedPaymentJo["ledger_transaction"]["ledger_entries"]).Add(ledgerEntryCredit);

            }

            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(expectedPaymentJo);
            Console.WriteLine(requestBody);
            return await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
        }

        public static async Task<string> CreateLedgerAssetCategoryAsync(string assetId, string pipelineLabel, string funding_date)
        {
            string categoryLabel = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.category_label + assetId;
            string targetLedger = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.unlock_ledger_id;
            string targetTopCategory = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.all_unlock_assets_cat_id;

            var targetFundingDateCategoryId = await ModernTreasuryUtils.FindFundingDateCategoryIdByNameAsync(funding_date);
             
            
            MTApiObjects.LedgerAccountCategory ledgerAccountCategory = new MTApiObjects.LedgerAccountCategory
            {
                name = assetId,
                currency = "USD",
                normal_balance = "debit",
                ledger_account_category_ids = new List<string> { targetTopCategory, targetFundingDateCategoryId },
                ledger_id = targetLedger,
                description = categoryLabel,
                metadata = new Dictionary<string, string>
                {
                    { "funding_date", funding_date },
                    { "asset_id", assetId },
                    { "initiated_by", "Drawflow.cs" },
                    { "pipeline_label", pipelineLabel }
                }
            };
            ;
            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ledgerAccountCategory);

            return await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
        }

        private static async Task CreateLedgerAccountsAsync(string server, string asset_id, string pipelineLabel, string categoryId, string investmentPaymentAmount, DataTable assets_and_fees, string title_escrow_company, string funding_date)
        {
            string createdInvestmentPaymentId = await CreateLedgerAccountAsync("investment_payment", asset_id, pipelineLabel, categoryId, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.investment_payment_label, funding_date);
            bool insert_investment_payment_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, asset_id, "create_ledger_account_investment_payment", createdInvestmentPaymentId, "ledger_account", pipelineLabel, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.investment_payment_label, asset_id, 1, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_url_prefix  + createdInvestmentPaymentId, "Drawflow.cs", title_escrow_company, 0, funding_date);
            if (insert_investment_payment_done != true)
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for asset_id: {asset_id} investment payment");
            }

            string createdOriginationFeeId = await CreateLedgerAccountAsync("origination_fee", asset_id, pipelineLabel, categoryId, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.origination_fee_label, funding_date);
            bool insert_orginnation_fee_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, asset_id, "create_ledger_account_origination_fee", createdOriginationFeeId, "ledger_account", pipelineLabel, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.origination_fee_label, asset_id, 1, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_url_prefix + createdOriginationFeeId, "Drawflow.cs", title_escrow_company, 0, funding_date);
            if (insert_orginnation_fee_done != true)
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for asset_id: {asset_id} origination");
            }

            string createdAppraisalFeeId = await CreateLedgerAccountAsync("appraisal_fee", asset_id, pipelineLabel, categoryId, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.appraisal_fee_label, funding_date);
            bool insert_appraisal_fee_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, asset_id, "create_ledger_account_appraisal_fee", createdAppraisalFeeId, "ledger_account", pipelineLabel, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.appraisal_fee_label, asset_id, 1, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_url_prefix + createdAppraisalFeeId, "Drawflow.cs", title_escrow_company, 0, funding_date);
            if (insert_appraisal_fee_done != true)
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for asset_id: {asset_id} appraisal");
            }

            
            decimal concessionsObj = 0;
            foreach (DataRow r in assets_and_fees.Rows)
            {
                if ((r["asset_id"]?.ToString() ?? string.Empty) == asset_id)
                {
                    concessionsObj = Convert.ToDecimal(r["concessions"]);
                    break;
                }
            }

            
            if (concessionsObj != 0)
            {
                string createdConcessionsId = await CreateLedgerAccountAsync("concessions", asset_id, pipelineLabel, categoryId, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.concessions_label, funding_date);
                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(createdConcessionsId)) 
                { 
                    bool insert_concessions_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, asset_id, "create_ledger_account_concessions", createdConcessionsId, "ledger_account", pipelineLabel, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.concessions_label, asset_id, 1, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_url_prefix + createdConcessionsId, "Drawflow.cs", title_escrow_company, 0, funding_date);
                    if (insert_concessions_done != true)
                    {
                        Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for asset_id: {asset_id} concessions");
                    }
                    
                }
                else 
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create MT Concessions Ledger Account for asset_id: {asset_id} concessions");
                    DXMessageBox.Show($"Concession found but not created in MT for: {asset_id} {funding_date}");
                }
            }
        }


        public static async Task<string> CreateLedgerAccountAsync(string ledger_account_type, string assetId, string pipelineLabel, string categoryId, string labelSuffix, string funding_date)
        {
            string accountLabel = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_label + assetId + labelSuffix;
            string targetLedger = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.unlock_ledger_id;
            string ledgerAccountName = "";

            switch (ledger_account_type.ToUpper())
            {
                case "INVESTMENT_PAYMENT":
                    ledgerAccountName = assetId + Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.investment_payment_label;
                    break;

                case "ORIGINATION_FEE":
                    ledgerAccountName = assetId + Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.origination_fee_label;
                    break;

                case "APPRAISAL_FEE":
                    ledgerAccountName = assetId + Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.appraisal_fee_label;
                    break;
                case "CONCESSIONS":
                    ledgerAccountName = assetId + Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.concessions_label;
                    break;
            }

            MTApiObjects.LedgerAccount ledgerAccount = new MTApiObjects.LedgerAccount
            {
                name = ledgerAccountName,
                currency = "USD",
                
                ledger_account_category_ids = new List<string> { categoryId },
                ledger_id = targetLedger,
                description = accountLabel,
                metadata = new Dictionary<string, string>
                {
                    { "funding_date", funding_date },
                    { "asset_id", assetId },
                    { "initiated_by", "Drawflow.cs" },
                    { "pipeline_label", pipelineLabel }
                }
            };

            JObject ledgerAccountJo = JObject.FromObject(ledgerAccount);

            if (ledger_account_type == "investment_payment")
            {
                ledgerAccountJo["normal_balance"] = "debit"; 
            }
            else
            {
                ledgerAccountJo["normal_balance"] = "credit"; 
            }

            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ledgerAccountJo);
            return await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
        }


        private static async Task<string> CreateCETInitialFeeExpectedPaymentAsync(string asset_id, string fee_amount, string fee_type, string title_escrow_company)
        {
            string receivingLedgerAccountUPS = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UPS_Cash_ledger_account_id;
            string TCB_internal_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_ups_clearing_account; 

            
            string fee_mtid = "";
            if (fee_type == "Origination")
            {
                fee_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_OriginationFee_Live( asset_id.ToString());
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(fee_mtid))
                {
                    DXMessageBox.Show("Could not find Origination Fee ID in log!");
                    return null;
                }
            }
            else if (fee_type == "Appraisal")
            {
                fee_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_AppraisalFee_Live( asset_id.ToString());
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(fee_mtid))
                {
                    DXMessageBox.Show("Could not find Appraisal Fee ID in log!");
                    return null;
                }
            }
            else
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Unknown fee type: {fee_type} for asset_id: {asset_id.ToString()}");
            }

            decimal fee_amount_decimal = Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(fee_amount), 2);
            int fee_amount_int = Convert.ToInt32(fee_amount_decimal * 100); 
            string file_num = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetFileNumByAssetId(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id);
            
            string formattedFeeAmountCents = (fee_amount_int / 100m).ToString("C2", CultureInfo.GetCultureInfo("en-US"));

            MTApiObjects.ExpectedPayment expectedPayment = new MTApiObjects.ExpectedPayment
            {
                ledger_transaction = new MTApiObjects.LedgerTransactionEP
                {
                    description = fee_type + " Fee (Initial) Expected Payment of " + fee_amount,
                    ledger_entries = new List<MTApiObjects.LedgerEntryEP>
                    {
                        new MTApiObjects.LedgerEntryEP
                        {
                            amount = fee_amount_int,
                            direction = "debit",
                            ledger_account_id = receivingLedgerAccountUPS
                        },
                        new MTApiObjects.LedgerEntryEP
                        {
                            amount = fee_amount_int,
                            direction = "credit",
                            ledger_account_id = fee_mtid
                        }
                    }
                },
                reconciliation_rule_variables = new List<MTApiObjects.ReconciliationRuleVariables>
                {
                    new MTApiObjects.ReconciliationRuleVariables
                    {
                        internal_account_id = TCB_internal_account_id,
                        direction = "credit",
                        amount_lower_bound = fee_amount_int,
                        amount_upper_bound = fee_amount_int,
                        custom_identifiers = new Dictionary<string, string>
                        {
                            { "amount", fee_amount_decimal.ToString() },
                            { "fee_type", fee_type },
                            { "asset_id", asset_id },
                            { "file_num", file_num },
                            { "title_escrow_company", title_escrow_company }
                        }
                    }
                },
                metadata = new Dictionary<string, string>
                {
                    { "amount", formattedFeeAmountCents.ToString() },
                    { "fee_type", fee_type },
                    { "asset_id", asset_id },
                    { "file_num", file_num },
                    { "initiated_by", "Drawflow.cs" },
                    { "title_escrow_company", title_escrow_company },
                    { "full_description", fee_type + " Fee Expected Payment of " + formattedFeeAmountCents + " for Asset ID " + asset_id + " (" + file_num + ")" }

                }
            };

            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(expectedPayment);
            Console.WriteLine(requestBody);
            return await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
        }




        private static async Task<string> CreateFAFeeExpectedPaymentAsync(string asset_id, string origination_fee, string appraisal_fee, string title_escrow_company)
        {
            string receivingLedgerAccountUPS = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UPS_Cash_ledger_account_id;
            string TCB_internal_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_ups_clearing_account;

            
            
            string fee_origination_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_OriginationFee_Live( asset_id.ToString());
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(fee_origination_mtid))
            {
                DXMessageBox.Show("Could not find Origination Fee ID in log!");
                return null;
            }
            string fee_appraisal_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_AppraisalFee_Live( asset_id.ToString());
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(fee_appraisal_mtid))
            {
                DXMessageBox.Show("Could not find Appraisal Fee ID in log!");
                return null;
            }


            decimal fee_orig_amount_decimal = Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(origination_fee), 2);
            decimal fee_appr_amount_decimal = Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(appraisal_fee), 2);
            decimal merged_decimal_fee = fee_orig_amount_decimal + fee_appr_amount_decimal;

            int fee_orig_amount_int = Convert.ToInt32(fee_orig_amount_decimal * 100); 
            int fee_appr_amount_int = Convert.ToInt32(fee_appr_amount_decimal * 100); 
            int merged_int_fee = fee_orig_amount_int + fee_appr_amount_int;

            
            string file_num = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetFileNumByAssetId(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id);

            string formattedFeeAmountCents = (merged_int_fee / 100m).ToString("C2", CultureInfo.GetCultureInfo("en-US"));

            MTApiObjects.ExpectedPayment expectedPayment = new MTApiObjects.ExpectedPayment
            {
                ledger_transaction = new MTApiObjects.LedgerTransactionEP
                {
                    description = "Merged FA Fee Expected Payment of " + merged_decimal_fee,
                    ledger_entries = new List<MTApiObjects.LedgerEntryEP>
                    {
                        new MTApiObjects.LedgerEntryEP
                        {
                            amount = fee_orig_amount_int,
                            direction = "debit",
                            ledger_account_id = receivingLedgerAccountUPS
                        },
                        new MTApiObjects.LedgerEntryEP
                        {
                            amount = fee_orig_amount_int,
                            direction = "credit",
                            ledger_account_id = fee_origination_mtid
                        },
                        new MTApiObjects.LedgerEntryEP
                        {
                            amount = fee_appr_amount_int,
                            direction = "debit",
                            ledger_account_id = receivingLedgerAccountUPS
                        },
                        new MTApiObjects.LedgerEntryEP
                        {
                            amount = fee_appr_amount_int,
                            direction = "credit",
                            ledger_account_id = fee_appraisal_mtid
                        }
                    }
                },
                reconciliation_rule_variables = new List<MTApiObjects.ReconciliationRuleVariables>
                {
                    new MTApiObjects.ReconciliationRuleVariables
                    {
                        internal_account_id = TCB_internal_account_id,
                        direction = "credit",
                        amount_lower_bound = merged_int_fee,
                        amount_upper_bound = merged_int_fee,
                        custom_identifiers = new Dictionary<string, string>
                        {
                            { "amount", merged_decimal_fee.ToString() },
                            { "fee_type", title_escrow_company + " final merged fee (origination + appriasal)" },
                            { "asset_id", asset_id },
                            { "file_num", file_num },
                            { "title_escrow_company", title_escrow_company }
                        }
                    },
                },
                metadata = new Dictionary<string, string>
                {
                    { "amount", formattedFeeAmountCents.ToString() },
                    { "fee_type", "Origination + Appraisal" },
                    { "asset_id", asset_id },
                    { "file_num", file_num },
                    { "initiated_by", "Drawflow.cs" },
                    { "title_escrow_company", title_escrow_company },
                    { "full_description", "Merged Final " + title_escrow_company + " Fee Expected Payment of " + formattedFeeAmountCents + " for Asset ID " + asset_id + " (" + file_num + ")" }

                }
            };

            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(expectedPayment);
            Console.WriteLine(requestBody);
            return await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
        }
