        public static async Task<string> PatchCETOriginationFeeExpectedPaymentForConcessionAsync(string asset_id, string orig_fee, decimal concession_value, string title_escrow_company)
        {

            
            string concession_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_Concessions_Live(asset_id.ToString());
            
            string orig_fee_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_OriginationFee_Live(asset_id.ToString());
      

            string receivingLedgerAccountUPS = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UPS_Cash_ledger_account_id;
            string TCB_internal_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_ups_clearing_account;

            decimal orig_fee_decimal = Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(orig_fee), 2);
            int orig_fee_amount_int = Convert.ToInt32(orig_fee_decimal * 100); 
            decimal concession_amount_decimal = Math.Abs(Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(concession_value), 2));
            int concession_amount_int = Convert.ToInt32(concession_amount_decimal * 100); 

            decimal ep_amount_orig_minus_concession_decimal = orig_fee_decimal - concession_amount_decimal;
            int ep_amount_orig_minus_concession_int = Convert.ToInt32(ep_amount_orig_minus_concession_decimal * 100); 

            string formattedFeeAmountCents = (ep_amount_orig_minus_concession_int / 100m).ToString("C2", CultureInfo.GetCultureInfo("en-US"));
            string file_num = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetFileNumByAssetId(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id);


            
            string ep_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetExpectedPaymentIdByAssetIdAndFeeType_Live(asset_id.ToString(), "Origination");
            string mt_target_url = "https:


            MTApiObjects.ExpectedPayment expectedPayment = new MTApiObjects.ExpectedPayment
            {
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                reconciliation_rule_variables = new List<MTApiObjects.ReconciliationRuleVariables>
                {
                    new MTApiObjects.ReconciliationRuleVariables
                    {
                        internal_account_id = TCB_internal_account_id,
                        direction = "credit",
                        amount_lower_bound = ep_amount_orig_minus_concession_int,
                        amount_upper_bound = ep_amount_orig_minus_concession_int,
                        custom_identifiers = new Dictionary<string, string>
                        {
                            { "amount", ep_amount_orig_minus_concession_decimal.ToString() },
                            { "fee_type", "Origination" },
                            { "asset_id", asset_id },
                            { "file_num", file_num },
                            { "title_escrow_company", title_escrow_company }
                        }
                    }
                },
                metadata = new Dictionary<string, string>
                {
                    { "amount", formattedFeeAmountCents.ToString() },
                    { "fee_type", "Origination" },
                    { "asset_id", asset_id },
                    { "file_num", file_num },
                    { "initiated_by", "Drawflow.cs" },
                    { "title_escrow_company", title_escrow_company },
                    { "full_description", "Origination Fee with Concession: "+ concession_amount_decimal +" adjustment - Ofee Expected Payment adjusted from "+ orig_fee_decimal + " to " + ep_amount_orig_minus_concession_decimal+" (" + file_num + ")" }

                }
            };

            JObject expectedPaymentJo = JObject.FromObject(expectedPayment);
            expectedPaymentJo.Remove("ledger_transaction");
            
            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(expectedPaymentJo, Formatting.Indented);

            var client = new ModernTreasuryClient2();

            
            return await client.SendHttpRequestAsync(mt_target_url, requestBody, "Patch");
        }


        public static async Task<string> CreateLedgerTransactionForConcessionAsync(string asset_id, string orig_fee, decimal concession_value, string title_escrow_company)
        {
            
            string concession_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_Concessions_Live(asset_id);
            string orig_fee_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_OriginationFee_Live(asset_id);

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(concession_mtid))
            {
                DXMessageBox.Show($"Concessions ledger not found in MT for asset: {asset_id}");
                Console.WriteLine($"Concessions MTID missing for asset_id: {asset_id}");
                return null;
            }

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(orig_fee_mtid))
            {
                DXMessageBox.Show($"Origination Fee ledger not found in MT for asset: {asset_id}");
                Console.WriteLine($"Origination Fee MTID missing for asset_id: {asset_id}");
                return null;
            }

            
            decimal concession_decimal = Math.Abs(Math.Round(concession_value, 2));
            int concession_int = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(concession_decimal * 100m, MidpointRounding.AwayFromZero));

            
            string file_num = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetFileNumByAssetId(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id);
            string formattedConcession = (concession_int / 100m).ToString("C2", CultureInfo.GetCultureInfo("en-US"));

            
            JObject ltPayload = new JObject
            {
                ["ledger_entries"] = new JArray
                {
                    new JObject
                    {
                        ["amount"] = concession_int,
                        ["direction"] = "debit",
                        ["ledger_account_id"] = orig_fee_mtid
                    },
                    new JObject
                    {
                        ["amount"] = concession_int,
                        ["direction"] = "credit",
                        ["ledger_account_id"] = concession_mtid
                    }
                },
                ["description"] = $"Concession adjustment of {formattedConcession} for Asset {asset_id} ({file_num})",
                ["metadata"] = new JObject
                {
                    ["asset_id"] = asset_id,
                    ["file_num"] = file_num,
                    ["initiated_by"] = "Drawflow.cs",
                    ["title_escrow_company"] = title_escrow_company ?? string.Empty,
                    ["concession_amount"] = formattedConcession
                }
            };

            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ltPayload);
            Console.WriteLine(requestBody);

            
            return await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
        }


        public static async Task<string> PatchFAExpectedPaymentForConcessionAsync(string asset_id, string orig_fee, string appraisal_fee, decimal concession_value, string title_escrow_company)
        {
            
            
            

            
            string receivingLedgerAccountUPS = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UPS_Cash_ledger_account_id;
            string TCB_internal_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_ups_clearing_account;

            decimal orig_fee_decimal = Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(orig_fee), 2);
            decimal appr_fee_decimal = Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(appraisal_fee), 2);
            decimal concession_decimal = Math.Abs(Math.Round(concession_value, 2));

            decimal orig_minus_concession_decimal = orig_fee_decimal - concession_decimal;
            decimal merged_adjusted_decimal = orig_minus_concession_decimal + appr_fee_decimal;

            int orig_minus_concession_int = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(orig_minus_concession_decimal * 100m, MidpointRounding.AwayFromZero));
            int appr_fee_int = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(appr_fee_decimal * 100m, MidpointRounding.AwayFromZero));
            int merged_adjusted_int = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(merged_adjusted_decimal * 100m, MidpointRounding.AwayFromZero));
            int concession_int = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(concession_decimal * 100m, MidpointRounding.AwayFromZero));

            string file_num = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetFileNumByAssetId(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id);
            string formattedMergedAmount = (merged_adjusted_int / 100m).ToString("C2", CultureInfo.GetCultureInfo("en-US"));
            string formattedConcession = (concession_int / 100m).ToString("C2", CultureInfo.GetCultureInfo("en-US"));

            
            string ep_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetExpectedPaymentIdByAssetIdAndFeeType_Live(asset_id.ToString(), "Origination + Appraisal");
            
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ep_mtid))
            {
                
                ep_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_InitialOriginationFee_Live(asset_id.ToString());
            }

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ep_mtid))
            {
                DXMessageBox.Show($"Could not locate merged FA expected payment EP for asset {asset_id} to apply concession.");
                Console.WriteLine($"Merged FA expected payment EP not found for asset_id: {asset_id}");
                return null;
            }

            string mt_target_url = "https:

            MTApiObjects.ExpectedPayment expectedPayment = new MTApiObjects.ExpectedPayment
            {
                
                reconciliation_rule_variables = new List<MTApiObjects.ReconciliationRuleVariables>
                {
                    new MTApiObjects.ReconciliationRuleVariables
                    {
                        internal_account_id = TCB_internal_account_id,
                        direction = "credit",
                        amount_lower_bound = merged_adjusted_int,
                        amount_upper_bound = merged_adjusted_int,
                        custom_identifiers = new Dictionary<string, string>
                        {
                            { "amount", merged_adjusted_decimal.ToString() },
                            { "fee_type", "Origination + Appraisal (adjusted for concession)" },
                            { "asset_id", asset_id },
                            { "file_num", file_num },
                            { "title_escrow_company", title_escrow_company },
                            { "origination_adjusted", orig_minus_concession_decimal.ToString() },
                            { "appraisal_amount", appr_fee_decimal.ToString() },
                            { "concession_amount", concession_decimal.ToString() }
                        }
                    }
                },
                metadata = new Dictionary<string, string>
                {
                    { "amount", formattedMergedAmount.ToString() },
                    { "fee_type", "Origination + Appraisal (adjusted for concession)" },
                    { "asset_id", asset_id },
                    { "file_num", file_num },
                    { "initiated_by", "Drawflow.cs" },
                    { "title_escrow_company", title_escrow_company },
                    { "full_description", $"FA merged expected payment adjusted to {formattedMergedAmount} (origination {orig_fee_decimal:C2} - concession {formattedConcession} + appraisal {appr_fee_decimal:C2})" }
                }
            };

            JObject expectedPaymentJo = JObject.FromObject(expectedPayment);
            expectedPaymentJo.Remove("ledger_transaction"); 
            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(expectedPaymentJo, Formatting.Indented);

            var client = new ModernTreasuryClient2();
            Console.WriteLine(requestBody);
            return await client.SendHttpRequestAsync(mt_target_url, requestBody, "Patch");
        }


        public static async Task<string> CreateDatedFundingDatesCategoryAsync(string fundingDate)
        {
            
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fundingDate))
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Funding date is required.");
                return null;
            }

            
            try { await SetEnvironment.SetEnv(); } catch {  }

            
            string parentFundingDatesCatId = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.funding_dates_cat_id;
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(parentFundingDatesCatId))
            {
                Console.WriteLine("FUNDING_DATES category id (funding_dates_cat_id) not set in ModernTreasuryKeys.");
                DXMessageBox.Show("FUNDING_DATES category id not configured for Modern Treasury environment.");
                return null;
            }

            
            
            
            
            try
            {
                var existingId = await ModernTreasuryUtils.FindFundingDateCategoryIdByNameAsync(fundingDate);
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(existingId))
                {
                    
                    return existingId;
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                
                Console.WriteLine($"Funding date lookup failed (will attempt create): {ex.Message}");
            }

            
            string orgId = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UNLOCK_MT_ORGANIZATION_ID;
            string apiKey = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UNLOCK_MT_API_KEY;
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(orgId) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(apiKey))
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Modern Treasury API keys not configured.");
                DXMessageBox.Show("Modern Treasury API keys not configured.");
                return null;
            }

            ServicePointManager.SecurityProtocol = SecurityProtocolType.Tls12;

            
            try
            {
                string targetLedger = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.unlock_ledger_id;
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(targetLedger))
                {
                    Console.WriteLine("Unlock ledger id not configured (unlock_ledger_id).");
                    DXMessageBox.Show("Unlock ledger id not configured for Modern Treasury environment.");
                    return null;
                }

                var ledgerAccountCategory = new MTApiObjects.LedgerAccountCategory
                {
                    name = fundingDate,
                    currency = "USD",
                    normal_balance = "debit",
                    ledger_account_category_ids = new List<string> { parentFundingDatesCatId },
                    ledger_id = targetLedger,
                    description = $"{Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.category_label}{fundingDate}",
                    metadata = new Dictionary<string, string>
            {
                { "funding_date", fundingDate },
                { "initiated_by", "Drawflow.cs" },
                { "category_type", "FUNDING DATES" }
            }
                };

                string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ledgerAccountCategory);
                Console.WriteLine(requestBody);

                string createdId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
                return createdId;
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create funding date category for '{fundingDate}': {ex.Message}");
                return null;
            }
        }
        

        public static async Task UpdateFeesInMTAsync(DataTable wireBreakdown, string title_type)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();

            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            

            if (title_type == "CET")
            {
                foreach (DataRow row in wireBreakdown.Rows)
                {
                    DataTable wirebreakdown_row = wireBreakdown.Clone();
                    wirebreakdown_row.ImportRow(row);

                    string updatedFeeExpectedPaymentId = await UpdateCETFeeExpectedPaymentAsync(wirebreakdown_row);
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(updatedFeeExpectedPaymentId))
                    {
                        string asset_id = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                        string fee_type = row["type"].ToString();
                        string transaction_label = "CET " + fee_type + "_fee_expected_payment_update of " + row["cet_amount"];
                        decimal total_amount = Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(row["cet_amount"]), 2);
                        string mt_object_url = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + updatedFeeExpectedPaymentId;
                        bool insert_fees_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id, transaction_label, updatedFeeExpectedPaymentId, "expected_payment", null, null, asset_id, total_amount, mt_object_url, "Drawflow.cs", "ClearEdge Title", total_amount, null);
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        Console.WriteLine($"Failed to update expected payment for asset_id: {row["asset_id"].ToString()}");
                        continue;
                    }
                }
            }
            else if (title_type == "FA")
            {
                
                foreach (DataRow row in wireBreakdown.Rows)
                {
                    DataTable wirebreakdown_row = wireBreakdown.Clone();
                    wirebreakdown_row.ImportRow(row);

                    
                    string updatedOrigFeeExpectedPaymentId = await UpdateFAFeeExpectedPaymentAsync(wirebreakdown_row, "origination");
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(updatedOrigFeeExpectedPaymentId))
                    {
                        string asset_id = row["fa_asset_id"].ToString();
                        string fee_type = "Origination";
                        string transaction_label = "FA " + fee_type + "_fee_expected_payment_update of " + row["origination_fee"];
                        decimal total_amount = Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(row["origination_fee"]), 2);
                        string mt_object_url = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + updatedOrigFeeExpectedPaymentId;
                        bool insert_fees_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id, transaction_label, updatedOrigFeeExpectedPaymentId, "expected_payment", null, null, asset_id, total_amount, mt_object_url, "Drawflow.cs", "First American Title", total_amount, null);

                    }
                    else
                    {
                        Console.WriteLine($"Failed to update expected payment for asset_id: {row["fa_asset_id"].ToString()}");
                        continue;
                    }

                    
                    string updatedApprFeeExpectedPaymentId = await UpdateFAFeeExpectedPaymentAsync(wirebreakdown_row, "appraisal");
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(updatedApprFeeExpectedPaymentId))
                    {
                        string asset_id = row["fa_asset_id"].ToString();
                        string fee_type = "Appraisal";
                        string transaction_label = "FA " + fee_type + "_fee_expected_payment_update of " + row["appraisal_fee"];
                        decimal total_amount = Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(row["appraisal_fee"]), 2);
                        string mt_object_url = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + updatedApprFeeExpectedPaymentId;
                        bool insert_fees_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id, transaction_label, updatedApprFeeExpectedPaymentId, "expected_payment", null, null, asset_id, total_amount, mt_object_url, "Drawflow.cs", "Frist American Title", total_amount, null);
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        Console.WriteLine($"Failed to update expected payment for asset_id: {row["fa_asset_id"].ToString()}");
                        continue;
                    }

                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(updatedApprFeeExpectedPaymentId) && (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(updatedApprFeeExpectedPaymentId))) 
                    {
                        
                        bool update_fa_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.UpdateFABreakdown_MTLoaded(MTDrawGlobals.server, row["fa_asset_id"].ToString());
                    }
                }
            }
            else
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Unknown title company type: {title_type}");
            }

        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        



        private static async Task<string> UpdateCETFeeExpectedPaymentAsync(DataTable wirebreakdown_single)
        {
            string receivingLedgerAccountUPS = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UPS_Cash_ledger_account_id;
            string TCB_internal_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uam_clearing_account;

            
            DataRow firstRow = wirebreakdown_single.Rows[0];

            string fee_ledger_name = firstRow["ledger"].ToString();
            string file_number = firstRow["file_number"].ToString();
            decimal bank_amount = Convert.ToDecimal(firstRow["bank_amount"]);
            decimal cet_amount = Convert.ToDecimal(firstRow["cet_amount"]);
            string asset_id = firstRow["asset_id"].ToString();
            string bank_trans_id = firstRow["bank_trans_id"].ToString();
            string fee_type = firstRow["type"].ToString();
            string address_full = firstRow["address_full"].ToString();
            string issued_date = firstRow["issued"].ToString();

            DateTime converted_date = Convert.ToDateTime(firstRow["issued"]);
            string issued_date_str = converted_date.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd");

            int bank_amount_int = Convert.ToInt32(bank_amount * 100); 
            string fee_type_ledger_wire_date = fee_type + "-" + fee_ledger_name + "-" + issued_date;

            
            string fee_mtid = "";

            if (ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_InitialOriginationFee_Live( asset_id.ToString()) == null ||
                ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_InitialAppraisalFee_Live( asset_id.ToString()) == null)
            {
                
                return null;
            }
            else
            { 
                if (fee_type == "Origination")
                {
                    fee_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_InitialOriginationFee_Live( asset_id.ToString());
                }
                else if (fee_type == "Appraisal")
                {
                    fee_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_InitialAppraisalFee_Live( asset_id.ToString());
                }
                else
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Unknown fee type: {fee_type} for asset_id: {asset_id.ToString()}");
                }
            }
            string mt_target_url = "https:

            decimal fee_amount_decimal = Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(cet_amount), 2);
            int fee_amount_int = Convert.ToInt32(fee_amount_decimal * 100); 
            string cet_file_num = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetFileNumByAssetId(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id);

            MTApiObjects.ExpectedPayment expectedPayment = new MTApiObjects.ExpectedPayment
            {
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                reconciliation_rule_variables = new List<MTApiObjects.ReconciliationRuleVariables>
                {
                    new MTApiObjects.ReconciliationRuleVariables
                    {
                        internal_account_id = TCB_internal_account_id,
                        direction = "credit",
                        amount_lower_bound = fee_amount_int,
                        amount_upper_bound = fee_amount_int,
                        date_lower_bound = issued_date_str,
                        date_upper_bound = issued_date_str,
                        custom_identifiers = new Dictionary<string, string>
                        {
                            { "amount", fee_amount_decimal.ToString() },
                            { "fee_type", fee_type },
                            { "asset_id", asset_id },
                            { "file_num", cet_file_num },
                            { "bank_transaction_id", bank_trans_id },
                            { "fee_type_ledger_wire_date", fee_type_ledger_wire_date},
                            { "ledger", fee_ledger_name },
                            { "issued_date",  issued_date}    
                        }
                    }
                }
            };

            JObject expectedPaymentJo = JObject.FromObject(expectedPayment);
            expectedPaymentJo.Remove("ledger_transaction");
            expectedPaymentJo.Remove("metadata");
            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(expectedPaymentJo, Formatting.Indented);

            var client = new ModernTreasuryClient2();

            
            

            Console.WriteLine(requestBody);
            return await client.SendHttpRequestAsync( mt_target_url, requestBody, "Patch");
        }

        private static async Task<string> UpdateFAFeeExpectedPaymentAsync(DataTable wirebreakdown_single, string fee_type)
        {
            string receivingLedgerAccountUPS = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UPS_Cash_ledger_account_id;
            string TCB_internal_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uam_clearing_account;

            
            DataRow firstRow = wirebreakdown_single.Rows[0];

            string file_num = firstRow["file_num"].ToString();
            decimal origination_fee = Convert.ToDecimal(firstRow["origination_fee"]);
            decimal appraisal_fee = Convert.ToDecimal(firstRow["appraisal_fee"]);
            decimal combined_fee = Convert.ToDecimal(firstRow["origination_fee"]) + Convert.ToDecimal(firstRow["appraisal_fee"]);
            string asset_id = firstRow["fa_asset_id"].ToString();
            string bank_trans_id = firstRow["bankactivity_id"].ToString();
            string wire_date = firstRow["wire_date"].ToString();

            DateTime converted_date = Convert.ToDateTime(firstRow["wire_date"]);
            string issued_date_str = converted_date.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd");

            string fee_type_wire_date = fee_type + "-" + issued_date_str;

            
            string fee_mtid = "";
            decimal fee_amount_decimal=0;
            int fee_amount_int=0;
            decimal combined_fee_amount_decimal = 0;
            int combined_fee_amount_int = 0;

            if (fee_type == "origination")
            {
                fee_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_InitialOriginationFee(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id.ToString());
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(fee_mtid))
                {
                    return null;
                } 
                fee_amount_decimal = Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(origination_fee), 2);
                fee_amount_int = Convert.ToInt32(origination_fee * 100); 
                combined_fee_amount_decimal = Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(combined_fee), 2);
                combined_fee_amount_int = Convert.ToInt32(combined_fee * 100); 
            }
            else if (fee_type == "appraisal")
            {
                fee_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_InitialAppraisalFee(MTDrawGlobals.server, asset_id.ToString());
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(fee_mtid))
                {
                    return null;
                }
                fee_amount_decimal = Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(appraisal_fee), 2);
                fee_amount_int = Convert.ToInt32(appraisal_fee * 100); 
                combined_fee_amount_decimal = Math.Round(Convert.ToDecimal(combined_fee), 2);
                combined_fee_amount_int = Convert.ToInt32(combined_fee * 100); 
            }

            string mt_target_url = "https:

            MTApiObjects.ExpectedPayment expectedPayment = new MTApiObjects.ExpectedPayment
            {
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                reconciliation_rule_variables = new List<MTApiObjects.ReconciliationRuleVariables>
                {
                    new MTApiObjects.ReconciliationRuleVariables
                    {
                        internal_account_id = TCB_internal_account_id,
                        direction = "credit",
                        amount_lower_bound = fee_amount_int,
                        amount_upper_bound = fee_amount_int,
                        date_lower_bound = issued_date_str,
                        date_upper_bound = issued_date_str,
                        custom_identifiers = new Dictionary<string, string>
                        {
                            { "amount", fee_amount_decimal.ToString() },
                            { "fee_type", fee_type },
                            { "asset_id", asset_id },
                            { "file_num", file_num },
                            { "bank_transaction_id", bank_trans_id },
                            { "fee_type_wire_date", fee_type_wire_date},
                            { "wire_date",  wire_date},
                            { "combined_orig_and_appr",  combined_fee_amount_decimal.ToString() }
                        }
                    }
                }
            };

            JObject expectedPaymentJo = JObject.FromObject(expectedPayment);
            expectedPaymentJo.Remove("ledger_transaction");
            expectedPaymentJo.Remove("metadata");
            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(expectedPaymentJo, Formatting.Indented);

            var client = new ModernTreasuryClient2();

            
            

            Console.WriteLine(requestBody);
            return await client.SendHttpRequestAsync(mt_target_url, requestBody, "Patch");
        }

using static ModernTreasuryLib.ModernTreasuryClient;
using static ModernTreasuryLib.MTApiObjects;

namespace ModernTreasuryLib
{
    public class FundingFeeDatedLoader

        public static void LoadDateRangeModernTreasuryDrawflow(string server, string start_date, string end_date)
        {
            if (!DateTime.TryParse(start_date, out var start))
                throw new ArgumentException("Invalid start_date", nameof(start_date));
            if (!DateTime.TryParse(end_date, out var end))
                throw new ArgumentException("Invalid end_date", nameof(end_date));

            if (end.Date < start.Date)
                throw new ArgumentException("end_date must be the same or after start_date");

            for (var d = start.Date; d <= end.Date; d = d.AddDays(1))
            {
                string target_funding_date = d.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd");
                
                DataTable assetsForMT = GetBulkFundingFundedAssetsTargetDate(server, target_funding_date);
                DataTable ceBreakdownDataForMT = GetCEBreakdownForFundingDate(server, target_funding_date);

                
                
                
                (DataTable faBreakdownDataForMT, DataTable faHiBreakdownDataForMT) = GetFABreakdownForFundingDate(server, target_funding_date);

                DataTable funding_date = CreateFundingDateTable(target_funding_date);
                
                
                ModernTreasury_Draw.CreateDrawMTAssetsAsync(assetsForMT, ceBreakdownDataForMT, faBreakdownDataForMT, faHiBreakdownDataForMT, funding_date);
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                


                
                
                
                
                
                
                

                
                
                
                

            }
            DXMessageBox.Show("MT DRAWFLOW LOAD for daterange COMPLETE!!!!!");
        }

        public static DataTable GetCEBreakdownForFundingDate(string server, string target_funding_date)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(target_funding_date))
                throw new ArgumentException("target_funding_date must be provided", nameof(target_funding_date));

            
            DateTime valueDate;
            if (!DateTime.TryParseExact(target_funding_date, "yyyy-MM-dd", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, DateTimeStyles.None, out valueDate))
            {
                if (!DateTime.TryParse(target_funding_date, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, DateTimeStyles.None, out valueDate))
                {
                    throw new ArgumentException("Invalid target_funding_date", nameof(target_funding_date));
                }
            }

            DataTable dt = GetBulkFundingDataFaster(server, valueDate);
           
            
            DataTable clearedge_dt = dt.Clone();
            foreach (DataRow row in dt.Rows)
            {
                if (row["TITLE_ESCROW_COMPANY"]?.ToString() == "ClearEdge Title")
                    clearedge_dt.ImportRow(row);
            }

            return clearedge_dt;
        }

        
        
        
        public static (DataTable faBreakdownDataForMT, DataTable faHiBreakdownDataForMT) GetFABreakdownForFundingDate(string server, string target_funding_date)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(target_funding_date))
                throw new ArgumentException("target_funding_date must be provided", nameof(target_funding_date));

            
            DateTime valueDate;
            if (!DateTime.TryParseExact(target_funding_date, "yyyy-MM-dd", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, DateTimeStyles.None, out valueDate))
            {
                if (!DateTime.TryParse(target_funding_date, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, DateTimeStyles.None, out valueDate))
                {
                    throw new ArgumentException("Invalid target_funding_date", nameof(target_funding_date));
                }
            }

            DataTable dt = GetBulkFundingDataFaster(server, valueDate);

            
            DataTable fa_nonhi_dt = dt.Clone();
            DataTable fa_hi_dt = dt.Clone();
            foreach (DataRow row in dt.Rows)
            {
                var title = row["TITLE_ESCROW_COMPANY"] as string;
                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(title) && title.StartsWith("First American", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                {
                    bool isHI = false;
                    if (dt.Columns.Contains("is_HI") && row["is_HI"] != DBNull.Value)
                    {
                        object v = row["is_HI"];
                        if (v is bool b) isHI = b;
                        else if (v is byte by) isHI = by != 0;
                        else if (v is short s) isHI = s != 0;
                        else if (v is int i) isHI = i != 0;
                        else if (v is string sv) isHI = sv.Equals("true", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) || sv == "1";
                    }

                    if (isHI)
                        fa_hi_dt.ImportRow(row);
                    else
                        fa_nonhi_dt.ImportRow(row);
                }
            }

            return (fa_nonhi_dt, fa_hi_dt);
        }


        public static DataTable GetBulkFundingFundedAssetsTargetDate(string server, string target_funding_date)
        {

            string sql = 
             " select distinct 'closed-won' AS APPLICATION_STATE," +
             " fn.asset_id as ASSET_ID," +
             " cl.CUSTOMER_PIPELINE_LABEL as customer_pipeline_label_max," +
             " cl.investment_payment," +
             " cl.investment_payment as AMOUNT," +
             " 'Shipped' as Shipment_Status," +
             " ven.name as TITLE_ESCROW_COMPANY," +
             " va.state," +
             " cl.effective_date" +
             " from Fundings_New fn" +
             " left join vClosing cl on cl.asset_id = fn.asset_id" +
             " left join vAssets va on va.asset_id = fn.asset_id" +
             " left join Vendors ven on ven.id = fn.titleescrowcompany_id" +
             " where fn.value_date = @target_value_date" +
             " order by fn.asset_id;";

            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@target_value_date", target_funding_date);
            DataTable dt = q.ExecuteTable();
            
            return dt;
        }


        public static DataTable CreateFundingDateTable(string target_funding_date)
        {
            var dt = new DataTable();
            dt.Columns.Add("VALUE_DATE_INPUT", typeof(string));

            var row = dt.NewRow();
            row["VALUE_DATE_INPUT"] = target_funding_date ?? string.Empty;
            dt.Rows.Add(row);

            return dt;
        }

            q.AddParameter("@value_date", value_date);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        {
            Query q = new Query("BulkFundingFaster.sql", server);
            
            q.AddParameter("@value_date", value_date);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }


        
        
        

        
        
        public static void LoadDateRangeModernTreasuryFeeProcessingCETAsync(string server, string start_date, string end_date)
        {
            
            if (!DateTime.TryParse(start_date, out var start))
                throw new ArgumentException("Invalid start_date", nameof(start_date));
            if (!DateTime.TryParse(end_date, out var end))
                throw new ArgumentException("Invalid end_date", nameof(end));
            if (end.Date < start.Date)
                throw new ArgumentException("end_date must be the same or after start_date");


            DataTable CETFeeIssueDateList = GetCETWireReportFeeReturnDateList(server, start_date, end_date);

            if (CETFeeIssueDateList == null || CETFeeIssueDateList.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                DXMessageBox.Show("No CET fee issue dates found for the specified date range.");
                return;
            }

            
            if (!CETFeeIssueDateList.Columns.Contains("issued"))
            {
                DXMessageBox.Show("CET fee issue date list does not contain an 'issued' column.");
                return;
            }

            foreach (DataRow row in CETFeeIssueDateList.Rows)
            {
                if (row == null || row["issued"] == DBNull.Value)
                    continue;

                string target_date;
                var issuedVal = row["issued"];

                if (issuedVal is DateTime dt)
                    target_date = dt.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd");
                else
                    target_date = issuedVal.ToString();

                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(target_date))
                    continue;

                PushDailyCETReceivedFeesToModernTreasury_daterange(server, target_date);
            }
        }

   
        public static void PushDailyCETReceivedFeesToModernTreasury_daterange(string server, string target_date)
        {
            
            
            DataTable CETwireBreakdown = GetCETWireReportBreakdownAndLedgers(server, target_date.ToString());
            if (CETwireBreakdown.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                DXMessageBox.Show("No CET Wire Report data found for the specified issued date.");
                return;
            }
            ModernTreasuryLib.ModernTreasury_Draw.UpdateFeesInMTAsync(CETwireBreakdown, "CET");
        }

        public static DataTable GetCETWireReportBreakdownAndLedgers(string server, string issued_date)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT ce_rpt.ledger,ce_rpt.file_number, bank.amount AS bank_amount, ce_rpt.amount as cet_amount,ce_rpt.asset_id," +
                         "bank_trans_id,bank.transaction_date, ce_rpt.[type], a.address_full, a.name_simple, ce_rpt.issued FROM " +
                         "ClearEdgeWireTransactionMap CE_Map LEFT JOIN ClearEdgeWireReports ce_rpt ON ce_map.issued = ce_rpt.issued " +
                         "AND ce_map.ledger = ce_rpt.ledger AND ce_map.[type] = ce_rpt.[type] LEFT JOIN bankactivity bank ON ce_map.bank_trans_id = bank.id " +
                         "LEFT JOIN vAssetsEx a ON a.asset_id = ce_rpt.asset_id WHERE ce_rpt.issued = @issued_date ORDER BY bank.transaction_date, bank_trans_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@issued_date", issued_date);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetCETWireReportFeeReturnDateList(string server, string start_date, string end_date)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT DISTINCT ce_rpt.issued FROM ClearEdgeWireTransactionMap CE_Map " +
                         "LEFT JOIN ClearEdgeWireReports ce_rpt ON ce_map.issued = ce_rpt.issued " +
                         "AND ce_map.ledger = ce_rpt.ledger AND ce_map.[type] = ce_rpt.[type] " +
                         "LEFT JOIN bankactivity bank ON ce_map.bank_trans_id = bank.id " +
                         "LEFT JOIN vAssetsEx a ON a.asset_id = ce_rpt.asset_id " +
                         "LEFT JOIN Fundings_New fn ON fn.asset_id = ce_rpt.Asset_ID " +
                         "WHERE fn.value_date BETWEEN @start_date AND @end_date;";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@start_date", start_date);
            q.AddParameter("@end_date", end_date);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        
        
        public static void LoadDateRangeModernTreasuryFeeProcessingFAAsync(string server, string start_date, string end_date)
        {
            if (!DateTime.TryParse(start_date, out var start))
                throw new ArgumentException("Invalid start_date", nameof(start_date));
            if (!DateTime.TryParse(end_date, out var end))
                throw new ArgumentException("Invalid end_date", nameof(end_date));
            if (end.Date < start.Date)
                throw new ArgumentException("end_date must be the same or after start_date", nameof(end_date));


            DataTable FAWireBreakdown = RemoveEmptyRows(GetFAWireReportFeeList(server, start_date, end_date));
            
            if (FAWireBreakdown == null || FAWireBreakdown.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                DXMessageBox.Show("No FA fee issue dates found for the specified date range.");
                return;
            }
            
            if (!FAWireBreakdown.Columns.Contains("wire_date"))
            {
                DXMessageBox.Show("FA fee issue date list does not contain an 'issued' column.");
                return;
            }
            foreach (DataRow row in FAWireBreakdown.Rows)
            {
                if (row == null || row["wire_date"] == DBNull.Value)
                    continue;
                string target_date;
                var issuedVal = row["wire_date"];
                if (issuedVal is DateTime dt)
                    target_date = dt.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd");
                else
                    target_date = issuedVal.ToString();
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(target_date))
                    continue;
                ModernTreasuryLib.ModernTreasury_Draw.UpdateFeesInMTAsync(FAWireBreakdown, "FA");
            }
        }

        public static DataTable GetFAWireReportFeeList(string server, string start_date, string end_date)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT fwb.* FROM Fundings_New fn " +
             "LEFT JOIN FirstAmericanWireBreakdown fwb ON fwb.fa_asset_id = fn.asset_id " +
             "WHERE fn.value_date BETWEEN @start_date AND @end_date " +
             "AND fn.fundingstatus_id <> 4 " +
             "AND fn.titleescrowcompany_id = 48;";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@start_date", start_date);
            q.AddParameter("@end_date", end_date);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable RemoveEmptyRows(DataTable source)
        {
            DataTable dt1 = source.Clone();
            for (int i = 0; i < source.Rows.Count; i++)
            {
                DataRow currentRow = source.Rows[i];
                foreach (var colValue in currentRow.ItemArray)
                {
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(colValue.ToString()))
                    {
                        dt1.ImportRow(currentRow);
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
            return dt1;
        }

    }

--- FILE: ModernTreasuryLib\LedgerCreator.cs ---
using static ModernTreasuryLib.MTApiObjects;
using static ModernTreasuryLib.ModernTreasuryClient;
namespace ModernTreasuryLib
{
    public class LedgerCreator
    {

        public static async Task CreateModernTreasuryLedgerAsync(DataTable dt_ledger_creator_curl)
        {
            ExecuteCurlCommandsAsync(dt_ledger_creator_curl);
        }
        public static async Task<DataTable> ExecuteCurlCommandsAsync(DataTable curlCommands)
        {
            if (curlCommands == null)
                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(curlCommands));

            
            string colNameName = curlCommands.Columns.Cast<DataColumn>().Select(c => c.ColumnName)
                .FirstOrDefault(n => string.Equals(n, "NAME", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                                   || string.Equals(n, "Name", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
            string colNameCurl = curlCommands.Columns.Cast<DataColumn>().Select(c => c.ColumnName)
                .FirstOrDefault(n => string.Equals(n, "CURL", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                                   || string.Equals(n, "COMMAND", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                                   || string.Equals(n, "Curl", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                                   || string.Equals(n, "Command", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));

            if (colNameCurl == null)
                throw new ArgumentException("Input DataTable must contain a column named 'CURL' or 'COMMAND' (case-insensitive).");

            
            DataTable result = new DataTable();
            result.Columns.Add("NAME", typeof(string));
            result.Columns.Add("id", typeof(string));
            result.Columns.Add("response", typeof(string));
            result.Columns.Add("success", typeof(bool));
            result.Columns.Add("error", typeof(string));

            foreach (DataRow row in curlCommands.Rows)
            {
                string name = colNameName != null ? (row[colNameName]?.ToString() ?? string.Empty) : string.Empty;
                string curlCommand = row[colNameCurl]?.ToString() ?? string.Empty;

                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(curlCommand))
                {
                    result.Rows.Add(name, DBNull.Value, DBNull.Value, false, "Empty curl command");
                    continue;
                }

                try
                {
                    
                    var execResult = await Task.Run(() => ExecuteShellCommand(curlCommand));

                    string stdout = execResult.stdout?.Trim() ?? string.Empty;
                    string stderr = execResult.stderr?.Trim() ?? string.Empty;
                    bool success = execResult.exitCode == 0 && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(stdout);

                    string idValue = null;
                    string errorMsg = null;

                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(stdout))
                    {
                        
                        idValue = TryExtractIdFromJson(stdout);
                        if (idValue == null)
                        {
                            
                            idValue = TryExtractIdWithRegex(stdout);
                        }
                    }

                    if (idValue == null && !success)
                        errorMsg = !string.IsNullOrEmpty(stderr) ? stderr : "No id found in response";

                    result.Rows.Add(name, idValue ?? (object)DBNull.Value, stdout, success && idValue != null, errorMsg);
                }
                catch (Exception ex)
                {
                    result.Rows.Add(name, DBNull.Value, DBNull.Value, false, ex.Message);
                }
            }

            return result;
        }

        
        private static (string stdout, string stderr, int exitCode) ExecuteShellCommand(string command)
        {
            
            
            ProcessStartInfo psi = new ProcessStartInfo
            {
                FileName = "cmd.exe",
                Arguments = "/c " + command,
                UseShellExecute = false,
                RedirectStandardOutput = true,
                RedirectStandardError = true,
                CreateNoWindow = true,
                StandardOutputEncoding = Encoding.UTF8,
                StandardErrorEncoding = Encoding.UTF8
            };

            using (Process p = new Process { StartInfo = psi })
            {
                StringBuilder outBuf = new StringBuilder();
                StringBuilder errBuf = new StringBuilder();

                p.Start();

                
                string stdout = p.StandardOutput.ReadToEnd();
                string stderr = p.StandardError.ReadToEnd();

                p.WaitForExit();
                int exit = p.ExitCode;

                return (stdout, stderr, exit);
            }
        }

        
        private static string TryExtractIdFromJson(string stdout)
        {
            try
            {
                JToken token = JToken.Parse(stdout);

                
                var idToken = FindIdToken(token);
                if (idToken != null)
                {
                    if (idToken.Type == JTokenType.String)
                        return idToken.Value<string>();
                    
                    var jv = idToken as JValue;
                    return jv != null ? Convert.ToString(jv.Value, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : idToken.ToString();
                }
            }
            catch
            {
                
            }
            return null;
        }

        private static JToken FindIdToken(JToken token)
        {
            if (token == null)
                return null;

            if (token.Type == JTokenType.Object)
            {
                foreach (var prop in token.Children<JProperty>())
                {
                    if (string.Equals(prop.Name, "id", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                        return prop.Value;

                    var found = FindIdToken(prop.Value);
                    if (found != null)
                        return found;
                }
            }
            else if (token.Type == JTokenType.Array)
            {
                foreach (var child in token.Children())
                {
                    var found = FindIdToken(child);
                    if (found != null)
                        return found;
                }
            }
            else
            {
                
            }

            return null;
        }

        
        private static string TryExtractIdWithRegex(string text)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(text)) return null;

            
            var m = Regex.Match(text, "\"id\"\\s*:\\s*\"(?<id>[^\"]+)\"", RegexOptions.IgnoreCase);
            if (m.Success) return m.Groups["id"].Value;

            
            m = Regex.Match(text, "'id'\\s*:\\s*'(?<id>[^']+)'", RegexOptions.IgnoreCase);
            if (m.Success) return m.Groups["id"].Value;

            
            m = Regex.Match(text, "\"id\"\\s*:\\s*(?<id>\\d+)", RegexOptions.IgnoreCase);
            if (m.Success) return m.Groups["id"].Value;

            
            m = Regex.Match(text, "\\bid\\b\\s*[:=]\\s*\"?(?<id>[0-9a-zA-Z\\-]+)\"?", RegexOptions.IgnoreCase);
            if (m.Success) return m.Groups["id"].Value;

            return null;
        }
    }
}

        public static async Task<string> FindLedgerAccountIdByNameAndAssetIdAsync(string asset_id, string nameContains)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(asset_id) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(nameContains)) return null;

            
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UNLOCK_MT_API_KEY) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UNLOCK_MT_ORGANIZATION_ID))
            {
                try { await SetEnvironment.SetEnv(); } catch {  }
            }

            string orgId = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UNLOCK_MT_ORGANIZATION_ID;
            string apiKey = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UNLOCK_MT_API_KEY;
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(orgId) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(apiKey)) return null;

            string encodedAssetId = WebUtility.UrlEncode(asset_id);
            string encodedName = WebUtility.UrlEncode(nameContains);
            
            string url = $"https:

            using (var client = new HttpClient())
            {
                ServicePointManager.SecurityProtocol = SecurityProtocolType.Tls12;
                var authString = Convert.ToBase64String(Encoding.ASCII.GetBytes(orgId + ":" + apiKey));
                client.DefaultRequestHeaders.Add("authorization", "Basic " + authString);
                client.DefaultRequestHeaders.Add("accept", "application/json");

                try
                {
                    var resp = await client.GetAsync(url);
                    if (!resp.IsSuccessStatusCode)
                        return null;

                    string json = await resp.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                    if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(json)) return null;

                    JToken root;
                    try { root = JToken.Parse(json); } catch { return null; }

                    IEnumerable<JToken> candidates = Enumerable.Empty<JToken>();
                    if (root.Type == JTokenType.Array)
                        candidates = root.Children();
                    else if (root["data"] != null && root["data"].Type == JTokenType.Array)
                        candidates = root["data"].Children();
                    else
                        candidates = new[] { root };

                    
                    var matches = new List<(string id, DateTime created)>();
                    foreach (var acct in candidates)
                    {
                        if (acct == null) continue;
                        string name = acct["name"]?.ToString();

                        if (!name.Contains(nameContains)) continue;

                        var meta = acct["metadata"] as JObject;
                        if (meta == null) continue;
                        string metaAssetId = meta.Properties().FirstOrDefault(p => string.Equals(p.Name, "asset_id", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))?.Value?.ToString();
                        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(metaAssetId) || !string.Equals(metaAssetId.Trim(), asset_id.Trim(), StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                            continue;

                        string id = acct["id"]?.ToString();
                        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(id)) continue;
                        DateTime created = DateTime.MinValue;
                        DateTime.TryParse(acct["created_at"]?.ToString(), out created);
                        matches.Add((id, created));
                    }

                    if (matches.Count == 0) return null;
                    
                    var latest = matches
                        .OrderByDescending(m => m.created) 
                        .ThenByDescending(m => m.id) 
                        .First();
                    return latest.id;
                }
                catch
                {
                    return null;
                }
            }
        }

        
        public static string GetMTIDbyAssetId_InvestmentPayment_Live(string asset_id)
        {
            try { return FindLedgerAccountIdByNameAndAssetIdAsync(asset_id, "Investment Payment").GetAwaiter().GetResult(); } catch { return null; }
        }

        public static async Task<string> FindLedgerAccountCategoryIdByAssetIdAsync(string asset_id)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(asset_id)) return null;

            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UNLOCK_MT_API_KEY) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UNLOCK_MT_ORGANIZATION_ID))
            { try { await SetEnvironment.SetEnv(); } catch {  } }

            string orgId = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UNLOCK_MT_ORGANIZATION_ID;
            string apiKey = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UNLOCK_MT_API_KEY;
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(orgId) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(apiKey)) return null;

            string encodedAssetId = WebUtility.UrlEncode(asset_id);
            
            string url = $"https:

            using (var client = new HttpClient())
            {
                ServicePointManager.SecurityProtocol = SecurityProtocolType.Tls12;
                var authString = Convert.ToBase64String(Encoding.ASCII.GetBytes(orgId + ":" + apiKey));
                client.DefaultRequestHeaders.Add("authorization", "Basic " + authString);
                client.DefaultRequestHeaders.Add("accept", "application/json");

                try
                {
                    var resp = await client.GetAsync(url);
                    if (!resp.IsSuccessStatusCode) return null;

                    string json = await resp.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                    if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(json)) return null;

                    JToken root; try { root = JToken.Parse(json); } catch { return null; }

                    IEnumerable<JToken> candidates = Enumerable.Empty<JToken>();
                    if (root.Type == JTokenType.Array) candidates = root.Children();
                    else if (root["data"] != null && root["data"].Type == JTokenType.Array) candidates = root["data"].Children();
                    else candidates = new[] { root };

                    var matches = new List<(string id, DateTime created)>();
                    foreach (var cat in candidates)
                    {
                        if (cat == null) continue;
                        string name = cat["name"]?.ToString();
                        if (!string.Equals(name?.Trim(), asset_id.Trim(), StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) continue;
                        string id = cat["id"]?.ToString(); if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(id)) continue;
                        DateTime created = DateTime.MinValue; DateTime.TryParse(cat["created_at"]?.ToString(), out created);
                        matches.Add((id, created));
                    }

                    if (matches.Count == 0) return null;
                    return matches.OrderByDescending(m => m.created).ThenByDescending(m => m.id).First().id;
                }
                catch { return null; }
            }
        }

        public static async Task AddLedgerAccountsToCategoryAsync(string server, DataTable assetCategoryTable, string ledgerAccountType)
        {
            if (assetCategoryTable == null || assetCategoryTable.Rows.Count == 0)
                return;

            string typeKey = (ledgerAccountType ?? string.Empty).Trim().ToLowerInvariant();
            if (typeKey != "investmentpayment" && typeKey != "purchaseproceeds")
                throw new ArgumentException("ledgerAccountType must be 'InvestmentPayment' or 'PurchaseProceeds'", nameof(ledgerAccountType));

            string FindColumn(params string[] candidates)
            {
                foreach (var cand in candidates)
                {
                    if (assetCategoryTable.Columns.Contains(cand)) return cand;
                    foreach (DataColumn col in assetCategoryTable.Columns)
                        if (string.Equals(col.ColumnName, cand, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                            return col.ColumnName;
                }
                return null;
            }

            string assetCol = FindColumn("asset_id");
            string categoryCol = FindColumn("ledger_account_category_id", "category_id", "target_category_id");
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(assetCol) || string.IsNullOrEmpty(categoryCol))
                return;

            var seen = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

            foreach (DataRow row in assetCategoryTable.Rows)
            {
                if (row == null) continue;
                string assetId = row[assetCol]?.ToString()?.Trim();
                string targetCategoryId = row[categoryCol]?.ToString()?.Trim();
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(assetId) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(targetCategoryId))
                    continue;

                string dedupKey = assetId + "|" + targetCategoryId + "|" + typeKey;
                if (!seen.Add(dedupKey))
                    continue;

                try
                {
                    string ledgerAccountId = ResolveLedgerAccountIdByType(server, assetId, typeKey);
                    if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ledgerAccountId))
                        continue;

                    string url = $"https:
                    string body = "{}";

                    var client = new ModernTreasuryClient2();
                    await client.SendHttpRequestAsync(url, body, "Put");
                }
                catch
                {
                    
                }
            }
        }
