set mt_loaded = 1
where fa_asset_id = @asset_id


--- FILE: ModernTreasuryLib\Tradeflow.cs ---
using static ModernTreasuryLib.MTApiObjects;

namespace ModernTreasuryLib
{
    public class MTTradeGlobals
    {
        public static string server = CommonInterfaces.Constants.Database.UAM_SQL_SERVER_LABEL;
        
        public static string trade_id = "";
        public static string account_id = "";
        public static string counterparty_id = "";
        public static string trade_date = "";
        public static string settle_date = "";
        public static decimal price = 0;
        public static string asset_id_string = "";
        public static string investor_memo_account_name = "";

        
        public static decimal total_purchase_proceeds = 0;
        public static decimal total_gain_on_sale = 0;
        public static decimal total_haircut_sweep = 0;
        public static decimal total_oface = 0;
    }

    public class ModernTreasury_Trade
    {
        public static async Task CreateTradeMTAssetsAsync(DataTable asset_trade_data, decimal total_proceeds_summary)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();

            if (asset_trade_data == null || asset_trade_data.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No asset sale data provided.");
                return;
            }

            DataRow row = asset_trade_data.Rows[0];
            MTTradeGlobals.trade_id = row["trade_id"].ToString();
            MTTradeGlobals.account_id = row["account_id"].ToString();
            MTTradeGlobals.counterparty_id = row["counterparty_id"].ToString();
            MTTradeGlobals.trade_date = row["trade_date"].ToString();
            MTTradeGlobals.settle_date = row["settle_date"].ToString();
            MTTradeGlobals.price = Convert.ToDecimal(row["price"].ToString());
            MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds = 0;
            MTTradeGlobals.total_gain_on_sale = 0;
            MTTradeGlobals.total_haircut_sweep = 0;
            MTTradeGlobals.total_oface = 0;
            List<string> assetIds = new List<string>();

            
            foreach (DataRow assetRow in asset_trade_data.Rows)
            {
                string asset_id = assetRow["asset_id"].ToString();
                assetIds.Add(asset_id);
                MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds = MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds + Convert.ToDecimal(assetRow["purchase_proceeds"].ToString());
                MTTradeGlobals.total_gain_on_sale = MTTradeGlobals.total_gain_on_sale + Convert.ToDecimal(assetRow["gain_on_sale"].ToString());
                MTTradeGlobals.total_haircut_sweep = MTTradeGlobals.total_haircut_sweep + Convert.ToDecimal(assetRow["haircut"].ToString());
                MTTradeGlobals.total_oface = MTTradeGlobals.total_oface + Convert.ToDecimal(assetRow["oface"].ToString());
            }
            MTTradeGlobals.asset_id_string = string.Join(",", assetIds);

            
            var tradesSubCategoryByAsset = new Dictionary<string, string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
            foreach (var aid in assetIds)
            {
                try
                {
                    string assetCategoryId = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_AssetCategory(aid);
                    if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(assetCategoryId))
                    {
                        Console.WriteLine($"Asset Category missing for asset_id {aid}; skipping Trades subcategory creation.");
                        continue;
                    }
                    
                    string tradesSubCatId = await ModernTreasuryUtils.CreateLedgerSubCategoryAsync("Trades", assetCategoryId, aid);
                    if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tradesSubCatId))
                        tradesSubCategoryByAsset[aid] = tradesSubCatId;
                }
                catch (Exception ex)
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Failed to create Trades subcategory for asset_id {aid}: {ex.Message}");
                }
            }

            
            try
            {
                
                DataTable memoCats = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMemoAccountsByAccountID(MTTradeGlobals.server, MTTradeGlobals.account_id, true);
                string ipCategoryId = null;
                if (memoCats != null && memoCats.Rows.Count > 0)
                {
                    
                    foreach (DataRow r in memoCats.Rows)
                    {
                        var matchType = r.Table.Columns.Contains("match_type") ? r["match_type"]?.ToString() : null;
                        var mtKey = r.Table.Columns.Contains("mt_key") ? r["mt_key"]?.ToString() : null;
                        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(mtKey))
                        {
                            ipCategoryId = mtKey;
                            if (string.Equals(matchType, "IP Category", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) break;
                        }
                    }
                }

                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(ipCategoryId))
                {
                    DataTable map = new DataTable();
                    map.Columns.Add("asset_id", typeof(string));
                    map.Columns.Add("target_category_id", typeof(string));
                    foreach (var aid in assetIds)
                        map.Rows.Add(aid, ipCategoryId);

                    await ModernTreasuryUtils.AddInvestmentPaymentToCategoryAsync(MTTradeGlobals.server, map);
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"IP categorization step skipped: {ex.Message}");
            }

            
            if (MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds != total_proceeds_summary)
                throw new InvalidOperationException($"Total purchase proceeds ({MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds}) do not match the provided summary ({total_proceeds_summary}).");

            
            await CreateGainOnSaleLedgerAccountAsync(MTTradeGlobals.server, asset_trade_data, tradesSubCategoryByAsset);
            await CreatePurchaseProceedsLedgerAccountAsync(MTTradeGlobals.server, asset_trade_data, tradesSubCategoryByAsset);
            
            await CreatePurchaseProceedsExpectedPaymentsAsync(MTTradeGlobals.server, asset_trade_data);
            
            await CreateHaircutSweepExpectedPaymentAsync(MTTradeGlobals.server, asset_trade_data);
            
            await CreateGainOnSaleSweepExpectedPaymentAsync(MTTradeGlobals.server, asset_trade_data);
            
            await CreateWarehouseLineSweepExpectedPaymentAsync(MTTradeGlobals.server, asset_trade_data);
            
            await CreateMSRAssetLedgerAccountAsync(MTTradeGlobals.server, asset_trade_data, tradesSubCategoryByAsset);
        }

        private static async Task<string> CreateGainOnSaleLedgerAccountAsync(string server, DataTable assets_trade_data, Dictionary<string,string> tradesSubCategoryByAsset)
        {
            string targetLedger = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.unlock_ledger_id;
            string result = null;

            foreach (DataRow row in assets_trade_data.Rows)
            {
                string asset_id = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                string accountLabel = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_label + asset_id + Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.gain_on_sale_label;
                string ledgerAccountName = asset_id + Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.gain_on_sale_label;
                string pipelineLabel = row.Table.Columns.Contains("pipeline_label") ? row["pipeline_label"].ToString() : null;

                if (!tradesSubCategoryByAsset.TryGetValue(asset_id, out string tradesSubCategoryId) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tradesSubCategoryId))
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Trades subcategory missing for asset_id: {asset_id}");
                    continue;
                }

                List<string> categoryIds = new List<string> { tradesSubCategoryId };
                if (row.Table.Columns.Contains("investor_mt_account_id") && row["investor_mt_account_id"] != DBNull.Value)
                {
                    string investorMemoCategoryId = row["investor_mt_account_id"].ToString();
                    if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(investorMemoCategoryId)) categoryIds.Add(investorMemoCategoryId);
                }

                
                var metadata = new JObject
                {
                    ["asset_id"] = asset_id,
                };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(MTTradeGlobals.trade_id)) metadata["trade_id"] = MTTradeGlobals.trade_id;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(MTTradeGlobals.account_id)) metadata["account_id"] = MTTradeGlobals.account_id;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(MTTradeGlobals.trade_date)) metadata["trade_date"] = MTTradeGlobals.trade_date;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(MTTradeGlobals.settle_date)) metadata["settle_date"] = MTTradeGlobals.settle_date;
                if (MTTradeGlobals.price > 0m) metadata["price"] = MTTradeGlobals.price.ToString();
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name)) metadata["investor_memo_account_name"] = MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name;
                if (row.Table.Columns.Contains("oface") && row["oface"] != DBNull.Value)
                    metadata["investment_payment"] = Convert.ToDecimal(row["oface"]).ToString();
                metadata["initiated_by"] = "Tradeflow.cs";
                metadata["modern_treasury_view"] = "trade_flow";

                LedgerAccount ledgerAccount = new LedgerAccount
                {
                    name = ledgerAccountName,
                    currency = "USD",
                    normal_balance = "debit",
                    ledger_account_category_ids = categoryIds,
                    ledger_id = targetLedger,
                    description = accountLabel
                };
                JObject ledgerAccountJo = JObject.FromObject(ledgerAccount);
                if (metadata.HasValues) ledgerAccountJo["metadata"] = metadata;
                string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ledgerAccountJo);
                result = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:

                bool insert_gain_on_sale_done = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, asset_id, "create_ledger_account_gain_on_sale", result, "ledger_account", pipelineLabel, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.gain_on_sale_label, asset_id, 1, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_url_prefix + result, "Tradeflow.cs", null, 0m, null);

                if (!insert_gain_on_sale_done)
                    Console.WriteLine($"Failed to insert MT mapping for asset_id: {asset_id} Gain On Sale");

            }
            return result;
        }

        
        private static async Task<string> CreatePurchaseProceedsLedgerAccountAsync(string server, DataTable assets_trade_data, Dictionary<string,string> tradesSubCategoryByAsset)
        {
            string targetLedger = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.unlock_ledger_id;
            string lastId = null;

            
            string trustCategoryId = null;
            try
            {
                DataTable memoCats = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMemoAccountsByAccountID(server, MTTradeGlobals.account_id);
                if (memoCats != null && memoCats.Rows.Count > 0)
                {
                    foreach (DataRow r in memoCats.Rows)
                    {
                        string matchType = r.Table.Columns.Contains("match_type") ? r["match_type"]?.ToString() : null;
                        string mtKey = r.Table.Columns.Contains("mt_key") ? r["mt_key"]?.ToString() : null;
                        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(mtKey) && string.Equals(matchType, "Category", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                        {
                            trustCategoryId = mtKey; break;
                        }
                    }
                    if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(trustCategoryId))
                    {
                        var first = memoCats.Rows[0];
                        if (first != null && first.Table.Columns.Contains("mt_key")) trustCategoryId = first["mt_key"].ToString();
                    }
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Unable to resolve Trust/Securitization category: {ex.Message}");
            }

            foreach (DataRow row in assets_trade_data.Rows)
            {
                string asset_id = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                string pipelineLabel = row.Table.Columns.Contains("pipeline_label") ? row["pipeline_label"].ToString() : null;
                string accountLabel = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_label + asset_id + Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.purchase_proceeds_label;
                string ledgerAccountName = asset_id + Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.purchase_proceeds_label;

                if (!tradesSubCategoryByAsset.TryGetValue(asset_id, out string tradesSubCategoryId) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tradesSubCategoryId))
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Trades subcategory missing for asset_id: {asset_id}");
                    continue;
                }

                var categoryIds = new List<string> { tradesSubCategoryId };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(trustCategoryId)) categoryIds.Add(trustCategoryId);

                
                var metadata = new JObject
                {
                    ["asset_id"] = asset_id,
                };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(MTTradeGlobals.trade_id)) metadata["trade_id"] = MTTradeGlobals.trade_id;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(MTTradeGlobals.account_id)) metadata["account_id"] = MTTradeGlobals.account_id;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(MTTradeGlobals.trade_date)) metadata["trade_date"] = MTTradeGlobals.trade_date;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(MTTradeGlobals.settle_date)) metadata["settle_date"] = MTTradeGlobals.settle_date;
                if (MTTradeGlobals.price > 0m) metadata["price"] = MTTradeGlobals.price.ToString();
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name)) metadata["investor_memo_account_name"] = MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name;
                if (row.Table.Columns.Contains("oface") && row["oface"] != DBNull.Value)
                    metadata["investment_payment"] = Convert.ToDecimal(row["oface"]).ToString();
                metadata["initiated_by"] = "Tradeflow.cs";
                metadata["modern_treasury_view"] = "trade_flow";

                var ledgerAccount = new JObject
                {
                    ["name"] = ledgerAccountName,
                    ["currency"] = "USD",
                    ["normal_balance"] = "debit",
                    ["ledger_account_category_ids"] = JArray.FromObject(categoryIds),
                    ["ledger_id"] = targetLedger,
                    ["description"] = accountLabel
                };
                if (metadata.HasValues) ledgerAccount["metadata"] = metadata;
                string body = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ledgerAccount);
                string id = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
                lastId = id;

                
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, asset_id, "create_ledger_account_purchase_proceeds", id, "ledger_account", pipelineLabel, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.purchase_proceeds_label, asset_id, 1, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_url_prefix + id, "Tradeflow.cs", null, 0m, null);
            }

            return lastId;
        }

        private static async Task<string> CreatePurchaseProceedsExpectedPaymentsAsync(string server, DataTable assets_trade_data)
        {
            string result = null;
            string TCB_internal_account_id = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_uf2_collections_account; 
            string receiving_ledger_account_UF2_coll = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UF2_collections_ledger_account_id;

            
            DataTable memoAccounts = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMemoAccountsByAccountID(server, MTTradeGlobals.account_id);
            MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name = null;
            if (memoAccounts != null && memoAccounts.Rows.Count > 0)
            {
                DataRow memoRow = memoAccounts.Rows[0];
                MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name = memoRow["mt_account_name"]?.ToString();
            }

            int total_purchase_proceeds_int = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds, 2) * 100);
            string epDescription = "Trade # " + MTTradeGlobals.trade_id + " Purchase Proceeds Expected Payment of " + Math.Round(MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds, 2).ToString();

            ExpectedPayment expectedPayment = new ExpectedPayment
            {
                ledger_transaction = new LedgerTransactionEP
                {
                    description = epDescription,
                    ledger_entries = new List<LedgerEntryEP>
                    { }
                },
                reconciliation_rule_variables = new List<ReconciliationRuleVariables>
                {
                    new ReconciliationRuleVariables
                    {
                        internal_account_id = TCB_internal_account_id,
                        direction = "credit",
                        amount_lower_bound = total_purchase_proceeds_int,
                        amount_upper_bound = total_purchase_proceeds_int,
                        custom_identifiers = new Dictionary<string, string>
                        {
                            { "asset_ids", MTTradeGlobals.asset_id_string },
                            { "trade_id", MTTradeGlobals.trade_id },
                            { "total_purchase_proceeds", MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds.ToString() },
                            { "account_name", MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name },
                            { "trade_date", MTTradeGlobals.trade_date },
                            { "settle_date", MTTradeGlobals.settle_date },
                        }
                    }
                },
                metadata = new Dictionary<string, string>
                {
                    { "transaction_type", "purchase_proceeds" },
                    { "initiated_by", "Tradeflow.cs" },
                    { "trade_id", MTTradeGlobals.trade_id },
                    { "account_name", MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name },
                    { "asset_ids", MTTradeGlobals.asset_id_string },
                    { "total_investment_payment", MTTradeGlobals.total_oface.ToString() },
                    { "total_gain_on_sale", MTTradeGlobals.total_gain_on_sale.ToString() },
                    { "total_purchase_proceeds", MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds.ToString() },
                    { "modern_treasury_view", "trade_flow" },
                    { "trade_date", MTTradeGlobals.trade_date },
                    { "settle_date", MTTradeGlobals.settle_date },
                }
            };

            JObject expectedPaymentJo = JObject.FromObject(expectedPayment);
            expectedPaymentJo["description"] = epDescription;

            
            foreach (DataRow row in assets_trade_data.Rows)
            {
                string asset_id = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                decimal purchase_proceeds = Convert.ToDecimal(row["purchase_proceeds"].ToString());
                int purchase_proceeds_int = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(purchase_proceeds, 2) * 100);
                decimal oface = Convert.ToDecimal(row["oface"].ToString());
                int oface_int = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(oface, 2) * 100);
                decimal gain_on_sale = Convert.ToDecimal(row["gain_on_sale"].ToString());
                int gain_on_sale_int = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(gain_on_sale, 2) * 100);
                string investment_payment_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_InvestmentPayment_Live(asset_id);
                string gain_on_sale_mtid = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_GainOnSale_Live(asset_id);

                
                string pp_ledger_id = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMTIDbyAssetId_PurchaseProceeds_Live(asset_id);
                string debit_ledger_id = !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(pp_ledger_id) ? pp_ledger_id : receiving_ledger_account_UF2_coll;

                JObject metadata = new JObject
                {
                    ["asset_id"] = asset_id,
                    ["trade_id"] = MTTradeGlobals.trade_id,
                    ["investment_payment"] = oface.ToString(),
                    ["gain_on_sale"] = gain_on_sale.ToString(),
                    ["purchase_proceeds"] = purchase_proceeds.ToString(),
                    ["account_name"] = MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name,
                    ["trade_date"] = MTTradeGlobals.trade_date,
                    ["settle_date"] = MTTradeGlobals.settle_date,
                    ["initiated_by"] = "Tradeflow.cs",
                    ["modern_treasury_view"] = "trade_flow"
                };

                JObject ledgerEntryDebit = new JObject
                {
                    ["amount"] = purchase_proceeds_int,
                    ["direction"] = "debit",
                    ["ledger_account_id"] = debit_ledger_id,
                    ["metadata"] = metadata
                };
                ((JArray)expectedPaymentJo["ledger_transaction"]["ledger_entries"])?.Add(ledgerEntryDebit);

                JObject ledgerEntryCredit = new JObject
                {
                    ["amount"] = oface_int,
                    ["direction"] = "credit",
                    ["ledger_account_id"] = investment_payment_mtid,
                    ["metadata"] = metadata
                };
                ((JArray)expectedPaymentJo["ledger_transaction"]["ledger_entries"])?.Add(ledgerEntryCredit);

                JObject ledgerEntryCreditGOS = new JObject
                {
                    ["amount"] = gain_on_sale_int,
                    ["direction"] = "credit",
                    ["ledger_account_id"] = gain_on_sale_mtid,
                    ["metadata"] = metadata
                };
                ((JArray)expectedPaymentJo["ledger_transaction"]["ledger_entries"])?.Add(ledgerEntryCreditGOS);
            }

            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(expectedPaymentJo);
            Console.WriteLine(requestBody);
            result = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:

            ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, null, "create_purchase_proceeds_expected_payment", result, "expected_payment", null, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_label, null, MTTradeGlobals.total_purchase_proceeds, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + result, "Tradeflow.cs", null, 0m, null);

            return result;
        }

        private static async Task<string> CreateHaircutSweepExpectedPaymentAsync(string server, DataTable assets_trade_data)
        {
            string result = null;
            string receivingLedgerAccountUPS = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UPS_Cash_ledger_account_id;
            string sourceLedgerAccountUF2Coll = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.UF2_collections_ledger_account_id;
            string receivingAccountUPS = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.TCB_recon_ups_account;
            int haircutIntAmount = Convert.ToInt32(Math.Round(MTTradeGlobals.total_haircut_sweep, 2) * 100);

            string epDescription = "Trade # " + MTTradeGlobals.trade_id + " Haircut Sweep Expected Payment of " + Math.Round(MTTradeGlobals.total_haircut_sweep, 2).ToString();

            ExpectedPayment expectedPayment = new ExpectedPayment
            {
                ledger_transaction = new LedgerTransactionEP
                {
                    description = epDescription,
                    ledger_entries = new List<LedgerEntryEP>
                    {
                        new LedgerEntryEP
                        {
                            amount = haircutIntAmount,
                            direction = "debit",
                            ledger_account_id = receivingLedgerAccountUPS
                        },
                        new LedgerEntryEP
                        {
                            amount = haircutIntAmount,
                            direction = "credit",
                            ledger_account_id = sourceLedgerAccountUF2Coll
                        }
                    }
                },
                reconciliation_rule_variables = new List<ReconciliationRuleVariables>
                {
                    new ReconciliationRuleVariables
                    {
                        internal_account_id = receivingAccountUPS,
                        direction = "credit",
                        amount_lower_bound = haircutIntAmount,
                        amount_upper_bound = haircutIntAmount
                    }
                },
                metadata = new Dictionary<string, string>()
                {
                    { "transaction_type", "haircut_sweep" },
                    { "initiated_by", "Tradeflow.cs" },
                    { "trade_id", MTTradeGlobals.trade_id },
                    { "account_name", MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name },
                    { "asset_ids", MTTradeGlobals.asset_id_string },
                    { "total_haircut_sweep", MTTradeGlobals.total_haircut_sweep.ToString() },
                    { "modern_treasury_view", "trade_flow" },
                    { "trade_date", MTTradeGlobals.trade_date },
                    { "settle_date", MTTradeGlobals.settle_date },
                }
            };

            JObject expectedPaymentJo = JObject.FromObject(expectedPayment);
            expectedPaymentJo["description"] = epDescription;

            string requestBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(expectedPaymentJo);
            result = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
            ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, null, "create_haircut_sweep_expected_payment", result, "expected_payment", null, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_label, null, MTTradeGlobals.total_haircut_sweep, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.expected_payment_url_prefix + result, "Tradeflow.cs", null, 0m, null);

            return result;
        }

        private static async Task CreateMSRAssetLedgerAccountAsync(string server, DataTable assets_trade_data, Dictionary<string,string> tradesSubCategoryByAsset)
        {
            string targetLedger = Constants.ModernTreasuryKeys.unlock_ledger_id;

            foreach (DataRow row in assets_trade_data.Rows)
            {
                string asset_id = row["asset_id"].ToString();
                if (!tradesSubCategoryByAsset.TryGetValue(asset_id, out string tradesSubCategoryId) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tradesSubCategoryId))
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Skipping MSR Asset creation. Missing Trades subcategory for asset_id: {asset_id}");
                    continue;
                }

                string msrAccountLabel = Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_label + asset_id + Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.msr_asset_label;
                string msrLedgerAccountName = asset_id + Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.msr_asset_label;
                List<string> categoryIds = new List<string> { tradesSubCategoryId };

                
                var msrAccountMetadata = new JObject
                {
                    ["asset_id"] = asset_id,
                    ["initiated_by"] = "Tradeflow.cs",
                    ["modern_treasury_view"] = "trade_flow",
                    ["msr_asset_percent"] = "3.25",
                };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name)) msrAccountMetadata["investor_memo_account_name"] = MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name;
                if (row.Table.Columns.Contains("oface") && row["oface"] != DBNull.Value)
                {
                    decimal oface = Convert.ToDecimal(row["oface"]);
                    msrAccountMetadata["investment_payment"] = oface.ToString();
                    msrAccountMetadata["msr_asset_amount"] = Math.Round(oface * 0.0325m, 2).ToString(); 
                }

                LedgerAccount msrLedgerAccount = new LedgerAccount { name = msrLedgerAccountName, currency = "USD", normal_balance = "debit", ledger_account_category_ids = categoryIds, ledger_id = targetLedger, description = msrAccountLabel };
                JObject msrLedgerAccountJo = JObject.FromObject(msrLedgerAccount);
                if (msrAccountMetadata.HasValues) msrLedgerAccountJo["metadata"] = msrAccountMetadata;
                string createAccountBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(msrLedgerAccountJo);
                string msrAccountId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, asset_id, "create_ledger_account_msr_asset", msrAccountId, "ledger_account", null, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.msr_asset_label, asset_id, 1, Constants.ModernTreasuryLabels.ledger_account_url_prefix + msrAccountId, "Tradeflow.cs", null, 0m, null);

                
                DataTable memoAccounts = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetContraMemoAccounts(server);
                string investor_contra_memo_account_id = null;
                if (memoAccounts != null && memoAccounts.Rows.Count > 0)
                {
                    DataRow memoRow = memoAccounts.Rows[0];
                    if (memoRow != null && memoRow.Table.Columns.Contains("mt_key")) investor_contra_memo_account_id = memoRow["mt_key"].ToString();
                }

                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(investor_contra_memo_account_id))
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"Skipping ledger transaction. Missing investor_contra_memo_account_id for asset_id: {asset_id}");
                    continue;
                }

                
                decimal baseInvestmentPayment = 0m;
                if (row.Table.Columns.Contains("investment_payment") && row["investment_payment"] != DBNull.Value)
                    baseInvestmentPayment = Convert.ToDecimal(row["investment_payment"]);
                else if (row.Table.Columns.Contains("oface") && row["oface"] != DBNull.Value)
                    baseInvestmentPayment = Convert.ToDecimal(row["oface"]);
                else
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"No investment payment or oface column value for asset_id: {asset_id}");
                    continue;
                }

                decimal msrAssetAmount = Math.Round(baseInvestmentPayment * 0.0325m, 2); 
                int msrAssetAmountInt = Convert.ToInt32(msrAssetAmount * 100);

                
                var msrDebitMetadata = new JObject
                {
                    ["asset_id"] = asset_id,
                    ["investment_payment"] = baseInvestmentPayment.ToString(),
                    ["msr_asset_percent"] = "3.25",
                    ["msr_asset_amount"] = msrAssetAmount.ToString(),
                    ["initiated_by"] = "Tradeflow.cs",
                    ["modern_treasury_view"] = "trade_flow"
                };
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name)) msrDebitMetadata["investor_memo_account_name"] = MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name;

                var ledgerTransaction = new JObject
                {
                    ["description"] = $"MSR Asset Creation (3.25%) for Asset {asset_id}",
                    ["ledger_entries"] = new JArray
                    {
                        new JObject
                        {
                            ["amount"] = msrAssetAmountInt,
                            ["direction"] = "debit",
                            ["ledger_account_id"] = msrAccountId,
                            ["metadata"] = msrDebitMetadata
                        },
                        new JObject
                        {
                            ["amount"] = msrAssetAmountInt,
                            ["direction"] = "credit",
                            ["ledger_account_id"] = investor_contra_memo_account_id
                        }
                    }
                };

                string ledgerTransactionBody = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ledgerTransaction);
                string ledgerTransactionId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:

                string ltUrl = "https:
                ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(server, asset_id, "create_msr_asset_ledger_transaction", ledgerTransactionId, "ledger_transaction", null, "_MSRAsset", asset_id, msrAssetAmount, ltUrl, "Tradeflow.cs", null, 0m, null);
            }
        }

        public static async Task CreateSecuritizationTradeMTAssets(DataTable asset_trade_data, decimal transfer_amount)
        {
            SetEnvironment.SetEnv();

            if (asset_trade_data == null || asset_trade_data.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("No asset trade data provided for securitization trade.");
                return;
            }

            DataRow first = asset_trade_data.Rows[0];
            MTTradeGlobals.trade_id = first.Table.Columns.Contains("trade_id") ? first["trade_id"].ToString() : null;
            MTTradeGlobals.account_id = first.Table.Columns.Contains("account_id") ? first["account_id"].ToString() : null;
            MTTradeGlobals.counterparty_id = first.Table.Columns.Contains("counterparty_id") ? first["counterparty_id"].ToString() : null;
            MTTradeGlobals.trade_date = first.Table.Columns.Contains("trade_date") ? first["trade_date"].ToString() : null;
            MTTradeGlobals.settle_date = first.Table.Columns.Contains("settle_date") ? first["settle_date"].ToString() : null;

            List<string> assetIds = new List<string>();
            foreach (DataRow r in asset_trade_data.Rows)
            {
                if (r.Table.Columns.Contains("asset_id") && r["asset_id"] != DBNull.Value)
                    assetIds.Add(r["asset_id"].ToString());
            }
            MTTradeGlobals.asset_id_string = string.Join(",", assetIds);

            
            DataTable investorMemoAccounts = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMemoAccountsByAccountID(MTTradeGlobals.server, MTTradeGlobals.account_id);
            if (investorMemoAccounts == null || investorMemoAccounts.Rows.Count == 0)
                throw new InvalidOperationException("No memo accounts found for investor account_id. Securitization trade aborted.");
            DataRow investorMemoRow = investorMemoAccounts.Rows[0];
            string investor_memo_account_id = investorMemoRow.Table.Columns.Contains("investor_memo_account_id") ? investorMemoRow["investor_memo_account_id"].ToString() : null;
            MTTradeGlobals.investor_memo_account_name = investorMemoRow.Table.Columns.Contains("investor_memo_account_name") ? investorMemoRow["investor_memo_account_name"].ToString() : null;
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(investor_memo_account_id))
                throw new InvalidOperationException("Investor memo account id missing. Securitization trade aborted.");

            
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(MTTradeGlobals.counterparty_id))
                throw new InvalidOperationException("counterparty_id is missing in trade data.");
            DataTable counterpartyMemoAccounts = ModernTreasuryUtils.GetMemoAccountsByAccountID(MTTradeGlobals.server, MTTradeGlobals.counterparty_id);
            if (counterpartyMemoAccounts == null || counterpartyMemoAccounts.Rows.Count == 0)
                throw new InvalidOperationException("No memo accounts found for counterparty_id. Securitization trade aborted.");
            DataRow counterpartyMemoRow = counterpartyMemoAccounts.Rows[0];
            string counterparty_memo_account_id = counterpartyMemoRow.Table.Columns.Contains("investor_memo_account_id") ? counterpartyMemoRow["investor_memo_account_id"].ToString() : null; 
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(counterparty_memo_account_id))
                throw new InvalidOperationException("Counterparty memo account id missing. Securitization trade aborted.");

            decimal roundedAmount = Math.Round(transfer_amount, 2);
            int amountInt = Convert.ToInt32(roundedAmount * 100);

            
            var ledgerTransaction = new JObject
            {
                ["description"] = $"Securitization Trade Transfer {roundedAmount} for Trade {MTTradeGlobals.trade_id}",
                ["ledger_entries"] = new JArray
                {
                    new JObject 
                    {
                        ["amount"] = amountInt,
                        ["direction"] = "debit",
                        ["ledger_account_id"] = counterparty_memo_account_id
                    },
                    new JObject 
                    {
                        ["amount"] = amountInt,
                        ["direction"] = "credit",
                        ["ledger_account_id"] = investor_memo_account_id
                    }
                }
            };

            string body = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(ledgerTransaction);
            string ledgerTransactionId = await MTRequestor.SendHttpRequestAsync("https:
            string ltUrl = "https:

            bool mapInserted = ModernTreasuryUtils.InsertModernTreasuryMap(MTTradeGlobals.server, null, "create_securitization_trade_ledger_transaction", ledgerTransactionId, "ledger_transaction", null, "_SecuritizationTrade", MTTradeGlobals.asset_id_string, roundedAmount, ltUrl, "Tradeflow.cs", null, 0m, null);
            if (!mapInserted)
                Console.WriteLine("Failed to insert MT mapping for securitization trade ledger transaction.");
        }
    }
}

        public DBOutputHelper ParseAndLoad()
        {
            DBOutputHelper loaded_lines = null;
            if (_input.Contains("INCANLDY"))
                loaded_lines = LoadIncomeDaily();
            if (_input.Contains("OPENBOND"))
                loaded_lines = LoadOpenBond();
            return loaded_lines;
        }

        public Nullable<DateTime> _asOf;
        public Nullable<DateTime> asOf { get { return _asOf; } }

        public DBOutputHelper LoadIncomeDaily()
        {
            
            _asOf = null;
            int count = 0;
            string[] lines = File.ReadAllLines(_input);
            ETA eta = new ETA(lines.Length, Console.WriteLine);
            int loaded = 0;
            string security_description = null;
            string profit_center = null;
            foreach (string line in lines)
            {
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
                if (count == 0)
                {
                    _asOf = System.Convert.ToDateTime(line.Split(' ')[6].Trim());
                    ClearLNRebates(_server, asOf.Value);
                }

                if(line.Contains("ROBERT W. BAIRD CO.") && !line.Contains("Consolidated"))
                {
                    profit_center = line.Split('-')[1];
                    if (String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(profit_center))
                        profit_center = "-";
                }

                if (line.Split(' ').Length > 0)
                {
                    bool is_cusip = UtilsLib.Validate.IsCusip(line.Split(' ')[0]);

                    if (is_cusip)
                    {
                        string cusip = line.Split(' ')[0];
                        security_description = PHelper.ShorterHelperNew(line, 11, 32);
                        
                        


                        Nullable<double> borrow_rebate = null;
                        PHelper.ParseHelperRobustNew(line, "%", 53, 54, 32, 44, ref borrow_rebate, null);

                        Nullable<double> borrow_rate = null;
                        PHelper.ParseHelperRobustNew(line, "%", 53, 54, 44, 53, ref borrow_rate, null);
                        {
                            borrow_rate = borrow_rate / 100.0;
                            if(null != borrow_rebate && borrow_rebate <0)
                            {
                                if (null != borrow_rate)
                                    borrow_rate = -borrow_rate.Value;
                            }
                        }


                        Nullable<double> loan_cost = null;
                        PHelper.ParseHelperRobustNew(line, "%", 75, 76, 55, 66, ref loan_cost, null);
                        

                        Nullable<double> loan_rate = null;
                        PHelper.ParseHelperRobustNew(line, "%", 75, 76, 66, 75, ref loan_rate, null);
                        {
                            loan_rate = loan_rate / 100.0;

                            if (null != loan_cost && loan_cost < 0)
                            {
                                if (null != loan_rate)
                                    loan_rate = -loan_rate.Value;
                            }
                        }

                        Nullable<double> total_income = null;
                        PHelper.ParseHelperRobustNew(line, ".", 129, 130, 121, 133, ref total_income, null);

                        WriteSingleRebate(_server, asOf.Value, cusip, security_description, borrow_rate, borrow_rebate, loan_rate, loan_cost, total_income, profit_center);
                        
                        loaded++;
                    }
                }
                count++;
                
            }
            DBOutputHelper oh = new DBOutputHelper();
            oh.rows = loaded;
            return oh;
        }

        public DBOutputHelper LoadOpenBond()
        {
            
            Nullable<DateTime> asOf = null;
            int count = 0;
            string[] lines = File.ReadAllLines(_input);
            ETA eta = new ETA(lines.Length, Console.WriteLine);
            int loaded = 0;
            string cusip = null;
            string security_description = null;
            Nullable<double> market_price = null;
            foreach (string line in lines)
            {
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
                if (count == 0)
                {
                    asOf = System.Convert.ToDateTime(line.Split(' ')[41].Trim());
                    ClearLNTrades(_server, asOf.Value);
                }
                if (line.Split(' ').Length > 0)
                {
                    
                    if (line.Length > 3 && line.Substring(0, 3) == "***")
                    {
                        cusip = line.Split(' ')[39];
                        security_description = PHelper.ShorterHelperNew(line, 52, 83);
                        PHelper.ParseHelperRobustNew(line, ".", 114, 115, 107, 119, ref market_price, null);
                    }

                    
                    if ((line.Contains("@") || line.Contains("Mrked")) && !line.Contains("Now"))
                    {

                        if (line.Length > 19 && (line.Substring(17, 1) == "D" || line.Substring(17, 1) == "I" || line.Substring(17, 1) == "U"))
                            continue;
                        
                        string counterparty = PHelper.ShorterHelperNew(line, 1, 20);
                        

                        Nullable<double> contract_id = null;
                        PHelper.ParseHelperRobustNew(line, ".", 42, 43, 20, 29, ref contract_id, null);

                        DateTime trade_date = System.Convert.ToDateTime(PHelper.ShorterHelperNew(line, 30, 38));

                        Nullable<double> borrow_rate = null;
                        PHelper.ParseHelperRobustNew(line, ".", 42, 43, 38, 48, ref borrow_rate, null);
                        borrow_rate = borrow_rate / 100;

                        Nullable<double> borrow_quantity = null;
                        PHelper.ParseHelperRobustNew(line, ".", 42, 43, 48, 60, ref borrow_quantity, null);

                        Nullable<double> borrow_price = null;
                        
                        PHelper.ParseHelperRobustNew(line, ".", 42, 43, 62, 72, ref borrow_price, "*");

                        Nullable<double> borrow_amount = null;
                        PHelper.ParseHelperRobustNew(line, ".", 42, 43, 77, 94, ref borrow_amount, null);

                        WriteSingleTrade(_server, asOf.Value, cusip, counterparty, security_description, trade_date, borrow_rate, borrow_price, borrow_quantity, borrow_amount, market_price);
                        
                        loaded++;
                    }
                }
                count++;
                
            }

            return new DBOutputHelper {rows = loaded};
        }

        public void SetETAFormat(string format)
        {
            eta_string_override = format;
        }
        public void WriteExportFile()
        {

        }


        public void WriteSingleTrade(string server, DateTime asOf, string cusip, string counterparty, string security_description, DateTime trade_date, Nullable<double> borrow_rate, Nullable<double> borrow_price, Nullable<double> borrow_quantity, Nullable<double> borrow_amount, Nullable<double> market_price)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.InsertUpdateLNTrade @asOf=@asOf, @cusip=@cusip, @counterparty=@counterparty, @trade_date=@trade_date, @security_description=@security_description, @borrow_quantity=@borrow_quantity, @borrow_rate=@borrow_rate, @borrow_amount=@borrow_amount, @borrow_price=@borrow_price, @market_price=@market_price";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.AddParameter("@cusip", cusip);
            q.AddParameter("@counterparty", counterparty);
            q.AddParameter("@security_description", security_description);
            q.AddParameter("@trade_date", trade_date);
            q.AddParameter("@borrow_rate", borrow_rate);
            q.AddParameter("@borrow_price", borrow_price);
            q.AddParameter("@borrow_quantity", borrow_quantity);
            q.AddParameter("@borrow_amount", borrow_amount);
            q.AddParameter("@market_price", market_price);
            q.Execute();
        }
            public void WriteSingleRebate(string server, DateTime asOf, string cusip, string security_description, Nullable<double> borrow_rate, Nullable<double> borrow_rebate, Nullable<double> loan_rate, Nullable<double> loan_cost, Nullable<double> total_income,string profit_center)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.InsertUpdateLNRebates @asOf=@asOf, @cusip=@cusip, @security_description=@security_description, @borrow_rate=@borrow_rate, @borrow_rebate=@borrow_rebate, @loan_rate=@loan_rate, @loan_cost=@loan_cost, @total_income=@total_income, @profit_center=@profit_center";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.AddParameter("@cusip", cusip);
            q.AddParameter("@security_description", security_description);
            q.AddParameter("@borrow_rate", borrow_rate);
            q.AddParameter("@borrow_rebate", borrow_rebate);
            q.AddParameter("@loan_rate", loan_rate);
            q.AddParameter("@loan_cost", loan_cost);
            q.AddParameter("@total_income", total_income);
            q.AddParameter("@profit_center", profit_center);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public void ClearLNRebates(string server, DateTime asOf)
        {
            string sql = "delete from LNRebates where asOf = @asOf";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.Execute();
        }
        public void ClearLNTrades(string server, DateTime asOf)
        {
            string sql = "delete from LNTrades where asOf = @asOf";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.Execute();
        }

    }
